Page 23

電影專刊

美國某電影雜誌所發的嚴重警告

— 開羅

各種電影競賽所造成之失望

無知無識靑年女子居其多數

美國電影界製片家，無時無刻不在尋求新的人才。他們在普天下搜索着，在上中下三等人物中尋覓着。他們用盡了心血與金錢，發起了無數種的競賽，以爲拔取眞材的途徑。這是不是美國女界的好消息？有人說是的，但是美國的MotionPicture，在正月號中已經發出了嚴重的警告。記者讀了裏面的内容，亦有些驚心動魄，現在且將那雜誌發出警告的原因，以及各種競賽的實在情形，約略叙述一下。

總而言之，好萊塢的魔力太大了，使全國女子都受了它的誘惑，脫離了家庭，抛棄丈夫子女，釀成種種慘案。大家都存了做電影明星的希望，等到事實上辦不到，就由失望而墮落，而自殺。而這種轟動全國的競賽，尤其是製造失望悲慘的開端。你要是一時勝利了，至終或許還是要失敗；倘使你失敗了，那你就永久失敗了，並且喪失了一切的希望，金錢與家庭。因此，稍爲曉得些電影事業的内容的，不得不向普天下的友子，發出一種警告：「最好是不要踏入是非之塲，走上毁滅之路；不然的話，應當前瞻後顧，不要一刻忘記出路的所在，以便隨時作急流勇退之計」。

據好來塢最近的統討，以往十二個月之中，各電影公司所發起的各種競賽，一共多至一百九十二次。競賽勝利者有二千一百人，曾受聘到好萊塢；而相近勝利，自已出貲去到好萊塢的，總有好幾倍。美國女子加入這許多競賽的，人數在一千一百萬以上，而全世界的人數，總有二千八百萬之譜。有一次競賽，竟吸引了四百六十四萬個女子。其中以中等城市報名的最多。如納希維爾一個地方，報名的竟逹二萬三千四百人之多。所以這様看來，美國經過了這許多次電影競賽之後，一定有幾千萬失望的與賽者！

各種競賽的名稱，眞是五花八門，可以提得起名稱的，至少有二三十種。但是結果，往往尋不到一個需要的人才，祗可以將幾個出類拔萃的美貌女子，請到好萊塢去遊歷一趟，然後再資遣回籍。在這一方面，恐怕上海人還没有忘記去年外國人亦曾在中國發起個一次競賽。結果如何，恐怕到現在還没有一個交代哩。不過當時中國女子參加的並不多，失望的當然也不甚重要，因爲中國女子到底還没中那個明星熱，很少肯傾家蕩産，入棄家庭去尋求機會的。但是美國女子的思想就有些超越常軌了。

這種競賽之中，最不幸的一件事，就是受吸引的人，普通都是小城市，學校裏的，比較的無知無識的靑年女子。他們從來没有和社會接觸過，所以没有嘗試過失望的滋味。他們没有吃苦的凖備，等到他們發現他們野心大於經騐的時候，往往不堪打擊，而走入一蹶不振的道道。祗要翻開報紙來看一看，就可以看到許多「尋人」的小廣告，若再細細地讀下去，就可以發現妻子失踪哩；她瞞了丈夫去加入美女競賽，失望之後，就一去不返了，還有競賽告終之後，就有許多自殺案發生；警察方面，受父母的請求尋覓他們的子女的，不計其數，探其原因，一部份亦都歸罪於電影公司的各種競賽。

影片談評

評「玉殿藏春」

— 摩爾

DieFledermaus

電影的宣傳效果，旣然爲世人所公認。但是有一部份人是故意不承認電影，乃至於一切藝術的宣傳性的。一方面他們却儘量製作宣傳片，所謂宣傳片自然不限於宣傳某種政治主張的正面影片，卽使那種催眠着他們所需要催眠的人，麻醉着他們所需要麻醉的人的影片，他們同様努力製作，自然，效果是并不壞於他們的正面宣傳的。一方面他們又可以不居宣傳影片和藝術的政治性之名。『玉殿藏春』之爲這類的影片，是顯而易見了。

很多人估量着這種宮幃中粉香脂膩的影片，都只是有閑者的消閑品，然而實際上，這種估計，是不够的。

一般的說，歐洲電影界製作宮幃片之類，是較之美國製片者容易得至效果的。因爲美國太年靑，而宮幃片等等故事和佈景，又都是過去時代的。所以美國的製片者都不很熟悉，一方面因爲美國最近代化的經濟組織的形態電影的表現手法，也同様的較適合於表現現代的男女糾紛，而不很適宜於宮幃故事。卽以『玉殿藏春』而論，他的佈景鏡頭，較之美國片一般的古老與緩漫，而這古老和緩漫無疑的中更逼眞，更適合於這一種影片。

卽以導演而論，他是非常注意分量的均匀，尤其是叙述中心故事的旁襯，這様觀衆得到的感覺，就非常的豐富與舒泰。當然，這豐富與舒泰，并不是指多餘和鬆懈而言。

演員的表現，在故事的决定之下，自然也不會像美國片中的跳浪和浮游。　　總之，假使我們想看一些歐洲電影的舊藝術的話，在這張『玉殿藏春』中，是看得到的。

評『瓊島風雲』

— 凌鹤

（一）

在這裏，我祗能寫出一點感想。

冬天，給與人們一種可怕的感覺，灰白色的雲層高壓在我們頭上，冷酷的空氣，緊緊縛紥着我們的心胸，使我們幾乎失了呼吸的本能。我懷着沉痛的感覺在冷風中掙扎着。我想：前幾天下了一層白雪，當然在這幾天以内，也許還有更可怕的白色呈現在我們眼前。然而一想到冬天過了，馬上便是春天的到臨，這給與我們一種極歡樂的新鮮的希望。一想到這裏，便增加了我極大的勇氣。好的，且掙扎着罷，可愛的春天，總會降臨到人間。

（二）

『瓊島風雲』正在這冷酷的冬天開映，格外使戲院的空氣嚴肅得可怕。

我極力忍耐着沉悶的情懷，看完了官製的新聞片之後，又看完了這一部極庸俗不通的『瓊島風雲』，我深深的惋惜電影藝術給人們無理由的毁滅。假使電影，這東西，在中國就這様糟踏下去，那末，朋友們，請想想罷！我們將必然的否認電影之眞價存在。

（三）

電影這東西，始終有其在藝術上的眞價，特别是在這狂風暴雨的年頭，在這無論誰都感覺藝術饑渴的時候，我們更應當維護電影在藝術上的尊嚴。

但是像『瓊島風雲』這類的影片，在藝術上的眞價，却完全給人們毁滅無餘，而完全成爲宣傳品，這是極其可鄙的地方。老實說，中國觀衆絶對不需要這種毫無理由的宣傳。在這國亡無日的時候，「安内而後攘外」的言詞，我們已經聽得够了。

（四）

再說罷，電影之成爲宣傳品，在目前已成爲顯明的事實。不過宣傳一定要有事實根據，同時這種宣傳一定要爲人們所接受。譬如說：「白宮風雲」是宣傳品，「羅宮春色」也是宣傳品，二者同様給人們厭惡的感覺，然而其宣傳的本領却是非常高强的。

那末『瓊島風雲』怎様呢？眞是可笑，不管在任何方面說，都是非常拙劣的。簡直可以說，完全不成其爲電影啊！

此外，我不想再說什麽了。

好萊塢的歲尾年頭

— 羅芬

好萊塢到了歲尾年頭，比較無論那裏都覺得熱鬧。好萊塢的人物，都是異常高興的消磨幾天快樂的光陰，在這幾天之中，都佈滿了喜氣，什麽憂患和任何一切的不快樂都已丢悼了。

卓别麟平常是不出外的。在好萊塢的街上平常很少看見他的。但是一到了歲尾年頭在好萊塢常常可以看見他出没於幾家小跳舞塲中和小咖啡館中。但是大宴會和大跳舞會中，是不大容易見他的。

約翰巴里穆亞和李昻巴里穆亞弟兄二人，並不是喜歡滑稽的人物，但是到了歲尾年頭亦很會取樂。他們二人在去年曾設立了一個巨大的慈善跳舞會。這一天所收入的票價，都捐作貧民救濟會中的基金。

梅樊斯德是最近好萊塢很紅的一個人物，她在今年的新年預備了許多的衣服送給一般貧苦人家的孩子就並且他親自在毎一件衣服上簽着自已的姓名。她立志毎一年都要如此盡力的去帮助這些貧苦人家的小孩子呢。

曼麗畢克馥也是一個喜歡送食品給貧苦的小孩子們的，她毎到了年終的幾天親自做了許多糕和食品到了元旦日的淸早她在門口分送給街上的貧苦人家孩子，這是她的老規則，元旦的早上她的家門口，一定有一番熱鬧的。

接吻的滋味

— 東林

美國電影界中的有名的小生，尼爾哈密爾頓在他的銀幕生涯中，曾和七十六位不同的女性接吻過，因此這亦就是說，他曾經騐過七十六種的接吻。據他說：「拍愛情片的時候，假使不考慮對方的女明星的個性而表演是一定要失敗的。接吻亦是同様的，隨對方的女人，其接的方法亦各相異。」

現在讓我把哈密爾頓所分類的，五大女明星的接吻方式介紹在下：「海倫海絲的是最理想的；瓊克勞馥的是暴風雨似的；瑙瑪希拉的是現實的；愛里沙郎弟的是理智的；瑪麗普拉安的是最純眞的。」

電影小說

歌壇絶TheCatandtheFiddle(二）

— 墨塵

米高梅公司出品|雷門諾伐羅琴妮麥唐娜合演

她瞪着他道：「不！」汽車夫回過頭問到什麽地方去。先莉告訴他到拉斐德公寓。維克多笑道：「那我們還是鄰居呢！我們還有機會見面：：：常常見面哩。」她亦不睬他。車子到公寓門口了。維克多連忙替她提着箱子跳下汽車。先莉和他搶着。箱子蓋好了，裏面絲綢的褻衣摔了一地。她連忙蹲下去拾，眼睛瑩然，差不多要哭出來了。維克多跪在旁邊，帮她拾着：：：那些薄綢，花邊，絲帶做成的東西，和先莉自已一様美麗動人：：：還有一陣陣飄忽的丁香花氣味，那就是先莉自已身上使人陶醉的氣息。

她怱怱地走進了公寓。公寓的門在她的身後砰的一聲關了起來，可來他手裏握着一圑細綢的胸衣。他好像得到了先莉自已似的：：：他已不能再生氣不理他了：：：她好似緊貼在他的心頭。他回到自已屋子裏，想要把自已心裏的一切糾紛衝激，譜成曲子，先莉的曲子，充滿了玫瑰花和黃金，他覺着音調在自已的胸口湧了起來，可是隔壁公寓裏，忽然發出了一種鏘鏘的爵士音樂，把他肚子裏的歌意，又壓下却了。他怒不可遏地跑到窗户口喊道：「鍋爐少敲吧！别敲啦！别鬧啦！聽見没有？」那面的窗開了，維克多的心亦沉下去了。那面窗口的人，不是别人，就是先莉。她說：「我聽見了。」維克多假意問道：「你在那里彈鋼琴嗎？好聽極了。那種和諧！那様的精神！」先莉道：「那不過是敲鍋爐吧了：：：不是你剛才說的嗎？」維克多連忙呌屈道：「我？我没有說什麽呀！我剛才正坐着做夢呢，等到夢醒了，我拾着一

件東西。」他說完了舉起他手裏的胸衣揚着，但是那面砰的一聲，窗户關了。

這弄得維克多太難過了，他知道不應當這様輕佻的。他喊着：「先莉！先筣！我知道錯了。」但是那面窗户還是關着，琴聲又起來了，這使他益加害怕了。什麽都完了！難道讓她一輩子當他是個輕佻男子而不理他嗎？要是他能够再見他一面，解釋一下，那他就死而無怨了。他於是從窗户裏跨了出去，在傾斜的屋頂上爬着。他跳了過去，拉住了一條窗　，懸空吊着。他忽然覺得她的手拉着他，帮他爬了起來。等他爬進了窗户，她問道：「你不摔怕死嗎？」維克多笑道：「你剛才所彈的調兒，好像在呼喚我似的。請你再彈一下，好不好？」於是她就坐了下來，重新彈着那醉人的音調，又提起淸脆的嗓子，唱着“Thenightwasmadoforlove"

維克多帶了一肚子的歌，興怱怱地從先莉的公寓裏，跑了出來。他一直奔向音樂院，因爲他的敎授貝蒂爾和道逹先生已經候了他好久了。等到他到了音樂院進門的時候，一個人正從那裏出來，恰巧和他撞個滿懷。維克多因爲那人把他的好夢撞醒了，不覺怒氣勃勃的駡了一聲「混蛋！」後面貝蒂爾敎授發狂似的喊道：「維克多，那就是道逹先生呀。不過你一定不認識他：：：」維克多的夢好像橡皮球一様，　然破裂了，因爲那個從巴黎遠道而來的戲院大�

經理，有意地轉了身走出去了。但是維克多突然間呌了起來：「我的前程送掉了。但是算得了什麽！我快樂極了！我今天看見了一位世界上最美麗的女子。前程算得了什麽：：：她對我笑了一笑！」（未完）

1934.01.11

The Xiamen Rebels Have Been Completely Eliminated

(Nanjing) According to naval sources, the Xiamen rebels have been gradually losing ground under the pressure of the naval fleet and marines for days. On the 10th, the Naval Department sent torpedo squadron commander Wang Shouting, leading ships like the [illegible] and marines, arriving in Xiamen at dawn on the 10th. They cooperated with the naval port commander Lin Guogeng and the fleet marines stationed in Xiamen to completely eliminate all the rebels in Xiamen. All agencies and the entire city have been flying the Blue Sky White Sun flag since 6:00 AM. Xiamen Island has been completely recovered. (10th Special Dispatch)

Complete Restoration of Order in Xiamen

(Nanjing) The rebel army in Xiamen, having been under the pressure of the naval fleet and marines for days, was gradually losing ground. Yesterday, the Naval Department again sent torpedo squadron commander Wang Shouting, leading warships like the Yat Sen and Zhongshan, along with marines, arriving in Xiamen at dawn on the 10th. Cooperating with the local naval port commander Lin Guogeng and the fleet marines stationed in Xiamen, they completely eliminated all the rebel army in Xiamen. This morning, all agencies and the entire city hoisted the Blue Sky White Sun flag, and order has been completely restored on Xiamen Island. (10th Central News Agency Dispatch)

(Nanjing) The navy in Fujian waters is gradually recovering territory. Various departments are discussing and consulting on measures for inspecting foreign ships entering Fujian, which will be suspended. (10th Special Dispatch)

All Xiamen Agencies Taken Over

(Xiamen) In addition to replacing Wang Zongshi with a new Public Security Bureau Chief, Lin Guogeng dispatched Liu Guangqian on the 10th to take over the Municipal Government. Yang Jianshu took over the Siming County Government. Tan, a secretary of the Public Security Bureau, and Lin Hongfei's brother Hongzhu, along with more than ten others, were arrested. (10th Special Dispatch)

Du Qiyun Arrived in Xiamen Yesterday to Work

(Xiamen) Du Qiyun arrived in Xiamen from Hong Kong on the 10th and set up an office to work. At 3 PM, he met with reporters, reporting the process of being ordered to enter Fujian to suppress the rebellion. (10th Special Dispatch)

Siming Party Rectification Committee Established Yesterday

(Xiamen) The Siming County Party Affairs Rectification Committee was established on the 10th. The three members of the committee, Chen Li and two others, took office. Branch party headquarters and sub-branch headquarters in each district were established simultaneously. (10th Special Dispatch)

Negotiations for the Submission of Tan's Troops

(Nanjing) Li Jinghao, Acting Education Director of the Central Military Academy, received a telegram from the front lines stating that the defense of the two cities, Yanping and Gutian, was originally by Tan Qixiu's troops. After one attack by the Central Army, they immediately sent personnel to negotiate, expressing their willingness to surrender. Our army immediately entered Yan City. Now that the city has been secured, the rebel forces are weakening, and a direct advance to Fuzhou is imminent. As for the enemy at Gutian Shuikou, they have also been surrounded and blockaded by our army's certain division and will soon be captured. (10th Special Dispatch)

Naval Vanguard Has Reached Lianjiang

(Nanjing) Chen Shaokuan told the Central News Agency reporter on the morning of the 10th that after the navy captured Luoyuan, the vanguard had reached Lianjiang and was fiercely fighting with the 6,000 troops of the rebel Qiu Zhaochen. The Xiamen navy is also advancing along the Zhangxia Road, attacking the rebel Huang Qiang's forces, which number no more than a few thousand. Our side at Lianshan is currently under the command of [illegible], and the Xiamen side is under the command of [illegible]. Lianjiang is only sixty li from Fuzhou, located northeast of Fuzhou. After the army captured Shuikou, Gutian is also under siege. Shuikou is about eighty li from Fuzhou, located west of Fuzhou. Fuzhou is now surrounded by the central army, navy, and air force and is expected to fall soon. The navy is now coordinating its actions with the army and air force. The rebels are currently in a state of panic. Tan Qixiu's troops have already defected, and Mao Weishou's troops have also requested to surrender. The rebel forces have disintegrated and will inevitably scatter. It is unlikely that the rebels will hold on to Quanzhou and Zhangzhou. Although Quanzhou and Zhangzhou have defenses, the rebel forces are isolated, and the people hate them intensely. After Fuzhou falls, the rebels can be completely eliminated. Furthermore, all naval agencies in Fujian have long been recovered, and two small gunboats have also returned to the fleet. The buildings damaged by the rebels are being repaired, and the losses are not significant. After Du Xigui's death, the affairs of the Naval Academy are temporarily managed by the director of military training. The selection of a successor as principal has not yet been determined and will likely be chosen from among the naval veterans. An announcement will be made soon. (10th Central News Agency Dispatch)

Confirmation of the Recapture of Yanping and Shuikou

(Nanjing) Military sources confirm that the Central Army has recaptured Yanping and Shuikou. However, in Gutian, the rebel Zhao Yijian is stubbornly defending the city, putting up a fierce resistance. The Central Army has surrounded the city and is attacking with fierce artillery fire, which will soon resolve the situation. (10th Special Dispatch)

Complete Elimination of Remaining Rebels at Shuikou

(Nanjing) Military sources state that our [illegible] Division attacked Shuikou on the morning of the 7th and recaptured it at 4:00 PM. This battle involved the main force of the rebel defenders. Over 1,300 rifles, 18 machine guns, and 8 mortars were seized, along with countless ammunition. The remaining rebels fled to the south bank, where they were intercepted and eliminated by our [illegible] Division. (10th Central News Agency Dispatch)

General Order Commending the Song and Liu Divisions

(Nanjing) Chiang Kai-shek issued a general order commending the Song Division for its role in capturing Yanping by occupying Jiudao Mountain, and the Liu Division for its occupation of Mingcui Pavilion, for their successive charges, breaking through the enemy's strong bunkers with blood and flesh. (10th Special Dispatch)

Forward Headquarters Issues Victory Report

(Nanjing) The Forward Headquarters issued a victory report stating that when Shuikou was captured on the 7th, 1,300 rifles, 18 machine guns, and 8 cannons were seized. The rebels fled to the south bank of Shuikou, where they were intercepted and eliminated. (10th Special Dispatch)

Establishment of Six Telegraph Bureaus on the Zhejiang Border

(Hangzhou) The telegraph bureaus in Suichang, Longquan, Ruian, Pingyang, Yunhe, and Qingyuan on the Zhejiang border have been established and are now in communication. In addition, the two new bureaus in Taishun and Jingning have also been brought online. (10th Special Dispatch)

Chen Qixuan's Troops Pursuing the Fujian Army

(Hangzhou) Military sources state that the Fujian army in Shouning has now retreated to Zengban and Badu in Ningde. Chen Qixuan's division has dispatched troops in pursuit, and fierce fighting has broken out. (10th Special Dispatch)

(Hangzhou) The Fujian side has recently been vigorously assisting the bandits and communists in northern Fujian to make a last-ditch effort. Therefore, the bandits in the Fu'an and Fuding areas have become active again. Chen Qixuan in Shouning has concentrated forces to suppress them. (10th Special Dispatch)

Bandits from Shoufu Scurry to Yangkengwei

(Hangzhou) A telegram from Taishun to the province states that on the 7th, more than 300 bandits from Shouning and Fu'an attacked Fuxitou and Xiangjing. They engaged in fierce fighting with the garrison troops for half the night. Unable to withstand the attacks, the bandits fled to Yangkengwei in Fujian Province. (10th Special Dispatch)

Lin Weibang's Troops Occupy Zhangping

(Hong Kong) Gao Yi's troops under Lin Weibang occupied Zhangping on the 3rd of this month. (10th Special Dispatch)

Wu Yuru Declares Independence in Zhangpu

(Hong Kong) It is reported that Wu Yuru, of Yang Tianyu's troops, has declared independence in Zhangpu. (10th Special Dispatch)

Chen and Li Plan to Persuade the 19th Route Army

(Hong Kong) After the disastrous defeat of the Fujian rebel army, the Guangdong army urgently deployed to southern Fujian to intercept them. Chen Jitang and Li Zongren plan to send a telegram persuading the entire 19th Route Army to immediately return to the central government, uphold the central government, and serve the party and the country again to atone for their past mistakes. (10th Central News Agency Dispatch)

Weng Zhaoyuan Assassinated in Quanzhou

(Xiamen) On his way back in Quanzhou, Weng Zhaoyuan was assassinated. The guards resisted, preventing the attempt from succeeding. (10th Central News Agency Dispatch)

Japanese Navy Reconnoitering Zhoushan Coastal Terrain

Seven or Eight Sailors Landed

(Hangzhou) The provincial authorities received a telegram from the Dinghai County Government stating that at 2:00 PM on the 9th, a Japanese destroyer, the No. 27, was anchored in the Dagui waters, ten li from Zhoushan. Seven or eight sailors landed, carrying telescopes, maps, and other items, seemingly reconnoitering our coastal terrain. Around 7:00 PM that evening, the ship weighed anchor and left, direction unknown. (10th Special Dispatch)

Wang Jialie Heads to Guangxi

Wuzhou: The Guizhou King [Wang Jialie] and Zhang Yunliang entered Guangxi on the morning of the 10th and are expected to arrive in Nanning on the 14th. They will stay for about three days and are expected to come to Guangzhou with Li Zongren before the 20th. (10th Central News Agency Dispatch)

Tangzhou: Wang Jialie set off from Guiyang on the morning of the 9th to Nanning, and will likely come to Guangdong with Li Zongren before the 20th. (10th Central (News Agency Dispatch)

(Hong Kong) Zou Lu discussed on the 10th that Li Zongren and Wang Jialie will indeed come to Guangdong, but the departure date is undetermined. Tan Qixiu's defection seems certain. It seems he intends to preserve the 19th Route Army. Whether Hu Hanmin goes to Beijing depends on whether the central government accepts his eight demands. (10th Special Dispatch)

Forward Headquarters Tightens Blockade of Bandit Areas

(Nanchang) The Forward Headquarters is tightening the blockade. Even military purchases of salt require permits and restrictions to prevent abuse by soldiers transporting salt. (10th Dispatch)

Announcement of the Directors of the Six Joint Defense Zones in the Eastern River Painting Zone

Zhong Shaokui's Troops in Shanghang Reorganized by Huang Renhuan

Li Yangjing Sets Up Fujian Military Reorganization Office in Meixian

(Hong Kong) Chen Jitang has divided Dongjiang into six joint defense zones, appointing Huang Renhuan as the director of the Yongding and Wuping joint defense zone, Zhang Ruigui for Chao'an 38th district, Huang Yanzhen for Meixian Jiaoping, Li Zhenliang for Xinghua and Zijin, Deng Longguang for Huiyang and Heyuan, and Luo Xiuli for Hailufeng. (10th Special Dispatch)

(Hong Kong) Military sources report that the Fujian military regiment stationed in Shanghang, Zhong Shaokui's Brigade, was reorganized by Huang Renhuan. Chen Jitang transferred Yan Yingyu's brigade to reinforce the defense of Shanghang and Wuping and transferred the 5th Division, Li Zhenliang's troops, to garrison the Pinghe area of southern Fujian. (10th Special Dispatch)

(Hong Kong) Many Fujian soldiers have recently been fleeing to Guangdong to surrender. Li Yangjing has set up an office in Meixian to reorganize them. Huang Yanzhen's and Huang Zhiwen's two divisions stationed in Xunwu have returned to defend the areas of Wuhua, Xingning, Meixian, and Fengshun. (10th Special Dispatch)

(Hong Kong) Guangdong has requested a loan of 15 million yuan from Hong Kong merchants, but it has not yet materialized. (10th Special Dispatch)

(Hong Kong) Guangdong has requested that Li Bai increase the deployment of a division to take over the defense of southern Jiangxi.

(Hong Kong) Wang Shihua's regiment stationed in Zhaoqing is scheduled to set sail for Hainan on the 12th, and Huang Guoliang's regiment will take over the defense of Zhaoqing. (10th Special Dispatch)

Japan's Purpose in Encouraging Puyi to Become Emperor Is to Prepare for Russia

Zheng Xiaoxu and Others Are Engaged in Fierce Disputes with the Japanese

(Beiping) Talk of Puyi's restoration has been rampant lately. It is heard that the rebel Zheng Xiaoxu and others still advocate restoring the Great Qing Empire, while the Japanese advocate a Manchurian-Mongolian Empire. Therefore, there is a fierce dispute over the title of emperor. At the same time, opinions within the Japanese side are also inconsistent. It is still difficult to predict whether Puyi will be able to usurp the throne and declare himself emperor on March 1st. According to foreign sources, Japan is determined to encourage Puyi's restoration. Its sole purpose is to prepare for Russia. The Japanese plan is that after the establishment of the Manchurian-Mongolian Empire, the puppet organization will be moved into the pass, or at least to Rehe, in order to calmly deploy military operations against Russia in the Northeast and avoid any worries about the rear. (10th Central News Agency) (Dispatch)

(Tokyo) The "Manchukuo" government is no longer officially relying on the Japanese government to find Puyi's tutor. The most likely candidate is rumored to be Count Hayashi Kenzo. This has been reported in previous telegrams. At the same time, it is also requesting to find three senior officials familiar with court affairs. Among the three, former Vice Minister of the Imperial Household Department, Sekiya Teisaburo, is a strong candidate. (10th News Agency Dispatch)

Sun Dianying's Vanguard Arrives at Woye

Military Headquarters Moves to Linhe

(Beiping) Sun Dianying's representative, Hu Jiesan, said that Sun's military headquarters has moved to Linhe. Part of Sun's army left Wuyuan on the 5th, following the Yellow River coast through the vicinity of the Ningxia garrison in Ningyuan Shizuizi and other places, moving towards Woye. The vanguard has arrived at Woye. (10th Special Dispatch)

(Beiping) Sun Dianying telegraphed the Military Sub-Council this morning, stating that his trip to the Wuyuan and Ninghe areas on the 4th was for the purpose of giving speeches to his troops. The rumor that he led his troops westward is not true. (10th Special Dispatch)

(Beiping) Ningxia telegraphed that Sun Dianying's troops are opening up wasteland in Woye for land reclamation. The central government has approved this. After receiving the telegram, the provincial government sent troops along the way to take care of them. The relocation of Sun's troops to Woye is scheduled to be completed within the month. (10th Special Dispatch)

(Beiping) Sun Dianying telegraphed He Yingqin, saying, "My troops rely on your protection and are honored with your generous treatment. We are grateful and will never forget it. I went to Wulin area on the 4th to inspect the defense zone and made a speech to officers and soldiers." (10th Special Dispatch)

No More Fighting in Southern Xinjiang

Provincial Army Garrisoned in Turpan

(Beiping) A telegram from Dihua states that Sheng Shicai is about to return after capturing Yili. Ma Zhongying retreated to Hami, and the provincial army is garrisoned in Turpan. There is currently no fighting in southern Xinjiang. The provincial government is rushing to handle the aftermath. (10th Special Dispatch)

Regular Meeting of the Beiping Military Sub-Council

Decision to Form Military Training Committee

(Beiping) This morning's regular meeting of the Military Sub-Council was adjourned after discussing two proposals because most of the committee members went to Shanghai to welcome Zhang Xueliang and only a few committee members in Beiping were present. (10th Special Dispatch)

(Beiping) This morning's regular meeting of the Beiping Military Sub-Council decided to form a Military Training Committee, with Zou Zuohua and five others as members. He Yingqin will also serve as the chairman of the committee. The organizational outline and powers will be drafted in detail by the General Staff Department and submitted for discussion at the next meeting. (10th Central News Agency Dispatch)

Agreement Reached on Defense of Eastern Chahar

(Beiping) Song Zheyuan summoned Zhang Yunrong, Ruan Xuanwu, Zhang Renjie, Zhang Shukai, and others to a meeting at his private residence tonight. A general decision was made regarding the defense of eastern Chahar. Zhang Renjie's division will be stationed in Chicheng and Longmensuo, Zhang Yunrong will be stationed in Dushikou, and Ruan Xuanwu will be responsible for the defense between Zhangbei and Shangdu. The area of Longmensuo has been taken over by a regiment from Zhang Renjie's division. After the meeting, Zhang and others returned to the defense of eastern Chahar. (10th Special Dispatch)

(Beiping) Zhang Yunrong, the commander of the Zhangbei Garrison, and Zhang Renjie, the commander of the Provisional Third Division, came to Beiping from Zhangyuan yesterday to meet with Song Zheyuan and report on the situation in Guyuan. They will return to Chahar in four or five days. It is heard that the situation east of Guyuan is extremely tense, and the Japanese and puppet troops have not yet shown any signs of withdrawal. Since Xinyuan was occupied by the Japanese and puppet troops, most of Zhang Yunrong's troops have been stationed in the Dushikou area. Zhang Renjie's troops still have two regiments, one stationed in Chicheng County and one taking over the defense of Longmensuo. Zhang Yunying and others believe that a detailed allocation of the defense of eastern Chahar is necessary, so they specially met with Song to ask for instructions on everything. Song is scheduled to return to Chahar to visit his mother in Tianjin Province within three to five days. Qin Decun is in Beiping and plans to stay for about a week before returning to northern Chahar to handle everything. (10th Special Dispatch)

Xiao Focheng Arrives in Shantou

(Shantou) Xiao Focheng arrived in Shantou from Hong Kong on the 8th and is scheduled to go to Siam on the 10th. Yang Dezhao arrived in Shantou from Dalian on the 8th and said that he would stay for two or three days before going to the province to see Chen Jitang for instructions. The date of his return to Nanjing is undetermined. (9th Special Dispatch)

Panchen Lama Scheduled to Depart for Xining

He and Huang Prepare to Welcome Him

(Beiping) The Panchen Lama has been scheduled to depart from Bailing Temple for Xining on the 13th and will arrive on the 17th. The Panchen Lama's office in Beiping and the Municipal Government held a welcome preparation committee meeting on the morning of the 10th and decided to proceed as before. The Panchen Lama's office has found the former residence of Chairman Huang in Fengze Garden in Zhongnanhai to be the location, and it is currently being actively arranged. (10th Central News Agency Dispatch)

(Beiping) The Panchen Lama's office telegraphed Beiping, stating that the central government had repeatedly telegraphed inviting the Buddha to enter Beijing. The lama is now scheduled to depart from the temple on the 13th, and requests that negotiations be made with the Beining Railway Bureau for vehicles to be prepared for use in Suiyuan as soon as possible. (10th Central News Agency Dispatch)

(Beiping) He Yingqin and Huang Fu, because the Panchen Lama's pacification of the border regions has been so meritorious, are preparing to hold a grand welcome meeting after his arrival in Beiping to express their respect. (10th Special Dispatch)

Opening of the Second Column Suppression Conference

(Changsha) The Second Column Suppression Conference opened in Pingxiang on the 10th, chaired by Liu Yinggu. Generals such as Tan Daoyuan, Tao Guang, Zhu Yaohua, and Yue Sen attended. After the closing on the 11th, Liu went to the front to supervise the suppression of Kong's bandits. (10th Special Dispatch)

Liu's Bandits Scattered into Five Groups

Totaling Over Two Thousand Men with Complete Armament

The Henan Giant Bandit Cui Bangjie Commands from Within

(Shi Yousan's Troops Implement Reorganization and Dismissal)

(Tianjin) Yu Xuezhong returned to Tianjin from Beiping at 3:00 AM on the 10th. In the afternoon, he told reporters at the Provincial Government that when Liu Guitang's troops first entered Hebei Province, they had 3,000 cavalry. After repeated attacks by garrison troops and local militias in various counties, they still had over 2,000 men with complete armament. Cui Bangjie, a giant bandit from Henan Province, is commanding from within. They have now scattered into five groups, scurrying towards Jiahe, Gaoyang, Suning, Hejian, Boye, and Raoyang. They appear to be defeated on the surface, but are actually closely connected and difficult to defeat. In addition to ordering Zhang Chengde's cavalry division to pursue them, he also ordered Bai Fengxiang's cavalry brigade to intercept them in the Nangong and Hengshui areas. He also telegraphed the chairmen of Shandong and Henan to prevent and block them at the border. It will not be difficult to wipe them out. Shi Yousan's troops, led by Hu Xie Wu, were sent to Yutian. The Provincial Government agreed to reorganize them into security forces, but they refused to be reorganized for a long time and extorted supplies from the local area. The gentry of the county could not bear this and jointly formed a militia of 7,000 to 8,000 people from Fengrun, Jixian, and other counties, setting up a militia headquarters in Zhushuwu Town and branches in Caiting Bridge and Hongqiao, surrounding the county seat and cutting off traffic. Hu's troops refused to surrender. The Provincial Government, together with the Military Department, sent Zhao Ruyi and Li Yupeng to investigate. Hu finally agreed to accept the reorganization of 1,000 men. The remaining 500 men were given 3,000 yuan by the Provincial Government and sent back to their hometown. The militia then lifted the siege. Regarding the Yuguan issue, the Japanese are intentionally creating difficulties, resulting in the reception being indefinitely postponed. Tao Shangming and Yin Rugeng hosted Yu Xuezhong at a banquet on the evening of the 10th to discuss this matter. (10th Dispatch)

(Beiping) After Liu's bandits fled south from Jiahe, they have reached the Nangle and Dongguang areas. Another small group scurried to the Botou and Nanpi areas and are currently in contact with the local militias. The Hebei Provincial authorities have dispatched additional troops to pursue them. (10th Special Dispatch)

(Jinan) Qingdao sources say that Han Fuju stated that Liu's bandits are still far from Shandong, but precautions must be taken. He has increased the deployment of a regiment from the 22nd Division to the area north of Shandong for joint defense. A cavalry regiment stationed in Zichuan will board a train tonight and pass through Jinan tomorrow morning to go north of Shandong. (10th Special Dispatch)

(Jinan) Today, Steel Armor Commander Dai Hongbin led the Taishan armored train to northern Shandong to patrol along the Tianjin-Pukou Railway to defend against Liu Guitang. Another armored train was dispatched to search and suppress the remaining bandits in southern Shandong. (10th Special Dispatch)

Current Commentary

Government Handling of Wheat Purchase

The other day, the newspaper reported that an official of the National Economic Council stated that the council had received a petition from Shanghai flour merchants alleging that the government's purchase and transportation of flour was harming the domestic flour industry. The responsible officials reviewed the matter and concluded that there was considerable justification for the complaint, and advocated against purchasing flour. Upon investigation, the government's $50 million gold yuan loan is different in nature from previous general loans. The current loan is not in cash, but the government first purchases American cotton and wheat in the United States, with the Financial Reconstruction Corporation of the United States paying the price. The limit for American cotton is 40 million yuan, and for American wheat, 10 million yuan. Our government must wait until the purchased cotton and wheat are transported to our country and sold before obtaining cash. This is what makes it different from general loans.

Some argue that with the government's current position, selling large quantities of foreign cotton and wheat domestically would harm the domestic rural economy. However, Premier Wang has repeatedly cited customs statistics, arguing that domestic cotton and wheat are insufficient, and imports are necessary and would not harm rural areas. Furthermore, the entire $50 million gold yuan loan will be managed by the National Economic Council, which will make overall plans for national construction and rural revitalization. Therefore, it may actually benefit rural areas. Given our nation's poverty, with military and administrative expenses already a struggle, how could we have surplus funds for construction? Moreover, how could we have the credit to borrow foreign debt without harming our sovereignty? Now that the government has managed to borrow 50 million yuan for construction, shouldn't we welcome it? However, on the other hand, regarding American flour, as determined by the experts of the Economic Council, they believe it is unnecessary to purchase. This makes perfect sense, and anyone with common sense would agree. However, is the government free to decide not to purchase under the terms of the contract? Upon investigation, the government's import tariff rates for rice, wheat, and flour, announced on December 16th, showed that the flour tax was twice that of the wheat tax, demonstrating the government's sincerity in protecting the domestic flour industry. Furthermore, it is said that the government suggested to the representatives of the flour mills who petitioned for tax exemption that a condition for tax exemption would be for the flour mills to undertake the sales of the American flour purchased by the government. If this is true, regardless of whether the mills agree, it is not a fundamental solution. If the mills were to undertake the sales of American flour, the flour mills would become sales merchants, inevitably impacting their internal operations. Furthermore, with foreign flour flooding the market, in just six months, the new wheat will arrive. Who will advise on this? This is a concern for the flour mills that would distribute American flour, and it is also something that the government, in its efforts to revitalize rural areas, must consider.

In this difficult situation for both sides, when thinking about construction, we dare to suggest to the government that this American flour, which must be purchased, should not be sold on the market to obtain cash. Instead, it could emulate the "work-for-wheat" approach after the floods of 1932, using the flour to develop the Northwest and provide relief for drought and flood victims in Henan and other places. After the loss of the Northeast, the people and the government have unanimously advocated for the development of the Northwest. Now that the Northwest Office of the Economic Council has been established, when development plans are implemented, all laborers involved in road construction and river dredging could be paid with flour instead of cash wages. The Northwest has suffered from drought for years, with a shortage of grain, and the people have long lost their purchasing power. The government can use American wheat to help them, without conflicting with the business of domestic flour mills. Other disaster areas could also implement the "work-for-wheat" method. Even in the Jiangnan region, where people are accustomed to eating rice, the government could deduct a portion of the wages of workers building roads and embankments and provide them with flour. This would be thinking about construction, forcing a portion of the population to change their diet, and also reducing the consumption of foreign rice, without the contradiction of competing with the domestic flour industry. Now that the people are impoverished and resources are exhausted, borrowing one item or one coin should be used as ten items or ten coins. From purchasing American wheat to implementing construction, management should be extremely economical. Currently, the price of American flour is generally higher than that of domestically produced flour. Selling it on the domestic market would inevitably require it to be cheaper than domestically produced flour. Now that grain prices in the Northwest and other disaster areas are higher than in other regions, wages should also be higher. If the government converts the purchased flour into cash and then disburses wages, it would suffer a double loss. Is this economical? If the purchased flour is directly transported to the work sites as supplies, it would not only avoid the aforementioned losses but also avoid harming the domestic flour industry. It would also save on the commissions of brokers during sales. Saving a penny allows for more construction, which cannot be considered unwise. What is particularly important is that the transportation of flour can indirectly increase people's livelihoods. From the start of transport to the destination, state-owned railways, shipping, lighterage, boatmen, brokers, and others would all benefit. After the 1932 floods, all industries were in decline, and cargo transport was at a standstill. If it were not for the Water Disaster Committee's "work-for-wheat" program, transporting and storing wheat flour, and using wheat flour as wages, it is unknown how many tens of thousands of civilian boats along the river would have been split into firewood, and how many tens of thousands of workers would have become bandits. This also has a significant impact on people's livelihoods.

Regarding the management of American wheat, we also feel compelled to speak. Recently, there have been rumors that the distribution of American wheat will be entrusted to five foreign import firms to sell to domestic flour mills. If the Chinese authorities are transacting with the Chinese people, why must they rely on foreign merchants as intermediaries? We suspect the accuracy of this claim. However, those who say this argue that if foreign merchants are not involved in the sales, then manufacturers, knowing it is government wheat, will suppress the price, making it unavoidable. The manufacturers have their own explanation. We believe that in national construction matters, the people should cooperate with the government. Manufacturers should have an organization whose members strictly adhere to agreements. Except for the necessary blending purposes, they should not purchase foreign wheat from foreign firms in addition to government wheat. They should also submit a comprehensive budget based on the size of the mill and the urgency of their needs for the government's reference when making purchases in the United States in stages. The government should disclose the purchase price and sell it to the mills at cost. Except for transportation fees, insurance fees, interest expenses, and other items, it should not seek additional profits, acting as a purchasing agent for the mills. However, since purchases are made at different times, prices will vary. If the mills are concerned about disputes arising from different purchase prices for the wheat they receive, they can use the average cost over a certain period as the selling price. As for the protection of payments, it should be handled according to common commercial practices. There are many ways to do this, so why must it involve foreign merchants? We hope the government and the flour mills will work together on this.

Pacific American-Russian Defense Alliance

U.S. State Department Denies Establishment of Understanding

(Washington) The State Department declared that rumors of an understanding between the United States and Soviet Russia to prepare for the conclusion of a Pacific defense alliance are completely unfounded. (Havas dispatch, 9th)

United States Expands Navy

House of Representatives Begins Discussion

(Washington) Today, the House of Representatives cited the strength of the Japanese Navy as a reason to increase the U.S. Navy. Representative Vinson, Chairman of the House Naval Affairs Committee, introduced a bill authorizing the President to build new ships and replace old ships, so that the strength of the U.S. fleet would be suitable to the extent permitted by treaties. When proposing this bill, Vinson mentioned Japanese naval power, saying that Japan already possesses the naval strength permitted by treaties, and Britain will also act accordingly. However, U.S. warships are uniquely behind, in a frighteningly dangerous position. Even if all the currently under construction new ships are completed, it will still feel that the strength is insufficient. (Reuters dispatch, 9th)

(Washington) Representative Vincent proposed today to add more warships. Vincent said that if the United States does not quickly add warships, it will lose its naval position in the world. He suggested building aircraft carriers of 15,000 tons, destroyers of 99,000 tons, and submarines of 35,500 tons. There have been two proposals regarding the Navy in Congress in the past two days. Yesterday, Representative Britten's proposal suggested building 101 warships over four years starting this year, costing approximately $482 million. (National Telegraph dispatch, 9th)

Hitler Actively Plots for Austria

National Socialist Party Challenges Austrian Government

Terrorist Incidents Expected in the Saar Region

(London) A dispatch from Berlin today revealed German Chancellor Hitler's plans for Austria. It is said that after Austria raises the flag of the National Socialist Party, Habicht will be the first National Socialist Prime Minister of Austria. This plan cannot be realized until Austrian Chancellor Dr. Dollfuss leaves office. However, the German and Austrian National Socialist parties expect Dollfuss to resign soon. At the same time, a report revealed in Geneva stated that the Saar Administrative Commission recently seized documents proving that the National Socialist Party had established an organization that uses terror and boycott tactics to undermine the Saar government, and plans to send members from within the Saar region to enter Austrian territory, because it is not difficult to obtain passports in the Saar. In order to prevent German expansion, Russia urgently wants to protect the security of its western frontier, fearing that it will be constrained once war with Japan breaks out. (Reuters dispatch, 10th)

(Vienna) National Socialists throughout Austria have now challenged the government. A Salzburg police station was bombed today, causing considerable damage. In the Dallas area, a gendarme was also injured by a bomb. Smoke bombs were also thrown in various places in Vienna. The government is now redoubling its efforts to clear the chaotic atmosphere. (Reuters dispatch, 10th)

League of Nations Scheduled to Meet to Discuss Saar Issue

Simon to Participate in the Opening Ceremony

(London) The next meeting of the League of Nations Council will be held on January 15th. The most important item on the agenda is the preparation plan for the 1935 Saar region plebiscite to determine whether the region should be returned to Germany, incorporated into France, or remain under the League of Nations' management. The important coal mines in the region owned by Germany have been acquired by France as compensation for the destruction of coal mines in northern France by the German army during the Great War. The ownership of the coal mines will not be affected by the result of the plebiscite, as it must belong to France according to the Treaty of Versailles. The Council meeting will also consider the report of the newly established Advisory Committee on Slavery, and the dispute between Bolivia and Paraguay, and seek a place to live for Assyrian Christians. British Foreign Secretary Simon will participate in the opening ceremony and plans to return to England afterwards, with Under-Secretary Eden representing the British Foreign Office. (Reuters dispatch, 9th)

Thorns in Disarmament Still Awaiting Diligent Removal

Preparatory Committee Meeting Postponed

Mussolini Receives French Ambassador

(London) According to reliable sources, European countries will postpone the opening of the Disarmament Preparatory Committee, originally scheduled for January 22nd, until early February. People close to the British Foreign Office declared that the reason for this postponement is to allow countries to have sufficient preparation and understanding. However, the main reasons are the following: (1) German Chancellor Hitler can have sufficient time to make a detailed reply to France's memorandum; (2) U.S. Plenipotentiary Davis will not be able to arrive in Europe until the end of January; (3) The British government still needs to study Italy's new proposal in detail, based on recent important talks between Italian Prime Minister Mussolini and British Foreign Secretary Simon; (4) Disarmament Conference Chairman Henderson still needs to contact various countries and adopt their opinions, which takes time. As for the Italian Prime Minister's determination to support Germany's demands, it will become the biggest issue for the Disarmament Preparatory Committee. According to the new proposal sent by the Italian Prime Minister to the British Foreign Office, he has repeatedly expressed his support for Hitler's demands. (National Telegraph dispatch, 9th)

(London) According to the Daily Telegraph's diplomatic correspondent, in the view of all sectors in Britain, holding the Disarmament Steering Committee meeting on January 21st as scheduled will be ineffective. It also stated that the earliest meeting date would be January 29th. (National Telegraph dispatch, 10th)

(Rome) No news has been released about the content of Italian Prime Minister Mussolini's talk with French Ambassador Chambrun. Diplomatic circles believe it is related to British Foreign Secretary Simon's recent visit to Rome. (National Telegraph dispatch, 10th)

League of Nations Fourteenth Anniversary Commemoration

French Government Fully Supports

Germany Will Not Join Without Reorganization

(Paris) Today is the fourteenth anniversary of the founding of the League of Nations. The French government still strongly supports the League of Nations. Foreign Minister Paul-Boncour will inherit Briand's legacy and strive to thoroughly reorganize it. Since its establishment, the League of Nations has achieved considerable success and has greatly benefited mankind, such as in the relief of infants and women, and the improvement of international transportation, postal services, public health, and economic construction. (National Telegraph dispatch, 10th)

(Berlin) According to general observation, Germany has gradually broken away from the constraints of the Treaty of Versailles, and its recent political policies have focused on two major issues: demanding equality in armaments and recovering the Saar region. It is now planning to begin discussing these issues with France, but whether it will succeed is difficult to predict. However, the two countries' views on disarmament issues are too divergent. As for the Saar region, France is determined not to easily return it to Germany. Germany withdrew from the League of Nations on October 14th last year, expressing its opposition to disarmament and its desire to undermine the Treaty of Versailles. In the fourteen years since the League of Nations was founded, Germany has been a member for only seven years. During these seven years, it was constantly dissatisfied with the League of Nations, saying that the League of Nations was a tool of French politics. Therefore, general politicians say that unless the League of Nations is thoroughly reorganized and not used by France, Germany will never be willing to join again. (National Telegraph dispatch, 10th)

French-Russian Business Negotiations Successfully Concluded

New Agreement Initially Signed Yesterday

(Paris) Authorities declared today that negotiations between France and Russia on a new trade agreement have been successfully concluded. This is sufficient proof that the relations between the two countries are becoming increasingly friendly. The agreement will be signed for the first time tomorrow, and officially signed on Thursday. It is heard that the agreement stipulates that Soviet Russia will purchase 2,500,000,000 francs worth of French goods this year, guaranteed by the French-Russian Trade Bureau. France will purchase Russian oil, wood, and manganese. Recently, relations between Russia and France have progressed rapidly, causing considerable unease in Japan and Germany. Political figures hope that the economic integration between the two countries can consolidate their political relations. (Reuters dispatch, 9th)

Little Entente Meets to Organize Economic Alliance

And Hopes Neighboring Countries Will Join

The Little Entente Economic Conference held its first meeting here today, chaired by Czech Foreign Minister Dr. Beneš. The conference is composed of five representatives from each country. This meeting is dedicated to discussing the close cooperation of railway transportation and telegraph and telephone communications, and will also involve standardizing commercial law and simplifying customs procedures. This is the beginning of the Little Entente's economic alliance. The main difficulty now lies in the fact that both Yugoslavia and Romania are increasing the export of agricultural products, which is strongly opposed by Czech farmers. (National Telegraph dispatch, 9th)

(Prague) Representatives of the three Little Entente countries, Romania, Yugoslavia, and Czechoslovakia, held an economic meeting in the Czech capital today. Czech Foreign Minister Dr. Beneš was the chairman of the first meeting. According to reliable sources, the three Little Entente countries will become the nucleus of a new economic body to replace the economic union destroyed by the failure of the Austro-Hungarian Empire. The Czech Foreign Minister stated that the three Little Entente countries do not want to adopt a closed-door policy, but are willing to cooperate with neighboring countries. (Reuters dispatch, 10th)

Wells Delivers Speech Saying the League of Nations Has No Backbone

Failure Is Inevitable Because It Is Not Suitable for the Times

Advocates Close Cooperation Between Britain and the United States

(London) Yesterday was the fourteenth anniversary of the founding of the League of Nations. The famous British writer H.G. Wells gave a radio broadcast speech in the evening, severely criticizing the League of Nations, saying that Geneva has completely failed, but it should be like this, because the League of Nations is a political machine without a backbone, and has nothing to do with our world and the current major economic problems. Wells also emphatically said that internationalism is now gradually declining around the world, and advocated for closer economic cooperation between Britain and the United States. (National Telegraph dispatch, 10th)

Paris Public Demonstrates Against Chautemps Government

Explosives Placed on Tram Tracks

Two Hundred and Fifty People Arrested

(Paris) Today, thousands of people in Paris demonstrated in protest of the Bayonne municipal bond case, opposing the Chautemps government. As a result, up to 250 people were arrested. The instigation of this demonstration was due to a certain Communist Party newspaper carrying a report that the death of Stavisky, the financier involved in the Bayonne municipal bond case, was secretly executed by the police, because Stavisky held evidence unfavorable to senior police officials. Except for the demonstrators, no one believes this claim. The demonstrators gathered in various places in Paris, often clashing with the cavalry. At the same time, they placed explosives on the tram tracks, further disrupting order. Fortunately, when the demonstrators attempted to break into the Chamber of Deputies, the police and cavalry rushed to prevent it. Currently, the government is trying to deal with the opposition's attacks after dismissing Colonial Minister Dalimier, and immediately introduced a bill in the Chamber of Deputies prohibiting untrustworthy people from engaging in the trading of stocks and bonds. Those who violate this prohibition will be sentenced to imprisonment for up to two years. This plan will be presented to Parliament on Thursday morning, and the opposition will begin attacking the government at the same time. If the government cannot overcome this difficulty, it may face collapse. Upon investigation, this cabinet was formed on December 27th last year. If it collapses, its term will be no more than one and a half months. It is heard that the police in Chamonix obtained Stavisky's whereabouts, led by Stavisky's ex-wife. (Reuters dispatch, 9th)

(Paris) Since the outbreak of the Stavisky scandal in France, the Chautemps cabinet has been in danger of collapsing. The reorganization of the cabinet is gradually taking shape, and everything is in line with expectations. However, Paul-Boncour will still be reappointed as Foreign Minister, as it was rumored in advance that Herriot would be appointed to the post of Foreign Affairs. Furthermore, since Stavisky's death, the media has continued to argue that Stavisky's suicide was actually facilitated by the government. In order to ease public sentiment, the authorities ordered a detailed examination of Stavisky's body. The deceased's wife also went to the location of Stavisky's suicide at the same time, under the strict protection of special detectives, with the aim of searching for any hidden banknotes, stocks, and bonds in the area. Currently, the committee organized by the people aims to thoroughly investigate the state of the Paris judiciary to determine how Stavisky evaded legal judgment and whether the Paris authorities were conniving. Today, it was discovered that Stavisky had been charged 19 times since 1929, and the 13th Paris Municipal Council actually postponed each case 19 times. During this period, four court presidents and five prosecutors were suspected of committing offenses. He was charged again last June, but on the day of the trial, not only did the defendant not report, but all witnesses and plaintiffs did not appear in court. Stavisky's lawyer, according to the law, told the court his usual story, that his client's mind was slightly unwell, and asked the court to grant him extreme leniency. The reorganized cabinet will face severe questioning in the Chamber of Deputies starting on Thursday, but it is expected that the cabinet will still be safe and sound. According to Léon Blum's daily newspaper, the Socialists will unanimously support the government to pass a vote of confidence. (National Telegraph dispatch, 9th)

(Paris) Radical Socialist members of Congress held a special meeting today to discuss the Bayonne scam. Someone asked Herriot if the party had received Stavisky's assistance. Herriot firmly replied with one word, "No." The conference then passed a resolution supporting Premier Chautemps's strict plan to investigate the case. (National Telegraph dispatch, 9th)

(Chamonix) Stavisky, the main figure in the Bayonne scam, repented and committed suicide. He was buried this morning. His wife attended the funeral. When the coffin was placed in the grave, she fainted from extreme grief. It is said that Stavisky's last letter to his wife was opened and read by the police in front of his wife last night. It contained the line, "The only love I can give you is to prove it with eternal farewell." (Reuters dispatch, 10th)

Saitō Hiroshi to Take Up Post in the United States Next Month

Exchange Views with Various Sectors in the United States First

Report Back to the Country and Determine Diplomatic Policy

(Tokyo) The new Japanese Ambassador to the United States, Saitō Hiroshi, has decided to go directly to Washington from the Netherlands and is scheduled to arrive in the U.S. capital in mid-February to take up his new post. Foreign Minister Hirota has cabled Ambassador Saitō to exchange views with political and business circles in the United States and examine the national conditions. He will return to Japan once in April or May with the basic materials for his diplomatic work in the United States. Foreign Minister Hirota will then, based on his report, personally instruct him on the steps for diplomatic work. (China United Press dispatch, 10th)

Greek Foreign Minister Arrives in London

(London) Greek Foreign Minister Maximos arrived in Britain via Rome and Paris to discuss the international situation with the authorities. He arrived here at 7:15 tonight. Foreign Minister Simon will receive him. (Havas dispatch, 9th)

Roosevelt's New Policy

Non-Productive Land Under State Management

(Washington) The U.S. government plans to establish a land management company in the near future. This is the U.S. President's land policy, which will place all non-productive land under public management. If this company is established, it will need to allocate 25 million to 50 million U.S. dollars from the Relief Loan as startup funds. According to a survey by the Land Economics Section of the Rural Economics Office, one-sixth of the land in the Rocky Mountains and along the Atlantic coast is unproductive. Farmers are eager to sell as soon as possible so that they can find other ways to make a living. The government will use this land for afforestation and other projects. (National Telegraph dispatch, 9th)

Import Restriction Issues

France Informs British Government

Ready to Start Negotiations

(Paris) The French Foreign Ministry issued a document stating that it has informed the British government that France is ready to start talks with Britain to discuss reducing the quota for British imports by 75 percent. These talks will be preceded by general trade negotiations between France, the United States, and Britain. Italy, Belgium, and the Netherlands are currently conducting these negotiations with France. The document also emphatically stated that France treats all countries equally and has no intention of discriminating against Great Britain. However, France's treatment of the United States cannot be uniquely preferential, and it cannot abolish all or part of the quotas without receiving something in return. (Reuters dispatch, 9th)

(Paris) The French government has reached an agreement with the United States regarding the issue of limiting the quantity of imported goods. The Foreign Ministry yesterday notified the U.S. Ambassador that the French government recently reduced the quantity of imported foreign goods by 75 percent, and now completely restores the original situation. However, the total quantity of U.S. imports will be divided into two parts. One part, 25 percent, is the quantity that the United States is sure to obtain. The remaining part, 75 percent, will be reserved for negotiations with the U.S. government to exchange for benefits. (Havas dispatch, 9th)

France Uncovers Another International Espionage Case

Another espionage case was recently uncovered near Metz and Guénange in France. A citizen of Luxembourg named Freyming was arrested for stealing diagrams of border defense works and has been imprisoned. After questioning by the investigating magistrate of Guénange, he has revealed part of the truth. (Havas dispatch, 10th)

Dumping of Japanese Goods Threatens the West

British Newspaper Urges Urgent Prevention

No Other Way Than to Prohibit Imports

(Tokyo) According to official statistics released today, Japan's trade in 1933 increased by 100 million yen compared to the previous year. Total exports amounted to 1,932,000,000 yen, and imports totaled 2,018,000,000 yen, resulting in an import surplus of 86,000,000 yen. (Reuters, 10th)

(London) The "Standard Evening News" published an article stating that the competition from Japanese commerce in Western markets is extremely fierce. The working classes in Britain and other countries are consequently affected, with their livelihoods increasingly threatened. Urgent measures should be taken on the economic front to prevent this. The author believes that prohibiting the import of Japanese goods is tantamount to economic warfare and would lead to the repeal or amendment of certain treaties. However, there is no other way to defend against Japanese competition. The author also stated that the threat from Japanese commerce to the West has reached an extreme level, and defensive measures are urgently needed. It is hoped that the government will take the initiative to defend itself. If the British government takes action, all countries with high wages will cooperate with it. (Havas, 9th)

New Investigation Department Established in the Japanese Foreign Ministry

Divided into Five Sections to Handle Affairs Separately

(Tokyo) (10th) The regulations for the division of sections within the newly established Investigation Department of the Foreign Ministry were announced on the 10th as follows: The Investigation Department is divided into five sections. The first section is responsible for investigating historical facts related to diplomacy and investigating matters belonging to other sections within the department. The second section is responsible for organizing records, foreign-related cases, and recording and organizing their progress. The third section is responsible for investigating all kinds of affairs related to politics, diplomacy, commerce, and economy in "Manchukuo" and China. The fourth section is responsible for investigating the politics, diplomacy, commerce, and economy of European countries and regions not under the jurisdiction of the third and fifth sections. The fifth section is responsible for investigating the politics, diplomacy, commerce, and economy of North, Central, and South American countries. (Domei, 10th)

Page 8

Dutchman Lubbe, Convicted of the German Reichstag Fire, Executed on the Guillotine

Remained Calm During Execution

Request for Pardon Denied

Leipzig: The Dutchman Lubbe, the main culprit in the German Reichstag fire case that shocked the world, was beheaded at the court at 7:30 this morning. According to official sources, the execution was carried out because President Hindenburg did not want to exercise his power of pardon. Since Lubbe was sentenced to death, he had been under the surveillance of Professor Penghefei, a psychiatrist.

Leipzig: The Dutch defendant Lubbe, sentenced to death in the German Reichstag fire case, was executed this morning in the Leipzig court prison. Last night, General Werner, the chief prosecutor, notified the defendant that President Hindenburg had decided not to exercise his supreme right of pardon. Lubbe showed no emotion upon hearing this news and remained in his gloomy state. The warden asked Lubbe if he needed any religious ceremonies or anything else before the execution, but Lubbe did not answer. At six o'clock this morning, the warden entered Lubbe's cell and announced that the time of execution had arrived. The prisoner immediately got up and followed the guards without saying a word. General Werner, the chief prosecutor, State Attorney Barisis, Federal Court President Pangrui, three other judges, a doctor, a Jesuit pastor, and other important figures were present at the execution site. Press representatives were not allowed to attend the execution. Lubbe listened to the reading of the death sentence with a calm face and without any expression. The court president asked if he had anything else to say, but Lubbe only shook his head. After Lubbe went up to the guillotine, the blade fell in a matter of seconds, and the execution was completed.

Note: Lubbe was a Dutchman. Shortly after the German Reichstag caught fire on February 27th last year, he was arrested near the Reichstag. At that time, the Hitler government blamed the Reichstag fire on the Communist Party, and the National Socialist Party relied on this case to seize power. In addition to Lubbe, those arrested included German former Communist Party member of parliament Dierglei, Bulgarian Communist Party members Dimedrov, Popov, and Danav, etc. After months of trial by the Leipzig court, Dierglei and the three Bulgarian defendants could not be proven guilty. Only Lubbe was proven to be the main culprit in the arson and was sentenced to death. However, Lubbe had lost his physical abilities during the trial, so the case became a mystery, and the truth could not be revealed. After Lubbe was sentenced to death, the Dutch government requested a pardon, but it was not granted, and he was executed today. (Havas, 10th)

A Glimpse of the Execution

(Berlin) Lubbe, the main culprit in the Reichstag fire case and a member of the Dutch Communist Party, was beheaded at 7:30 this morning because President Hindenburg refused to grant him clemency. It had been nineteen days since Lubbe was sentenced to death. It was not until late last night that the Leipzig warden informed Lubbe that the president did not want to exercise his power of pardon and that the execution would be carried out the next morning. Lubbe responded with the same indifferent attitude he had shown during the trial. He was then asked if he wanted a priest to pray for him, but Lubbe did not answer a word and did not express any special wishes. The executioner and his assistants built a guillotine overnight at the prison site. At six o'clock this morning, the warden led Lubbe to the prison site. Only the prison bell rang slightly, announcing that a guilty person was being executed. The public did not pay attention to the execution and did not expect that the executed person was Lubbe. Those present at the scene included Public Prosecutor Dr. Weiler, Leipzig Court President Bunge, three Supreme Court judges, the Senate Warden, and twelve others, as well as one doctor and one pastor each. Lubbe listened with his head bowed to the death sentence. The whole scene was silent. Lubbe followed the executioner to the guillotine. The executioner wore evening dress and white gloves. After Lubbe was secured, his head fell in less than thirty seconds. The executioner then announced that the execution was over. It is reported that the German authorities notified the Dutch government of the execution date two days ago, but no Dutch official was present this morning. Lubbe was examined by a doctor last night, who said that his mind was clear. (Reuters, 10th)

Jade Pagoda Displayed in Chicago

Request for Seizure Due to Unpaid Commission

May Not Be Effective Even with High Court Approval

(New York) A jade pagoda produced by Zhang Wenji (transliteration) of Shanghai, which has been displayed in the Chinese Pavilion of the Chicago Exhibition and the Rockefeller Institute in New York, is now being sued by a man named A. Jin in the Supreme Court. Because Zhang Wenji, the producer of the pagoda, owes a commission of $10,160, he is requesting seizure. Judge Laurie of the High Court has approved the request, but because the Rockefeller Institute has provided a guarantee of $250,000 to ensure that the pagoda is shipped out of the United States, according to U.S. law, this seizure approval is invalid. (Havas, 10th)

Government Rescue Ineffective

The Dutch government in The Hague expressed great disappointment today at Germany's execution of Lubbe. It is reported that the government had tried its best to rescue him, hoping to reduce the death sentence to life imprisonment. The German authorities notified the Dutch consul in Leipzig that Lubbe's family would be allowed to claim the body for burial. (Reuters, 10th)

Unlikely to Have Further Action

The Hague: According to authorities, German Foreign Minister Neurath notified the Dutch ambassador in Berlin last night that there was no reason to pardon Lubbe and that he would be executed the next morning. Dutch officials believe that this is a matter of the German government's judicial rights, and the Dutch government is unlikely to take further action. (Reuters, 10th)

Dutch People Are Very Outraged

Amsterdam: When the Dutch people heard the news of Lubbe's execution, they were generally very outraged. They felt that after negotiations with the Dutch government, President Hindenburg would definitely reduce Lubbe's death sentence to life imprisonment. Now that the bad news has arrived, everyone is shocked and at a loss. (Reuters, 10th)

Inside Story of the Japanese Financial World

Mitsui Zaibatsu Secretly Colludes with the Bank of Taiwan

The Minseito Party Plans to Raise Questions in the Diet

Involving the Minister of Railways and Communications Gives Military Cliques an Opportunity to Take Advantage

(Tokyo) As a result of the investigation by the Policy Research Council of the Minseito Party, an improper relationship between the Mitsui Zaibatsu and the Bank of Taiwan has been discovered, and it is planned to question the government in the 65th Diet. In Showa 2 (1927), during the Hamaguchi Cabinet, the Bank of Taiwan had a deficit of 200 million yen due to the bankruptcy of Suzuki Shoten. The government allocated funds, and all business was reorganized under the Bank of Taiwan. Among them, the Imperial Artificial Silk Company made huge profits after the September 18th Incident. The Mitsui Zaibatsu then sought to acquire its shares. Representatives of the Mitsui Zaibatsu, such as Ikeda Seihin and Go Seinosuke, secretly negotiated with the president of the Bank of Taiwan, selling the shares to the Mitsui Zaibatsu at a 20% discount compared to the market price. It is reported that the two ministers of the Seiyukai Party, Mitsudo and Hatoyama, were involved in this case. The matter concerns official discipline, and they want to launch a crusade in the Diet. If this matter is raised, the financial cliques will give military cliques an excellent opportunity due to private disputes. Financial figures are very worried about this case. (Chinese United Press, 10th)

Ministry of Finance Prepares to Issue Customs Bonds

(Nanjing) At the regular meeting of the Central Political Council on the 10th, Finance Minister Kong Xiangxi temporarily proposed that approval be given to issue 100 million yuan in customs bonds for the Republic of China in 1934. The reason was that the government had misappropriated funds from the Central Bank over the years, amounting to nearly 100 million yuan. The Central Bank's funds are relied upon to circulate in the market, and they cannot be borrowed for a long time without repayment. However, the government's financial difficulties make it difficult to raise large sums of money. It is now proposed to issue the above-mentioned bonds to repay the Central Bank in full as collateral, so that they can be cleared in installments. Since they do not circulate in the market, they are not related to the market's finances. On the one hand, the Central Bank's funds are consolidated, and on the other hand, the government retains room for financial turnover. The discussion at the scene lasted for quite a long time, and in the end, the principle was passed and handed over to the Legislative Yuan for deliberation. After the meeting was adjourned, Finance Minister Kong invited Legislative Yuan President Sun Ke to talk privately in the hall committee office for an hour and a half, explaining the difficult situation. It is heard that Sun has become more understanding, and it is hoped that the proposal can be submitted for passage at the Legislative Yuan's meeting this week. (Special Dispatch, 10th)

Ministry of Finance Requests Correction of Measures for Rewarding Assistance in Smuggling Suppression

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Finance submitted a report to the Executive Yuan stating that, according to the Inspector General of Customs, smuggling was becoming increasingly rampant. It requested that local authorities assist customs in preventing the illegal import of foreign goods. Measures were drafted stating that when taxable foreign goods and contraband were smuggled into various coastal areas without customs checkpoints, the local authorities should detain both the ship and cargo and hand them over to the nearest customs office for handling. After the customs office confiscated the ship and cargo, half of the bonus should be sent to the local authorities for distribution, etc. Upon instruction from the Executive Yuan, orders were issued to the governments of Zhejiang, Jiangsu, Guangdong, Fujian, Shandong, and Hebei provinces to comply accordingly. The Inspector General of Customs reported that since these measures had been circulated by the Executive Yuan, all provincial agencies would certainly comply uniformly without shirking responsibility. However, regarding the bonus, according to current customs practices, if customs officers seize smuggled goods without any informants, they are awarded 20% of the proceeds from the sale of the goods. If there are special meritorious services, the bonus is 30%. For contraband, the bonus ranges from 20% to 60% of the estimated value, depending on the quantity and whether the suspects are apprehended. Now, if various agencies are awarded half of what customs officers receive, the bonus for seizing ordinary goods would only be 10% or 15%, and for contraband only 10% to 30%, which seems too meager to encourage action. Furthermore, the customs office has always treated public security and postal bureaus that assist in seizing smuggled goods and transferring them to customs as informants, awarding them 40% for ordinary goods and 30% to 50% for contraband, depending on the quantity and whether the suspects are apprehended, as per established procedures. Now, giving other agencies assisting in seizing smuggled goods a similar amount to customs officials is inappropriate. For the sake of promoting smuggling suppression and maintaining tax revenue, it is proposed to follow the precedent of awarding public security and postal bureaus and to uniformly award local government, tax, police, army, and navy agencies that assist in seizing smuggled goods and transferring them to customs according to the informant bonus method. (10th Day Special Dispatch)

Jinpu Railway Plans to Build a Branch Line from Bengbu to Zhengyangguan
