World War Panic襲擊瑞士　列·山·　(European Correspondence)

｜The Swiss Militia System is Worth Noting｜

No matter how moving Hitler's peace speeches are, no matter how loudly the French sing about security guarantees, hoping that Europe will be safe and sound, no matter how much Britain fears the danger of war, no matter how Mussolini changes direction, acting as a peace envoy to mediate the European situation, all these actions cannot conceal an iron-like fact: the outbreak of European war is only a matter of time. These platitudes and peace-promoting actions only prove that everyone's preparations are not yet complete, and they are unwilling to act for the time being, a scene of conserving energy and waiting for the right moment. The good show is yet to come.

During the last European war, Switzerland was fortunately spared. In the eyes of the Swiss people, this was an extremely lucky thing. Currently, everyone's premonition is different. It is clear that in the coming war, Switzerland will not be able to remain neutral. Will it align with Italy or with Germany? Switzerland must choose between Germany and France. Therefore, a group of military professionals, capitalists in military-related industries, and French politicians are secretly fueling the flames, expanding the situation and intensifying the public's perception of war. Especially since the second half of this year, newspapers have repeatedly promoted the German military general staff's plan to take Switzerland's path when waging war against France. For a time, this caused a great uproar. Later, on the border between Germany and Switzerland, the German Nazi stormtroopers clashed with the Swiss border guards. This was tantamount to adding fuel to the fire, a propaganda material of the best kind. A neutral small country, whose citizens are usually called pacifists, is now slowly being drawn to the altar of the god of war.

The one who is causing the European situation to fall into a state of tension again is naturally Hitler. He advocates that all German peoples unite and return to Germany. The German population accounts for 69% of Switzerland's population, while the French population accounts for only 21%. If Hitler's proposal is implemented, it would be tantamount to Switzerland being annexed to Germany. This is not only dangerous for the French, but the Swiss themselves also feel uneasy. On the other hand, as the editorial of a Swiss newspaper said, Switzerland is located between the three fascist powers of Germany, Italy, and Austria. Once the European situation changes, Switzerland will be in an extremely difficult position. Under the pressure of the above reasons, there is naturally no other way to go except to strengthen military preparedness. Therefore, the military budget has been increased, and the military organization law has been re-improved to make it more modern.

Although Switzerland is a small country with only four million people, in terms of military preparedness, we have no reason to underestimate it. They themselves are also very clear that it is better to prepare more strength than to rely solely on justice and fairness to maintain their neutrality, perhaps the effect will be greater. To date, Switzerland's military preparedness has at least the following advantages, which seem to surpass the major powers: ㈠ Implementing universal conscription, a thorough militia system; ㈡ The excellent shooting skills of individual soldiers, probably unmatched by any other country in the world; ㈢ In addition, Switzerland also has special strengths in chemical warfare military supplies. If any country wants to invade Switzerland and take this risk, Switzerland will immediately counterattack head-on. Although victory or defeat is not guaranteed, it will never be a case of non-resistance.

Switzerland does not have a formal standing army. All it has is a militia. But in the world, we will never easily find a second country like Switzerland that has achieved the point of "no one is not a soldier." And not only in terms of technology, with exquisite achievements, but also in terms of military ethics, there is a very in-depth education. The Swiss people in general, that is, the soldiers, believe that protecting their country and maintaining Switzerland's neutrality has almost become a national characteristic of Switzerland. The foundation of the Swiss militia is organized on this point.

The general Swiss people, rather than saying that they are living various professional lives, it is better to say that they are living military lives. Every person has a rifle, a full set of military uniforms, and other war necessities. All these items are allowed to be taken home for safekeeping. Every Sunday, even in the smallest village, there is a target range. Almost all young people come to participate in shooting practice.

This target range belongs to the local community, but it is also under the jurisdiction of the military. This is speaking of the infantry. As for the cavalry, in addition to full armour, there are also horses. Most farmers can also use these horses to work on the farm, but they must pay attention to protection, because every year the cavalry captain comes to take charge of the inspection work. Their weapons, horses, and shooting practice results are usually recorded in a book for reference.

The population of Switzerland totals over 4.1 million. In wartime, approximately 500,000 soldiers can be mobilized. This type of army, organized by age, can be divided into three types. Young men from 20 to 29 years old join the artillery corps. Young men from 20 to 32 years old join the infantry corps. Together, 220,000 people can be drawn from these two groups. The reserve team, from 30 or 33 years old to 40 years old, can reach more than 110,000 people. People aged 41 to 48 form the national army, which is also about 100,000 people. Others, such as the ambulance teams and transport teams serving in the rear, etc., can also recruit 150,000 people. Moreover, Switzerland's borders are narrow and transportation is convenient. In the event of an emergency, all can be mobilized and concentrated within a few hours. Recently, it has been working hard to expand new military equipment, paying special attention to aviation plans, which will soon be fully realized. At that time, the combat effectiveness will naturally be even stronger. Although the number of Swiss troops is not large, its combat capability is naturally inferior to that of major countries in terms of endurance. However, if an enemy wants to invade Swiss territory in a short period of time, it is feared that it will have to make extremely large sacrifices. In addition, for another reason, Switzerland is mostly mountainous, with high ground and easy defense and difficult offense, and the geography also occupies a considerable advantage.

The term of service for Swiss soldiers is 29 years for ordinary soldiers and 32 years for officers. New recruits are required to undergo military education when they reach the age of 20. In the recruit school, the infantry receives 65 days of training, the cavalry receives 90 days, including horsemanship, and the artillery and flight teams receive 75 days. If the new plan is implemented, this time will probably be further extended. Every year, there are usually 25,000 new recruit students. In addition to this formal training, their usual training is almost non-stop throughout the year, especially for the training of pilots and artillery. In addition, with the support of the federal government and the governments of various states, there are various para-military educations, such as the Swiss Sports Federation, which spends 450,000 Swiss francs each year to train 25,000 young people in snow sports. Another example is the Shooting Federation, which trains 10,000 16-year-old young people to practice shooting every year. Each young shooter can receive five Swiss francs and fifty bullets each year. There is also a national Swiss shooting competition held every year under the auspices of the Junior Infantry League. This naturally encourages and cultivates many talents. But the most important thing is that their lives at ordinary times are already connected to life in the barracks. For the Swiss, shooting practice every Sunday does not seem to be a job, but a game or entertainment. They themselves no longer have the feeling that practicing shooting is being a soldier. This is because of a long historical relationship, which has gradually made them feel that their behavior is natural and has become a habit. In addition, an exercise battle is held once a week or every few weeks, which reviews the tactics they learned in the recruit school and makes their knowledge of war more sophisticated.

In the eyes of us Orientals, Switzerland is such a small country, and it is also a permanently neutral country. Naturally, the people should not only say peace, but also be unable to hold a gun. However, in fact it is not so. Not only do they not wag their tails and beg for mercy, hoping to get a temporary peace, but they go a step further and fully prepare to give any ambitious person a blow when they try it. This is armed peace. We don't care how Switzerland is forced by the environment and has to embark on a road. But the facts that are revealed, maintaining peace through armament, this is indeed worthy of our deep reflection.

The world is probably not going to be peaceful from now on. Before, everyone thought that the United States could last forever. What is it like now? Switzerland, the only safe country in the West, is now in a storm. We should be worried about the group of important people in China. Once a crisis strikes, where will they escape to?

There is no pure land in the world at present, which is indeed a problem. 1933·12·14·Europe

Puyi to Move to Rehe After Declaring Himself Emperor of Puppet State

Puppet State's National Title Set as Great Harmony Manchuria

Attempt to First Invade Chahar and Suiyuan, then Gradually Advance

Japanese Army Acts Arbitrarily Everywhere, Disregarding China

Beiping Correspondence. Japan is actively preparing for a world war and has decided to expand the puppet organization of Manchuria in order to suppress its aggression in North China and defend against the desires of a strong Russia. Since the signing of the armistice agreement, the Japanese side has not given up its aggressive ambitions in North China. The North China Independence Movement, the separatist movement, and various other conspiracies have emerged endlessly. However, because of the actual impossibility of success, all have failed to materialize. Recently, they have changed their policy, on the one hand using Shi Yousan and others to secretly engage in activities, seizing opportunities to disrupt, and on the other hand instigating Puyi to declare himself emperor, expand the organization, and extend its influence to western Mongolia. The movement to restore Puyi has been brewing for a long time. Some advocate changing the name to "Great Qing Empire" and expanding the scope to include the interior of China. Others advocate maintaining the status quo of the puppet state of Manchuria, only changing to an imperial system. Still others advocate "Manchu-Mongol State," including Mongolia. Zheng Xiaoxu went to Tokyo before the new year to discuss this matter, and it was roughly determined that the national policy committee of the puppet state, which was preparing for the restoration, convened an important meeting at the beginning of this year and decided that the national title would be "Great Harmony Manchuria" and the political system would be a constitutional monarchy. On the 15th of this month, it will issue a declaration of change of regime, and Puyi will ascend the throne on March 1. After ascending the throne, the first step will be to move the capital from Changchun to Rehe, the second step will be to invade Chahar and Suiyuan, so that when fighting against Russia, it can both prevent Russia's attack and copy the Russian army's rear by Mongolia. The third step is that after seizing Chahar and Suiyuan, it will see the changes in the situation and slowly advance towards North China. At the same time, the traitors bought in the interior of China will rise up in response, forming another situation, or the "Great Harmony Manchuria" will be expanded again.

Recently, the actions of the Japanese army in the north have often gone beyond the scope, disregarding China. The Japanese army invading eastern Chahar is building airfields, constructing roads for automobiles, and deploying fortifications. All kinds of facilities are extremely busy. The Japanese military in the war zone, also in the name of blocking Liu Guitang, is acting freely, from Gubeikou to Miyun. Yesterday, they moved from Miyun to Sanhe, traveling freely. The authorities can do nothing. Observing the current situation, the hidden dangers in North China are worrying, even worse than in the Northeast before September 18. (January 7)

Details of the Jinpu Railway Robbery

Fortunate That Public Funds in the Guard Car Were Not Robbed

Jinan Correspondence. The Jinpu Railway's third southbound express train was robbed by bandits in the early hours of the 8th, at 0:45, in the Heihuzhuang (i.e., Heifengkou) area south of Dongbeibao in Tai'an County. The losses were quite heavy. When the train left Tai'an Station and was heading towards Dongbeibao Station, a person used one yuan in Real Estate Bank notes and two yuan in cash to purchase ten third-class tickets to Darukou Station. The ticket seller at the station immediately sold them the tickets at the price. Subsequently, ten people, all dressed as farmers, entered the station and boarded the train. When the train passed the first signal flag outside, at kilometre 441.100, Liu Guangyu, squad leader of the fourth team of the train's escort, considered it suspicious that ten people had boarded the train at a station that was both small and at night. He intended to conduct an inspection immediately. As he walked from his office location between the second-class and third-class cars, the bandits became aware of it and fired a shot at Squad Leader Liu to demonstrate. One bullet struck Liu in the shoulder. The bandits continued firing shots and began robbing. At this time, one oiler and two teahouse workers were injured, the oiler being more seriously injured. The train still did not stop and traveled about a *li*. More than ten people were found beside the train, immediately shouting to board the train. The bandits on the train also crawled to the front of the train. After the driver was forced to stop the train, only the sound of people shouting to board the train from all directions could be heard. Both the first and second-class passenger cars were searched, and those on the third-class cars who were neatly dressed were also not spared. When the Tai'an and Dawenkou stations learned of the incident, it was already past 2:00 AM. Military police rushed to the scene, but the bandits had already scattered. Fortunately, the large sum of money in the guard car, which was being transported from Jinan to the general office, was not robbed. Zhou Baiqi, the magistrate of Tai'an County, rushed to the Dawenkou area to search. The third armored car arrived at the scene of the incident this morning (the 8th), but no trace of the bandits could be found. (8th Day)

After the organization is established, work can begin on a scheduled basis.

Those Escaping to Shanghai Say Panic in Fujian

People fleeing : : Market depressed

Since the Central Army recaptured Yanping, people in Fuzhou have been extremely uneasy. Yesterday, the Jardine Matheson’s ship “Jie Sheng” came to Shanghai from Fujian with many passengers. Our reporter specifically asked passengers about the recent situation in Fujian. They stated that people are panicked every day, and the market is even more depressed.

People Extremely Uneasy

Fujian is very secretive about the war on the front lines, so the people cannot know. Since the Central Army occupied Yanping and the Fujian Army was defeated on the front lines, the defense of Fuzhou became suddenly tense a few days ago. When the Jie Sheng ship left Fujian, there were defensive works on the outskirts of Fuzhou, with barbed wire and sandbags along the city, as well as obstacles. After 6:00 p.m., all the lights in the city were turned off, and there were no more night markets in the shops, so people were greatly panicked. Japanese residents in Fujian have been moving to Nantai to take refuge.

Residents Fleeing Everywhere

The wealthy residents of Fujian fled to Hong Kong and Shanghai to take refuge as early as a month ago. After the authorities banned the migration of the masses, and those leaving the country had to be certified by the Public Security Bureau, the residents were even more panicked. Therefore, the middle and lower classes have also been fleeing far away recently, fearing interference from the authorities, so most of them fled to Xiamen, and then from Xiamen to various places. Those who have not left Fujian are all people who are unable to travel far.

[P-City Extremely Depressed>

Business in Fuzhou has been stagnant for the past two months, and trade in all industries has almost completely stopped. Because of import and export goods, the customs has no tax revenue. The authorities telegraphed the shipping companies in various places last month, requesting them to restore the Fuzhou route, and requested Chinese ships to change their flags to foreign flags. As a result, none of the Chinese merchant ships sailed, causing financial panic to reach an extreme level.

Foreign Ships Profiting Immensely

In the past two months, only the British Jardine Matheson’s ship “Jie Sheng” has been sailing on the Shanghai-Fujian line. The Osaka Company of Japan has three ships, but only one ship sails every day. Therefore, the “Jie Sheng” has the best business. Every time it comes to Shanghai, the ship is full of passengers. In the past, the steerage berths were only sold for six or seven yuan per person, but now they have been successively raised to more than fifty yuan. A canvas berth also costs more than forty yuan, and you have to plead with them, fearing that others will buy it. Mr. Deng, the comprador of the ship, has always suffered losses every time, but since the Fujian Incident, the income from passengers has increased more than ten times compared to before, and he can earn more than one or two thousand taels per trip. The comprador has become a millionaire in more than two months. Jardine Matheson has a guaranteed payment system, which has also increased relatively. Recently, when the ship goes to the Min River, it is often inspected by the navy when entering the port.

Refugees in the “Jie Sheng” Ship

In the last trip between Shanghai and Fujian on the “Jie Sheng” ship, there was a shortage of both import and export goods. On this trip to Shanghai, water transport and other items from Fujian are full again. As for the export goods shipped from Shanghai to Fuzhou, they have also suddenly increased, about three or four hundred tons, mostly wheat flour and textiles needed for people’s livelihood. This time, there are more than 400 Fujian refugees taking the “Jie Sheng” ship to Shanghai to take refuge.

Su Bing Wen’s Speech

Coming to Shanghai this time to meet old subordinates

Ma Zhan Shan going to the United States is not true

Meeting Old Subordinates

According to Su, since he settled in Suzhou, he has been writing and reading behind closed doors all day long, and has not been able to clearly understand external affairs. There is no task for coming to Shanghai this time. Because many of my former generals who fought against Japan in the Northeast in the past are now scattered in Shanghai, seeking a living, and it has been several months since we last met, so I came to Shanghai to meet them. Recent Situations of Ma and Li

The reporter then asked about the Jin telegram claiming that General Ma Zhan Shan recently requested the government to allocate 30,000 yuan to go to the United States for inspection. Is this true? According to Su, I have not been in contact with General Ma for a long time, and I do not know his recent situation. However, I learned that the visit to the United States for inspection is probably not true. As for General Li Du, he has not left Shanghai since returning from Mount Lu, and his brain disease has not yet healed. Su did not say that my former subordinate, Zheng Run Cheng’s army, who retreated from the Northeast to Xinjiang via Russia, is now stationed in Dihua, and its station is within the jurisdiction of Sheng’s department, which should be close to the provincial government. Because Xinjiang is located on the frontier and transportation is inconvenient, communication is difficult, and the recent situation cannot be known.

Zhang Xue Liang Invited Old Subordinates to a Banquet Yesterday Afternoon

Asked in Detail About the Situation in North China

Written Speech Rescheduled to be Released Today

Zhang Plans to Enter Beijing for the Fourth Plenary Session

Since Zhang Xue Liang, former chairman of the Peiping Military Affairs Committee Branch, arrived in Shanghai, the date of his departure from Shanghai has not yet been determined. Zhang continued to receive guests at his residence yesterday morning, and hosted a banquet for his old subordinates in Shanghai at noon. He is scheduled to release a written speech this afternoon. The details are as follows:

After the Central Army’s Victory in the Campaign Against Fujian, China Merchants Bureau Formally Takes Over Two Sea Vessels

Hai Xiang and Hai Rui Change to Hang Bureau Flags

Because of the business development of the China Merchants Bureau, the number of ships is insufficient for distribution, so there is a move to build seven new river and sea ships. During the time of the former Guo Wai Feng, two Norwegian sea vessels were purchased and assigned to the North and South Ocean routes. However, because the ship price was not paid, it was impossible to take over for a long time. Until Liu Hong Sheng took office, in order to develop the business and lack tonnage, he paid the ship price first. Now it has been formally taken over, and it will be reported to the Customs immediately to correct the ship name and change the Bureau flag, and it will be assigned to the North and South Ocean routes. This is also the price of valuable documents.

Two Norwegian Vessels

Hai Rui was originally named Beutem, with 1,850 tons, and Hai Xiang was originally named Bentik, with 1,852 tons, each with a draught of 261 feet. They were both Norwegian merchant ships. In the 21st year of the Republic of China, Guo Wai Feng purchased them from a Norwegian shipping company while in office. It is heard that the ship price was 16,000 pounds, and it was agreed to pay in installments. The ships were first used by the Bureau, and must wait for the ship price to be paid off before they can be received by the Bureau. Therefore, although the two ships have been assigned to various routes for two years, they still fly the Norwegian flag.

Ship Price Paid Off

In November of last year, due to the successful intermodal transport of the Longhai Railway, the Bureau initially planned to send the two ships to operate on the Lao Yao route, so Liu Hong Sheng paid the final installment of the ship price for the two ships, preparing to have the Bureau formally take over and assign them to the Haizhou intermodal transport route. Later, due to the draught relationship, Tonghua and other ships were changed to operate on the Lao Yao route, and Hai Rui and Hai Xiang were still sailing on the Qingdao-Guangdong line. After the ship price was paid, it was originally scheduled to be received and renamed in December of last year, but the Fujian Incident occurred again and was postponed until today.

Formally Receiving Passengers

After the Fujian Incident occurred, the two ships were relatively safer to operate in Xiamen and other places because they flew the Norwegian flag. Therefore, the receiving date was postponed until today. Recently, because the Central Army won the campaign against Fujian, there is no problem for merchant ships to operate, so the Bureau decided to formally take over the two ships as soon as possible and assign them to the route as soon as possible. The Bureau has issued the ship names "Hai Rui (HaeJui)" and "Hai Xiang (HaeHsiang)," the tonnage, length, hatch, machinery, number of wheels, deck, and construction year (built in the United States in 1918), and submitted them to the Maritime Administration of the Ministry of Communications, the Jianghai Customs, and other places for registration, and applied for ship licenses. The documents were sent out immediately in order to remove the Norwegian flag and change to the Bureau flag.

Assigned Route

The two new ships are purely cargo ships and have no passenger seats. The Bureau has already decided that after receiving them, the Qingdao to Nanhua route has the most cargo transportation, so the two ships will still be ordered to operate on that line, and the Wu Yang and Kun Xing ships will replace them to operate on the Lao Yao route in Haizhou, and the Tonghua ship will be replaced to operate on the Tianjin route. The Jiahe ship will temporarily run on the Yangtze River route, so that the ships will not be empty and the goods can be transported.

Invited Huang Shao Gu to Meet and Talk

Zhang started receiving guests at his residence on Moliai Road from 10:00 a.m. yesterday, such as Liu Zhi Lu, the former army commander of Zhang Zong Chang, and invited Central Committee Member Huang Shao Gu to his residence at 11:00 a.m. for a meeting.

He may enter Beijing for the Fourth Plenary Session, but he has not made a decision, and will decide based on the situation in the Central Government and other aspects.

Mrs. Chen Zong Dai, Son, and Others

Li’s Old Subordinates Also Sent Personnel to Visit Li and Ask for Instructions

Min Yan News Agency says that after General Li Du, the former deputy commander of the Northeast Border Defense Army stationed in Jilin, retreated to Russia, tens of thousands of his old troops remained stationed in Jilin Province, led by Chen Zong Dai as the acting commander-in-chief, and continued to resist Japan for another year. Because Chen ran out of ammunition and supplies, his dependents retreated to Russia first, and arrived in Shanghai on the Sergei Kiroff ship from Vladivostok the night before last. The details are as follows:

Retreating from Jilin to Russia and Returning to China

Mrs. Chen and her two sons, one daughter, and eight relatives of Chen, cared for by adjutant Wu Bing Wen, retreated to Russia in August of last year and stayed in a Russian hospital. On January 3 of this year, they set off from Vladivostok on the Sergei Kiroff, a cargo ship of the Business Office of the Dongxing Railway of this port, and sailed for a week. It arrived in Shanghai the night before last and was docked at the No. 15 pontoon in Yangshupu. General Li Du, together with his wife, Ms. Xie Yi Qing, went to express condolences to Mrs. Chen and other dependents of the anti-Japanese generals who came to Shanghai that evening. Because the rear supply had been cut off, Yu and others were forced to retreat to Russia and return to China in August of last year. The thousands of troops who retreated to Russia were led by Chief of Staff Xu Qi Dong to Boli. Mrs. Chen spoke with grief and indignation.

Ding Chao is Still Alive

Among those who came with Chen’s dependents this time was also Liang Qi Shan, the representative of Gao Yu Shan. This time, he came to meet General Li to ask for instructions on everything. As for General Ding Chao, chairman of the Jilin Provincial Government, because he was forced to surrender to Japan, he was sent to Changchun. News has been cut off, and it was previously reported that he was killed. Now it is learned that Ding is still living in Changchun and has not held any false positions. He also sent Zhao to Shanghai last month to report the recent situation to General Li.

First Special District Rent Reduction Movement

The Citizens' Union Held a Representative Assembly Yesterday

Resolved to Contact Various Groups to Carry it out Jointly

The First Special District Citizens' Union of this city, citing the economic depression and high rents in the concession area, which are unbearable, convened its fourth representative assembly at the Municipal Chamber of Commerce meeting room yesterday afternoon at 2:00 PM to discuss all matters. Zhang Yichen, Hu Fengxiang, and Ye Jiaxing served as the presiding group, and Zheng Dongshan served as the recorder. The meeting adjourned at 5:00 PM. It was also decided to invite assistance from all sectors on the 16th. The details of the meeting are recorded below:

Representatives Present

The following representatives from various branches were present: Zhou Fuzhang, Zhang Henghai, Zhang Renyan, Chen Hanquan, Chen Jiufeng, Cai Qiaojun, Wang Hanliang, Qiu Jialiang, Shen Hefu, Zhang Yichen, Zhang Xianfang, Xing Guxiang, Chen Jingxuan, Liu Zhongying, Le Shuzi, Hu Fengxiang, Ye Jiaxing, Ye Qichang, Wang Honghui, Wang Hesong, Chen Jicheng, Shen Tianxin, Wang Yansong, Wang Xiaolai, Cao Zhigong, Chen Binghui, and more than forty others.

Chairman's Report

After the formal salutations, the presiding group reported, stating in brief: (A) The representative assembly convened today is due to the economic depression in Shanghai, which has been hit by financial difficulties and difficult for all industries to maintain. Although the prices of all goods have fallen, rents remain high and difficult to bear. Therefore, this union has initiated a rent reduction movement to relieve the suffering of the people. (B) The resolutions passed by the previous rent reduction preparatory committee are submitted to this assembly for discussion and approval.

Resolutions

After the report, discussions began. (1) Proposal for rent reduction: Resolved: (A) Contact various groups to cooperate unanimously. (B) Request various groups to nominate one or two responsible representatives to attend. (C) Convene a representative assembly of various groups at 2:00 PM on the 16th of this month. (2) How to handle the rent reduction proposal: Resolved: (A) Submit it to the representative assembly of various groups for detailed discussion. (B) Request various groups to submit written opinions on rent reduction measures for discussion at the representative assembly. (3) Proposal to name this union the Shanghai Rent Reduction Movement Committee: Resolved: Submit it to the representative assembly of various groups for discussion. (4) How should we start on all rent reduction plans: Resolved: Have the Rent Reduction Preparatory Committee formulate and submit it to the representative assembly of various groups for discussion and approval. (5) Proposal to expand the union's affairs and establish branches: Resolved: Approved in principle, with the executive committee to formulate detailed measures. (6) Proposal to set a date for the third general election of this union: Resolved: Tentatively scheduled for February 1st.

Announcement of Proceedings

After the meeting, notices were sent to various groups, stating: "Dear Sirs, since the impact of the January 28th Incident, Shanghai's prosperity has declined, and commerce is in distress, making it difficult to sustain. At a time when prices are falling and the rural economy is bankrupt, if we want to alleviate the people's livelihood slightly, we must reduce rents to maintain commercial hardship and help people's livelihoods. It was resolved at the fourth representative assembly on the 10th of this month to unite various groups to carry out a rent reduction movement. A representative assembly of various groups will be held at the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce meeting room at Tianhou Palace Bridge at 2:00 PM on the 16th of this month to discuss the measures. We also request each group to nominate one or two responsible representatives to attend in order to promote the proceedings. We hope that opinions on rent reduction will be submitted to the meeting for discussion. This matter concerns the relief of people's livelihood and the maintenance of commerce. We hereby write to your esteemed group, requesting you to nominate one or two representatives and hope that you will take time to attend. Please do not delay. We earnestly pray."

Last Year's Total Operating Income of the Two Railways

Totaled 20,058,000 Yuan

Monthly Income of More Than 1.5 Million at the End of the Year

The Shanghai-Nanjing and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railways Administration announced the operating income for the last month of last year. The Shanghai-Nanjing Railway's income was 1,087,745.99 yuan, with 784,126.39 yuan from passenger transport and 303,619.60 yuan from freight. The Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway's income was 475,566.44 yuan, with 317,343.70 yuan from passenger transport and 158,222.74 yuan from freight. The combined income of the two railways was 1,563,312.43 yuan, with 1,101,470.09 yuan from passenger transport and 461,842.34 yuan from freight. According to the report from the Administration's Accounting Office, the total operating income for the entire year was approximately 14.08 million yuan for the Shanghai-Nanjing Railway and 6.5 million yuan for the Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway, totaling 20.058 million yuan.

Formal Levy of Land Value Tax in the Fahua and Pusong Areas is Scheduled to Begin

The Land Bureau Announced the Collection Maps for the Two Districts

Property Owners Must Declare Prices Starting Today, Deadline is One Month

Formal Levy Set to Begin on March 1st

The city's land value tax, since the municipal government announced it would be levied from August 1st of last year, all land value tax in the Nanshi and Zhabei districts had land values assessed by the Land Bureau and the Valuation Committee, and the collection was started by the Municipal Finance Bureau. Now, the second batch to be levied will be the Fahua and Pusong districts. The Land Bureau has already delineated map numbers and is actively carrying out valuation. It was announced today that the period for property owners in these two districts to declare their prices automatically will be from the 11th of this month to the 10th of February, and the formal levy will begin on March 1st. The details are recorded as follows:

Property Owners Start Declaring Prices Today

The Municipal Land Bureau's levy of land value tax in the Fahua and Pusong districts is scheduled to begin today and last until the 10th of next month as the period for property owners in these two districts to declare their prices automatically. The Land Bureau has scheduled the announcement today for public knowledge. The original text of the announcement is recorded below: "It has been found that the land in each block and household in the Fahua and Pusong districts within the area of the city's temporary land value tax collection has been organized and completed by this bureau, and agricultural taxes should be abolished immediately and land value tax collected instead. According to Article 6 of the Shanghai Municipality's Temporary Land Value Tax Collection Regulations and Articles 3 and 4 (Property Owners Declare Land Value) of the Implementation Rules of the same regulations, the map numbers of each district are hereby opened, and the period for property owners to declare land value is set from January 11th of this year to February 14th. Property owners are required to come to the bureau within the deadline to collect the land value declaration form, fill it out separately, and no extensions will be granted after the deadline. The remaining districts will be handled after subsequent announcements. Let everyone know. This announcement, Bureau Chief Jin Liren."

Fahua and Pusong Collection Maps

As for the detailed maps and blocks within the Fahua and Pusong districts that are stipulated to be priced and levied immediately this time, according to the Shen Shi News Agency reporter's inquiry, they are: (A) Fahua District, Map 1, Tianzi Block No. 1 to No. 18, Dizi Block No. 1 to No. 24, Yuanzi Block No. 1 to No. 21, Map 2, Huangzi Block No. 1 to No. 20, Yuzi Block No. 1 to No. 25, Zhouzi Block No. 1 to No. 11, Map 3, Hongzi Block No. 1 to No. 10, Huangzi Block No. 1, No. 2, No. 3, No. 9, No. 10, No. 16, No. 22, No. 26, No. 27, Map 4, Yuezi Block No. 1 to No. 25, Yingzi Block No. 1 to No. 23, Zezi Block No. 1 to No. 33. (B) Pusong District, Map 1, Dizi Block No. 1 to No. 18, Huangzi Block No. 1 to No. 7. The above households' land is located east to Haig Road, south to Puhuitang, west to the Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway, and west along Lizongjing Suzhou River to the western end of Zhoujiaqiao Town, north to within the scope of the railway.

Scheduled to Start Levying on March 1st

The Municipal Land Bureau has opened the levy of land value tax in the two districts. In addition to the procedures for property owners to declare prices automatically, which have already been announced and are underway, the Land Bureau's pre-valuation procedures are being actively carried out based on various points. According to the reporter's inquiry to the Land Bureau yesterday, most of the Fahua District has been completed, and the Pusong District will start within a few days. After the preliminary valuation is completed, it will be combined with the property owners' automatic price declaration, submitted to the Land Valuation Committee for review, and then sent to the Finance Bureau for joint announcement of the levy. The formal levy date for the two districts has been set for March 1st. If there are no special circumstances at that time, it can be implemented on schedule. The tax payment procedures are exactly the same as those in the already levied Nanshi and other districts.

The Question of the Authority in Charge of Agricultural Tax Collection

In addition, regarding the collection of all income after the levy of land value tax in this city has been completely assigned to the Finance Bureau, the agricultural taxes collected in the districts where the levy has not yet started are still collected by the Land Bureau. Recently, it has been reported that the Ministry of Finance has instructed that, according to regulations, the Finance Bureau should handle these agricultural taxes, and it is said that they will be transferred within a few days. However, according to the person in charge of the Land Bureau yesterday, the bureau has not yet received an order regarding this matter. However, if these agricultural taxes are assigned to the Land Bureau, it would indeed facilitate consolidation.

Japan Plots to Monopolize Fishing in the Eastern Hemisphere

Our Country's Territorial Fishing Rights Will Be Infringed

According to a compilation of foreign intelligence published by the Guidance Department of the International Trade Bureau, the Fisheries Bureau of the Japanese Ministry of Agriculture and Forestry has invested 300,000 yuan over the past two years (i.e., Showa 7 and 8) in a large-scale survey of southern fishing grounds in the South China Sea and the South Seas, discovering countless new fishing grounds and achieving great success. Based on this experience, the bureau plans to expand the overseas fishing ground survey on a wider scale and fundamentally reorganize to adopt a comprehensive policy of seizing overseas fisheries. The budget for the next fiscal year has been increased to 1.46 million yuan, which has been decided by the Ministry of Agriculture and Forestry and is currently being negotiated with the Ministry of Finance. It is said that this revised plan for overseas fisheries policy also includes a base plan for the future of Northern Ocean fisheries, and even intends to expand dramatically to the entire ocean in the Eastern Hemisphere, opening an unprecedented situation in the history of Japanese fisheries. This move is not only for the development of fisheries, but also attempts to provide powerful assistance to its navy in Pacific operations, which is worthy of attention. The outline of the plan is briefly described as follows:

Survey of Fishing Grounds in the Eastern Hemisphere

In the past, the Japanese government's fisheries research institute did not have fishing ground survey vessels. Now, it plans to invest 900,000 yuan to build a 1,000-ton fishing ground survey vessel to search for new fishing grounds in the entire South China Sea, Southern Ocean, Indian Ocean, and Pacific Ocean. The new fishing grounds obtained with more than 500,000 yuan in the next fiscal year will focus specifically on the Pacific Ocean, so that the dispatched fishing vessels can also serve as reconnaissance of the sea surface, creating a powerful intelligence network to provide powerful assistance for Pacific operations in the event of an emergency. As for the Antarctic, whale populations are known to be abundant, and the harvest will be great. In addition, the fisheries research institute will study the utilization and disposal of fish and other large quantities of fish.

New Inspection Vessels for Northern Ocean Fisheries

The navy will allocate 1,000-ton-class special service ships and destroyers to be converted into Northern Ocean fisheries surveillance ships to replace the existing Kinshū Maru. The estimated first-year budget is 350,000 yuan, and the second-year budget includes equipment for shipboard aircraft for surveillance and investigation of fish schools. This is because the current surveillance ships, such as the Shōhō Maru, Hakukō Maru, and Shun'yō Maru, are felt to be insufficient for application, and it is planned to build two new 100-ton and 60-ton vessels, with a budget of 370,000 yuan.

Reorganization of Fishing Grounds Has Already Begun

Because the current fishing grounds and fishing areas are complex and uneven, and disputes over fishing rights are constant, it is planned to carry out controlled reorganization and unification to guide economic development and seek the revitalization of the fishing village economy. The Ministry of Agriculture and Forestry and the prefectures and counties will send special guidance to take charge of this matter, with a budget of 240,000 yuan. In addition, an advance base for Northern Ocean fisheries will be established as part of a five-year plan, with a total cost of 16 million yuan (3.3 million yuan in the first year), and preparations have already begun. The base location is roughly on Paramushiro Island, Funato Bay. This base case is an important part of the ocean fisheries expansion plan, and a decision has been temporarily reserved due to budget concerns. According to the above, if each is realized, there is no doubt that the fishing rights within China's territorial waters will be greatly infringed upon, and it is advisable to pay attention to this as soon as possible.

Postal Service to Xinjiang Partially Suspended

According to news from the Shanghai Post Office, the postal routes to Xinjiang have all been blocked, causing the postal services to and from that area to be temporarily suspended. All types of mail sent to that area that have already been mailed are being held in transit. Airmail to Gaolan and areas west of Jiuquan has already been suspended. Although other types of mail to Xinjiang are currently being accepted as usual, they will only be forwarded to the point where transportation is blocked. As soon as the postal routes are open, they will be forwarded to the recipients' locations.

General Labor Union Petitions for Protection of Laborers

Year-End Dismissals Are Approaching

Employers Dismissing Workers

Requesting Prompt Prevention

The Shanghai General Labor Union yesterday submitted a petition to the Municipal Party Headquarters, the Municipal Government, the Bureau of Social Affairs, and other agencies, stating: "Petition to prevent employers from dismissing workers without reason at the end of the lunar year, to relieve the hardship of workers and ensure social stability. After the Establishment of the Fishery Protection Office, Various Ships Departed Yesterday for Patrols

After the Ministry of Industry abolished the Fishery Administration Bureau and established the Fishery Protection Office, the original site of the former Jiangsu-Zhejiang Fishery Administration Bureau in Runshoufang, Tongqing Street, was inconvenient for dispatching patrol ships, so it was planned to find a suitable location on the Bund for office work. The patrol ships of the Jiangsu-Zhejiang, Hebei-Shandong, Fujian-Guangdong, and Hebei-Shandong-Guangdong bureaus, except for the two patrol ships of the Fujian-Guangdong and Hebei-Shandong bureaus, have not yet been taken over by the office. The remaining four ships of the Jiangsu-Zhejiang area, such as the Haihong, Haigu, Haiying, and Biaohai, were dispatched yesterday to protect fisheries. It is estimated that: (1) the Haiying patrols the area between Shenjiamen and Shengshan; (2) the Haigu defends between Chongming Island and Shengshan; (3) the Haihong is in charge of the area between Shenjiamen and Wentai; (4) the Biaohai departs at any time to patrol various places. According to Director Yuan Lianghua, the fisheries protection by the ships is sufficient for distribution. The winter fishing season is about to expire, and the spring fishing season will begin around mid-January of the lunar calendar. The office has decided to set up fisheries protection according to the past management bureau's methods.

The Sanbei Company's New Ship, the Jing'an, Sails to Qingdao This Morning

Hosted Visitors from All Circles Yesterday

The Sanbei Company purchased the Jing'an ocean liner from the Ministry of Navy for 260,000 yuan. After the company thoroughly repaired and greatly transformed it, added passenger seats, and built new rooms, the entire project was completed a few days ago. In order to open a new route between Shanghai and Qingdao and inaugurate a formal passenger ship, it is permitted to depart from Shanghai to Qingdao for its first voyage today. Because the ship's hull is strong, its machinery is excellent, and its speed is high, it is expected to take 32 hours to reach Qingdao from Shanghai. Yesterday, the ship was docked at the company's pier in Nanshi. Tea and refreshments were specially prepared on board, and Yu Qiaqing and manager Shen Zhongyi, among others, hosted visitors from all circles and fellow countrymen. Many guests came on board to visit and were treated with tea and refreshments. The ship has a displacement of 3,500 tons, a length of 260 feet, a width of 40 feet, a draft of 15 feet 4 inches, and an engine power of 1,000 horsepower, with a speed of 12 nautical miles per hour. The cabins are divided into ten first-class dining rooms, seven second-class dining rooms, sixteen official cabins, and third-class and steerage cabins can accommodate 1,000 passengers. The overall layout and painting of the ship are very beautiful and it is the most excellent ship in the Sanbei Company's fleet.

Generals of the Righteous Army in Shanghai Jointly Appeal to All Circles

Patriotic Heroes Fight Bitterly in the Black Mountains and White Waters

In the Icy and Snowy Lands, They All Become Gaunt and Wretched

The Far East News Agency reports that Zhou Tiehua, commander of the 4th Detachment of the 9th Route of the Northeast Righteous Army, arrived in Shanghai in December of last year via Rehe to report on the fighting situation of his unit over the past two years and request assistance from all circles. After a month of futile appeals, the iron-blooded warriors on the front lines, huddling in the icy and snowy lands, have all become wretched and gaunt, and their miserable plight is indescribable. Therefore, representatives of various units and generals in Shanghai jointly sent a letter to Song Qingling, Song Ziwen, Kong Xiangxi, Xu Shiying, Zhu Ziqiao, Wang Xiaolai, Du Yuesheng, Huang Jinrong, Jian Zhaojie, and other celebrities, requesting relief. The original letter is recorded below: "Dear Sirs, Since 1918, Tiehua and others have either led our country's heroes in bitter battles in the Black Mountains and White Waters, or followed our anti-Japanese generals and shed blood in eastern Rehe and western Liaoning. In the past two years, although we have not been able to defeat the Japanese bandits and return our mountains and rivers, we represent the patriotic spirit of our entire nation, which is recognized by the people of the country. After the signing of the Tanggu Truce, our army's rear support was cut off, but our work continued. Hundreds of thousands of heroes are still struggling in hardship, making a final struggle. Therefore, Tiehua and others risked danger to come south and seek assistance from all circles. Unexpectedly, after arriving in the south, the government did not provide any assistance, and society did not even inquire. Recalling the time when we left the customs, we received generous assistance from heroes at home and abroad. Compared to the past, we have unlimited regrets. Who would have thought that those who resisted Japan in the past are now displaced and in a miserable state beyond description. Tiehua and others have a heart to serve the country, but there is no way to appeal. Therefore, we have been wandering around Shanghai for months, sighing at the roof. Now that the weather is cold and the year is coming to an end, starvation and cold are imminent. All units are in urgent need of reorganization. Therefore, we have no choice but to boldly and tearfully appeal to all circles, requesting you to grant assistance so that we can return north early and continue to kill the enemy, to live up to the earnest hope of the people of the country and fulfill our duty as ordinary people. We cannot express our urgent anticipation. On behalf of Zhou Tiehua, Zhang Zhendong, etc."

Shanghai Chamber of Commerce Cables for Reduction of Coal Freight Rates on the Zhengtai Railway

National Railway Coal Freight Rates Are Uniquely High on the Zhengtai Line

Unequal Treatment for Other Mines as Well

The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce yesterday telegraphed the Nanjing Executive Yuan, the Ministry of Railways, and the Zhengtai Railway Bureau, stating (titles omitted): On the 8th of this month, we received a joint letter from the Pingding County Coal Merchants Association and the Pingding County Coal Mine Affairs Office of Shanxi Province, stating: Shanxi has always been known as a coal-producing area, and Pingding County, where Yangquan coal is produced, is particularly abundant. The entire area is mountainous, and more than 200,000 people, directly and indirectly, rely on coal mining and transportation for their livelihood. This coal production relies solely on the Zhengtai Railway for export, amounting to approximately 700,000 tons annually. The distance from Yangquan to Shijiazhuang is 121 kilometers, with a freight rate of 3.025 yuan per ton, or 0.025 yuan per ton per kilometer. The annual freight revenue accounts for nearly half of the railway's total income. The quality of Yangquan coal is excellent, comparable to Hongay coal produced in French Indochina. In the past, the largest sales area for Yangquan coal was along the Pinghan Railway, south to Shunde and north to Baoding, accounting for more than half of the annual output. The remainder was sold in Tianjin, Shanghai, and other places. Currently, due to rural bankruptcy in the interior, purchasing power is weak, and due to various factors related to national economy and people's livelihood, mines are unable to reduce production, resulting in mountains of stockpiled coal. Although efforts are being made to reduce costs, sales have not improved. We believe that the annual sales of Hongay coal in Shanghai are nearly 400,000 tons. Yangquan coal can compete with and substitute for this Hongay coal, and can recover more than 6 million yuan in concessions annually. However, the extraordinarily high freight rates on the Zhengtai Railway make it difficult to develop external markets, which is contrary to the purpose of promoting domestic coal. Furthermore, all national railways, with the Pingsui Railway being the most difficult, have reduced freight rates on Shanxi coal due to the abundance of coal in northern Shanxi and high freight rates. The export freight rate for Shanxi coal from Kouquan to Fengtai has been reduced from 4.7 yuan per ton to 3.7 yuan per ton. Since its implementation, the number of exported coal has increased dramatically. Recently, the Pinghan Railway has also implemented a 10% reduction in the special export coal freight rate from Shijiazhuang to Fengtai, totaling a 20% reduction, to support the development of domestic coal. The Zhengtai Railway's coal freight rates have always been exceptionally high compared to other railways. The freight rate for Yangquan coal on the same route is several times higher than the freight rates for the Jingxing Zhengfeng mines, which are very close. This violates the principle of decreasing freight rates with increasing distance, and lacks the spirit of cooperation between railways and mines. If this continues, all Yangquan coal mines will inevitably be shut down, affecting national tax revenue, workers' livelihoods, and local security, which is a cause for concern. The recovery of the annual leakage of over 6 million yuan will be merely an illusion. Our association has repeatedly considered that reducing Zhengtai freight rates is a crucial measure to save the nation and the people. In addition to writing to the Zhengtai Railway Bureau and submitting separate reports to the Executive Yuan and the Ministry of Railways and Industry requesting a reduction in freight rates, we hereby earnestly request your association to provide assistance by telegraphing the Executive Yuan and relevant departments to approve the reduction of freight rates to maintain the mining industry and alleviate the difficulties of merchants. We would be deeply grateful. The association checked the survey tables published by the said association. Among all national railways, the freight rates for coal are the lightest in Jinpu and Hunan-Hubei, the heaviest in Pinghan, and Zhengtai is even higher than Pinghan. Most recently, the most unfair thing is that the Zhengtai Railway charges lighter rates for other mines such as Jingxing Zhengfeng, but charges heavier rates solely for Shanxi coal. The ratio of light to heavy is four to one. How could we not be indignant! In the past, the railway had foreign debt relations, and the authority was also inverted, which is not surprising. Now that the railway's debt has been cleared and the management rights have been fully recovered, why should we continue to repeat the same mistakes, harming the only industry lifeline of Shanxi Province? Even if the railway's income is reduced after the reduction of freight rates, the development of mining will increase railway transportation, and the gains and losses will compensate each other. Moreover, the railway's finances are much better than those of the Pingsui Railway. The Pingsui Railway is still able to reduce freight rates for Shanxi coal, but this railway alone maintains existing practices, which is even more difficult to understand. Based on the above circumstances, we should telegraph your office to review and approve, and order the Zhengtai Railway Bureau to reduce the freight rates for Shanxi coal to maintain the mining industry and for public convenience.

It was said that there were disputes at the meeting that day, and some directors left in anger. Some said that the collective deliberation system of the board of directors had changed to a dictatorship of the government. If it were a normal person, who had received such support from the government, how would they inspire their conscience and work hard to repay the favor? But Zhou did not seek anything else, but only saw him placing his cronies in positions. On New Year's Day this year, on the day he took office as president, he first dismissed the clerical staff who were inconvenient for his private plans, using the excuse of streamlining, and dismissed them without following the hospital's six-month dismissal regulations, causing unexpected disputes. Recently, there have been similar hints to professional personnel in medicine and pharmacy. For the sake of reputation and personality, colleagues have had to question him about the matter. Zhou said that all facilities follow the orders of Director Shen. Zhang Hongsheng and His Mother Injured

Neighbor Shen Dagen Also Affected

At 9:00 PM the night before last, a firecracker exploded inside a workshop at 4 Wangjiazhai, Gaochang Temple, Hubei South. Residents in the vicinity were alarmed. Su Patrolman of the Gaochang Temple Police Station of the Second District of the Municipal Public Security Bureau led police officers to investigate. Fan Jinpan, a policeman from the 46th Gang at the scene, reported that the workshop at 4 Wangjiazhai had been careless in making firecrackers, causing the explosives to explode. The owner of the workshop, Zhang Hongsheng, 19 years old, from Taixing, was brought to the station. He confessed that he usually placed the remaining gunpowder outside the door when making firecrackers. At about 8:00 AM today, he accidentally touched the gunpowder and was injured in the corner of his eye and his mother, Zhang, was injured in her right leg. His uncle took them to the Shanghai Hospital for treatment. Su Patrolman sent police officers to investigate the scene, and the front wall of the house was destroyed. Shen Dagen, the son of neighbor Shen Aiyu, was also injured. Su Patrolman sent Zhang Hongsheng to the Second District Headquarters. After a brief interrogation by District Chief Li, Zhang Hongsheng was allowed to be released on bail to handle the matter and await summons.

Compilation of Bank Issuance Reserve Reports

The 43rd Inspection Report on the Issuance Reserve of Zhejiang Industrial Bank states that the issuance of Zhejiang Industrial Bank has always been completely separated from business operations, and the reserve is sufficient. On the 10th of this month, accountant Yan Ouke checked and found that the cash reserve was over 60% and the guarantee reserve was below 40%. The numbers are as follows: total amount of exchange coupons issued was 8,300,008.715 yuan, total amount of reserve funds was 8,300,008.715 yuan. Among them: the bank issued 4,680,087.715 yuan, the reserve fund was 2,865,232.6 yuan in cash, and 1,815,638.9 yuan as guarantee. The number of banknotes claimed by its counter-part was 3,620,000 yuan, the reserve fund was 2,810,000 yuan in cash, and 810,000 yuan as guarantee.

The 210th report on the Issuance Reserve of the Four Banks Shanghai Reserve states that the Four Banks Reserve is jointly established by the Yanye, Jincheng, Zhongnan, and Dalu banks to specifically handle the issuance of Zhongnan Bank banknotes. According to the issuance regulations of the reserve, the issuance of banknotes is fully reserved, with a cash reserve of at least 60% and a guarantee reserve of at most 40%. It is announced once a week, and is checked by the auditors and accountants of the four banks. Here is a record of the 210th announcement of the Shanghai Reserve on January 6, 1934: the amount of banknotes in circulation was 28,193,437 yuan, the total amount of reserve funds was 28,193,437 yuan. Among them, the cash reserve was 21,975,487 yuan, and the guarantee reserve was 6,217,950 yuan.
