Buddhist Laymen's Forest Opens a Loan Fund for the Poor

Brief Regulations and Loan Procedures

The loan office is located at the Lin on Xinmin Road

The Buddhist Laymen's Forest in this city, in response to a letter from a person signing himself as Bao Yin Jushi and donating 8,000 yuan to establish a loan fund for the livelihood of the poor, the Forest's Director Wang Yiting immediately submitted it to the 69th Standing Committee meeting for approval, and it was immediately opened. Li Jinglun Jushi was recommended to draft the regulations, etc. This has been reported in the newspapers. Now that the regulations have been drafted, they are recorded below for the convenience of the poor when applying for loans, so that they know what to follow.

Brief Regulations for the Loan Fund

1. This Forest, in order to implement humanitarianism and assist social undertakings, specifically raises funds to establish a livelihood loan fund.

2. The purpose of this office is to relieve the poor and unemployed masses by lending capital to enable them to engage in business and make a living, thereby avoiding freezing and starvation.

3. The scope of loans from this office is temporarily limited to Zhabei. Borrowers must be introduced by a friend of this Forest. When there are sufficient funds, expansion will be considered.

4. Borrowed capital for livelihood cannot be used for businesses that violate Buddhist compassion or harm morality.

5. The aforementioned poor people who wish to borrow from this office should first fill out the application form and guarantee form prepared by this office and submit them to this office for verification.

6. The guarantee form must be guaranteed by a reputable shop or someone with a reliable job who affixes their seal.

7. If the borrower cannot write, the application form may be filled out by a staff member of this office, but the guarantee form must be filled out and sealed by the guarantor in person.

8. The amount of the loan is in units of five yuan, with a maximum of twenty-five yuan. However, whether or not to grant the loan and the amount to be granted must be determined after this office sends someone to investigate the facts and examine the situation.

9. No interest is charged on the loan, only a one-time handling fee of four percent (i.e., two dimes for a loan of five yuan, four dimes for ten yuan, and so on). This handling fee must be paid in full with the last installment.

10. The repayment dates for the loan are divided into the following three types. If there are special circumstances, with the approval of this office, a one-time repayment may be agreed upon, but it shall not exceed nine months. A. Repayments are made every ten days. B. Repayments are made every half month. C. Repayments are made monthly. The above methods are determined by the borrower and approved by this office. Once determined, they must be fulfilled as agreed and cannot be changed.

11. If the borrower cannot pay the loan installment each time, the guarantor must be responsible for paying it in advance. If there are repeated delays in repayment, the guarantor may be ordered to pay off the borrower's outstanding loan and the handling fee in one lump sum, depending on the circumstances.

12. These brief regulations shall be implemented after being approved by the Board of Directors of this Forest and reported to the Shanghai Municipal Government's Social Affairs Bureau for record.

Instructions for Borrowers

1. Anyone who truly intends to make a living and wants to borrow from this office should first obtain a blank application form and guarantee form from this office, fill them out according to the instructions, and send them to this office. A document receipt will be issued, and the loan date will be noted.

2. After receiving the application form and guarantee form, this office will immediately send someone to investigate whether they are true. The household registration at the Public Security Bureau's household registration office may also be checked to prevent fraud.

3. On the date of the loan, the borrower should bring the document receipt to this office. If this office believes that the loan can be granted, the document receipt will be submitted to the office, and another loan document will be filled out, with the borrower's photo affixed (taken by this office at no charge) to receive the loan. If this office believes that the loan cannot be granted, the guarantee form will be returned with the document receipt.

4. When the borrower receives the loan, they will also receive a repayment schedule, and according to the dates and amounts due, they should return to the office to repay the loan on schedule. The collector and accountant will stamp the repayment schedule as proof. When the total amount of the loan has been repaid, the borrower will return the card to this office and receive back the guarantee form and loan document.

5. The borrower may not borrow again until the loan has been fully repaid. If they wish to borrow again after repayment, they must fill out the application form and guarantee form again.

6. If the repayment schedule is lost, this office must be notified immediately to obtain a new card, but a handling fee of one dime will be charged.

7. If the borrower loses the document receipt or loan document, resulting in fraudulent receipt, the original applicant and the original guarantor shall be responsible, and this office shall not be liable.

Austrian Young Sculptor Travels the World to Shanghai

Regular Exhibition of Personal Works

Press Conference Today

The Greater Shanghai Evening Post reports that Austrian Halben began traveling after the end of the European War when he was just eighteen years old. He first went from Vienna to Paris and entered art school, where he was famous for his sculpture. He then used this skill to travel around the world, and his travel expenses came from the sale of his sculptures. He was able to absorb the spirit and atmosphere of the countries he visited. He came to the East and arrived in Peiping in November of last year, staying for several weeks and trying his best to study its artistic background and indigenous life. His exhibits in Tokyo, etc., were supported by the American Ambassador, the Swedish Minister, the Canadian Minister, etc. He has now arrived in Shanghai and is scheduled to exhibit and sell fifty pieces related to Mexico, Cuba, the United States, Italy, France, Egypt, Palestine, Hawaii, and the South Seas at the Shanghai Art Club on the sixth floor of 453 Xiafei Road from 2 p.m. to 8 p.m. on the 12th and 13th of January, and a press conference is scheduled for 5:30 p.m. on January 11th.

The Receiving and Dispatching Director of the Mobil Oil Company Embezzles More Than 20,000 Yuan

Using Account Funds for Personal Spending

The Huge Amount of Money Completely Spent

Hu Hongyun from Anhui was the receiving and dispatching director at the Mobil Oil Company at 11 Guangdong Road. Between November 7 and December 12, 1929, the Western manager gave him many checks to pay to various merchants. The value of these checks was 20,708.97 yuan. He suddenly had a bad thought and took the money separately and absconded without a trace. The company reported to the General Inspectorate and requested an investigation. It was discovered that Hu was hiding in his home and arrested, but he was not caught. A wanted warrant was signed by the First Special District Court and ordered to be arrested. It has been more than three years since then, and there has been no trace. On the 7th of this month, Chief Detective Pang Jinshan of the General Inspectorate suddenly learned that Hu was hiding at No. 37 Yanqing Lane, Dunjili in the city. He then met with Western Detective Ross and detectives from the Second Branch of the First District Public Security Bureau and went to the address to arrest Hu. He was brought back to the police station the day before yesterday. Under questioning, Hu confessed that he had embezzled the above-mentioned amount. However, he claimed that the money had been completely used up. He used 5,000 yuan to open the Zhongnan Huayang Grocery Store on Chengdu Road, 7,000 yuan was lost in the Liyuan roulette gambling den, 3,000 yuan was lost to dog racing, and 5,000 yuan was sent back to his home in Anhui. There was also 708.97 yuan that was spent in various small amounts. Yesterday morning, Li Zhishan, a lawyer from the criminal court of the First Special Court, explained the case to the court, accusing him of embezzlement under Article 357 of the Criminal Law. Because further investigation was required, he requested a postponement. Judge Feng Shide questioned the defendant and ordered a postponement of the hearing for one week.

A Case of a Prostitute Being Shot by a Guest at Juhua Courtyard

The Defendant and Witnesses Describe the Situation at the Time

Closing Arguments Completed, Sentencing Scheduled for the 15th

Chen Linrong, a native of Ningbo, who is a driver for the Wang family at 634 Xiafei Road in the French Concession, was 42 years old this year. On the afternoon of the 4th of this month, he was invited by his friend Chen Lanfang to play with Lin Jinyuan (i.e., Juxian), a prostitute from Suzhou, in the pavilion on the second floor of the Juhua Courtyard at No. 2 Hongyun Lane, Huagenier Road in the French Concession. At 9 p.m. after dinner, Zhou Hongshan, a Chinese police officer from the British Concession No. 65, had an urgent need to go to the toilet. He took off his pistol and put it on the edge of the pillow on the bed. Chen saw it, took it out of curiosity to play with it, and because the safety was not on, he accidentally pulled the trigger. The bullet shot out and hit Lin, killing her. The French police took Chen to the Second Special District Court for prosecution, interrogation, and investigation. The details have been reported in previous newspapers. Yesterday morning, Xiong Huiping was recommended to hold the trial in the First Criminal Court. The police brought all the witnesses at the scene for questioning. First, Yao Zhaodi, a lawyer from the police, explained the police's investigation. Then, Qian Ziqing, the adoptive father of the victim, stated the circumstances of his adopted daughter Lin Juxian being shot and killed. When Chen Linrong was interrogated, he confessed that he was invited by Chen Lanfang to play that day. He saw the pistol on the bed, and out of curiosity, he picked it up to play with it. He did not expect to accidentally pull the trigger, and the bullet flew out, hitting Lin. He immediately sent her to the hospital with Chen Lanfang and other friends, but she died despite treatment. The facts were unintentional, and he begged for leniency. Then, witness Zhou Hongshan testified that when he went to the toilet, he put his gun on the bed, fearing that someone would touch it, so he pinched one end of the belt in his hand. He did not expect Chen Linrong to take it out to play with it. He immediately stopped him and shouted that there were bullets in the gun and not to move it. At that time, someone else asked if the safety was on. He replied that it was not on. As soon as he finished speaking, he heard a gunshot, causing a great disaster, etc. At the end, after mutual arguments between the lawyer hired by the defendant and the police lawyer, the defendant's lawyer requested that the defendant be allowed to post bail. The court verified the statements and announced the end of the debate, scheduling the sentencing for the 15th. The defendant was allowed to stop the detention with a bail of 600 yuan. If no bail was paid, he would be held in custody pending instructions.

The Fierce Momentum of the Women's Army Leads to a Tragic Fall from a Building

He Jinbao's Life is in Danger

Ding Yuezhen's Methods are Ruthless

Yang Jiong, also known as Yang Yuqin, a native of Yin County, Zhejiang, is 34 years old and works for the Meiya Company. He owns an Austin car. He previously married Ding Lunsheng's daughter Ding Yuezhen, a local woman. Ding currently resides at No. 5 Nanyang Lane, North Zhejiang Road. However, Yang met He Jinbao, the main star of the Quntianfang Yang Lanchun brothel, who is 24 years old, two years ago, and found another golden house to hide her. Ding filed a lawsuit against Yang in the First Special District Court, accusing him of neglecting to provide support and seeking to recover living expenses. The court ordered them to separate, stipulating that Yang should give Ding 40 yuan per month for living expenses and that Ding should not interfere with Yang's actions. At 2:30 p.m. on the 9th, Ding suddenly led her father Ding Lunsheng, younger brother Ding Ziren, and more than ten other men and women in cars to Yang Jiong and his lover He Jinbao's golden house on the third floor of No. 77 Mingde Lane, broke into the house, and launched a punitive expedition, dragging He Jinbao and punching and kicking her. At the same time, they packed the soft and valuable items in the room into a large package, intending to take them outside. However, Ding still refused to stop and continued to beat He. Somehow, He suddenly fell out of the window and fell from the third floor, bleeding profusely and breathing weakly. Seeing that they had caused a disaster, Ding and the others went downstairs one after another and fled out the door. Ding, Ding Lunsheng, and Ding Ziren, the three main perpetrators, were caught by the patrolman in charge of the lane. Yang took He Jinbao to Baolong Hospital on Baker Road for treatment and reported to the French police. Detective Guo Shaorong arrested Ding and the other three defendants. Yesterday morning, the police escorted the defendants to the First Criminal Court of the Second Special District for investigation. Judge Xiong Huicui held the trial. First, Yao Zhaodi, a lawyer from the police, explained the case, saying that the police had not yet investigated the case and that the victim He Jinbao was still recovering in the hospital. He requested a postponement and asked for an investigation after the victim had recovered from her injuries. He temporarily detained the defendants. Then, the plaintiff Yang Jiong stated the process of the defendants gathering people to commit violence. He also said that Ding was actually a concubine of a businessman and not his legal wife. The First Special District Court ruled for separation. He did not know how she suddenly came to make trouble unreasonably and pushed the businessman's concubine He Jinbao out of the window, causing her to fall and be seriously injured, and there was a risk of death. When he spoke, he thought of the tragic situation and burst into tears. The court stopped him before he stopped. When Ding Yuezhen was interrogated, she confessed that Yang Jiong was indeed her husband. After he abandoned her and her daughter, they sued in the First Special Court and reached a settlement, with 60 yuan per month given to the woman for living expenses, which was later reduced to 40 yuan. However, he had not paid a penny for several months recently. Not only did he ignore her when she asked for it, but he also went to the woman's place on the morning of the 7th and falsely accused her of having an affair with someone, slapping her twice and leaving. The woman was angry and went to argue with him alone. She did not dare to gather people to commit violence. Ding Lunsheng and Ding Ziren, father and son, confessed together that Ding Yuezhen first went to tell them about the situation, and they rushed over after hearing about it. They did not commit any violence. The court verified the confessions and ordered the defendants to be held in custody and the hearing to be continued on the 19th.

Shao Lizi and His Wife Raise Funds for the Xijing Midwifery School

Since their arrival in Shaanxi, Chairman Shao Lizi of Shaanxi Province and his wife, Ms. Fu Xuewen, have diligently sought to understand the people's hardships. They learned that the mortality rate of women and children was higher than that of men due to poor midwifery. Therefore, they used their personal funds to establish the Xijing Midwifery School, which has already opened. However, due to a lack of funding, its long-term sustainability is uncertain. They have published a donation appeal to solicit donations from philanthropists. The appeal states that Shaanxi has suffered from frequent disasters in recent years, leading to a sharp decline in population. There are many ways to seek relief, but the promotion and implementation of midwifery education are particularly urgent. It is observed that in folk customs, when childbirth occurs, ignorant old women are often employed to undertake the important task of delivery. These old women lack basic physiological knowledge, let alone midwifery skills. As for disinfection and prevention, etc., they are beyond their wildest dreams. In cases of difficult labor, they recklessly use barbaric procedures. If successful, they demand credit and reward. If unsuccessful, they attribute it to fate, causing widespread harm and treating human life as mere grass. The situation is too tragic to describe. A small number of wealthy families who are aware of the drawbacks seek help from hospitals, but even they often refuse to be examined by male doctors, causing delays in treatment. As for the general populace, they have no choice but to follow the customs and entrust the lives of mothers and children to the hands of ignorant old women. This is a major scourge on humanity and a hidden danger for the nation. Having recognized this, we have initiated the Xijing Midwifery School, which specifically recruits female students from various counties and teaches them midwifery knowledge. The aim is to spread this knowledge throughout the province in the future, pass it on from generation to generation, protect the lives of mothers and infants, reduce the panic surrounding population problems, and provide some relief for women's employment. However, establishing the school is only the first step. It is even more important to maintain it in the long run. To ensure its long-term sustainability, raising funds is essential to strengthen its foundation. We have limited resources and are making this appeal in the hope that benevolent people at home and abroad will act courageously, generously donate, and help us achieve this goal. We sincerely express our gratitude on behalf of the millions of people in Guanzhong for their future lives and hope for your kind consideration.

Notice on Vehicle Tax Collection in the City Area

Spring Tax Payment Deadline

January 20th

In this city, it is stipulated that motor vehicles must obtain new vehicle licenses from the Public Works Bureau in the spring, and then pay vehicle tax to the Finance Bureau with the new license. Recently, the renewal of licenses and tax payment have been very active. However, because it involves two procedures, it takes a little longer than other seasons. To avoid congestion for taxpayers, the Finance Bureau has temporarily added staff to assist in tax collection to speed up the process. Moreover, the office is open as usual on Saturday and Sunday afternoons, which is very convenient for taxpayers. It is also reported that due to the three-day New Year holiday in the spring, the deadline for tax payment has been extended to January 20th. Starting from the 21st, vehicle licenses will be inspected to prevent tax evasion.

Method for Calculating Freight Transport per Ton

Calculate the Total Amount First, Then Round to the Cent Place

The Ministry of Railways issued a directive to the Railway Bureau yesterday, stating that according to the Third Congress Proposal A36 of the Unified Railway Accounting and Statistics Committee, the freight rate per ton for passenger and freight transport on each route should be calculated to the cent place or a certain decimal point below the cent place. It seems appropriate to clearly stipulate this to standardize the process. The second meeting decided to first calculate the total amount according to the original price. The bureau has instructed the Transportation Department to comply accordingly.

The 20th Anniversary Memorial Service for Xia Ruifang, Founder of the Commercial Press

Held Yesterday Morning at the Cemetery on Shuidaian Road

Xia Ruifang, the founder of the Commercial Press, was a native of Qingpu, Jiangsu. He was murdered on January 10th of the third year of the Republic of China at the age of 43. Yesterday was the 20th anniversary of Xia's death. His son, Xia Xiaofang (the current manager of the Commercial Press), held a 20th-anniversary memorial service at the cemetery on Shuidaian Road to express his condolences. The entire family, children, and more than twenty old employees of the Commercial Press from 20 years ago, including Wei Fuqing, Shi Jiuyun, Huang Jingwan, Li Fuchen, Xie Binlai, and Zhao Lianchen, attended to offer flowers and pay their respects. They also recalled the difficulties of Xia's entrepreneurship and the progress after the revival. According to a reporter from the "Shenshi Society," Xia studied at Qingxin Middle School in his youth. Later, he entered Tongren Hospital, but he did not succeed in studying medicine. He then went to the Dahui News Agency to learn typesetting. After accumulating some savings, he and his colleagues Gao Hanqing, Bao Xianchang, and others raised a capital of 4,700 yuan to establish the Commercial Press on Beijing Road. At that time, the building was only one floor. The first English textbook published was "Hua Ying Chu Jie" (Chinese-English Primer), and the first textbook was "Latest National Language Textbook." Today, the business has developed into the only organization in China that promotes culture and enjoys a worldwide reputation. Remembering Xia's spirit of hard work and outstanding achievements, he is truly worthy of admiration.

Cold Weather in This City

Since the beginning of winter, the weather in this city has been very mild. The Fahrenheit thermometer has often been between 50 and 60 degrees. Therefore, pedestrians on the road have found cotton clothes to be too warm, and most wear lined jackets and velvet long gowns. After a slight snowfall the day before yesterday (the evening of the 7th), the weather remained as warm as before. Unexpectedly, from 1:00 PM yesterday, the northwest wind howled, and the weather suddenly became bitterly cold. After nightfall, the temperature dropped below zero, and ice formed under the water boards of the stoves.

World-Renowned Anatomist Visits the Children's Dental Hospital

Professor Dr. Julius Tandler, a world-renowned anatomy expert from the University of Vienna, has been invited by the Medical School of Central University to lecture in China. Dr. Tandler is an expert in anatomy and is known throughout the world. Whenever he gives a lecture, audiences of four to five thousand people come uninvited. His admiration in the scientific community can be imagined. This invitation from Central University is truly a rare event. He recently passed through Shanghai and heard that the Family Industrial Society had newly established a Children's Dental Hospital, and that all the equipment was a model for China. He specifically asked Mr. Zhou Shangjun of the Education Bureau to introduce him. Yesterday, he personally visited the hospital on Nanjing Road. Dr. Gu Hailing, the director of the hospital, received and showed him around. Letters

Discounting Drafts and Freight Transport by Zheng, Bao, Zhao

｜A Great Opportunity for Cooperation Between Banks and Railways｜

The purpose of railways in handling freight business is to circulate goods and help the development of the social economy. Most of our country's railways are state-owned and state-operated. The freight business should especially be based on serving society. Compared to passenger transport, which should facilitate travel, the mission is even more important. Because a country's wealth, strength, and weakness are often based on the rise and fall of agriculture, industry, and commerce, and the capital for the turnover and circulation of agriculture, industry, and commerce is goods. Therefore, inconvenient freight transport is the main reason for the inability to develop agriculture, industry, and commerce. If agriculture, industry, and commerce do not develop, the country cannot become rich and strong. Looking at the cheap, fast, and prosperous railway freight transport in various countries in the East and West, it is enough to know the source of their wealth and strength. Its great mission cannot be regarded as trivial.

The operation of state-owned railways and its business is not aimed at seeking profits. Therefore, all kinds of businesses that can facilitate society, with very thin profits or even no profits, should also be given priority. In the past, although our country's railways were state-owned, they mostly ignored the end of serving society. Therefore, they often failed to penetrate into the people and seek convenience for the masses. Taking freight transport as an example, merchants often felt inconvenience and suffered greatly. Therefore, intermediaries emerged in response to the situation. People were willing to pay unnecessary prices in order to obtain a deserved convenience. The reason for this is that railways did not have a correct concept of business policy, believing that railway transportation is mostly monopolistic in nature. No matter how inconvenient or expensive it is, merchants must have no other way to go. All the places that can facilitate society are considered superfluous and have nothing to do with the business of railways. How can they know that the purpose of railway business is not only to seek their own interests?

Now, the railway authorities, in view of the errors in the past business policy, are eager to penetrate into society, seek happiness for merchants, seek convenience, lighten burdens, and do not take their own interests as a prerequisite, but take the interests of society as the basis. Recently, various routes have created railway business offices to handle all passenger and freight transportation procedures on behalf of customers. The intention is here. The business office is purely a service organization run by the railway itself, and it is also the external representative of the railway business. All services are based on the purpose of serving society, and it is not the responsibility of seeking profits. It can also penetrate into agriculture, industry, and commerce to solve all transportation problems for merchants, eliminate their pain, and reduce their burdens, sweeping away the bad habits of closing the door for business, being arrogant and self-respecting. This is the latest innovation in railway business.

As far as consignment is concerned, the railway business office can already pick up and deliver goods on behalf of customers, handle all freight transportation procedures, answer questions from all walks of life about freight rates at any time, and do its best to solve various freight transportation difficulties for customers within its ability. Society calls it convenient, and the effect has been achieved. However, the railway handles freight transport with the aim of circulating goods, as has been said above. The method of circulating goods, in addition to transportation convenience, still depends on the flexibility of transportation finance. Because the goods are transported from A to B, it is the formation of buying and selling transactions. The result of the transaction is the liquidation of the price of the goods. There are various methods for liquidating the price of the goods: (1) The buyer carries cash to purchase. (2) The buyer carries a bill to discount for purchase. (3) The seller remits the money in advance before the transaction is completed. (4) The seller only reconciles after the transaction is completed. All of this requires paying the money first and then purchasing the goods, or delivering the goods first and then receiving the money, which is inconvenient for the buyer or unfavorable to the seller. Only the method of discounting drafts can take care of both parties and benefit them. Even if the buyer and seller do not know each other, they can complete their transaction by means of discounting drafts. This is a good method for flexible transport finance. If the railway wants to fulfill its mission of circulating goods and helping the development of the social economy, it must not only facilitate transport, but also assist in the flexibility of transport finance. Otherwise, the development of many freight transports will be impossible because of this.

Now that the railway has established business offices to be the vanguard of serving society, in the future, if it wants to be able to do its best to serve society in terms of freight transport, it must handle discounting drafts to regulate transport finance. Although discounting drafts is one of the important businesses of banks, if the railway business office wants to engage in discounting drafts, it still needs the assistance of the banking industry before it can develop. Therefore, the purpose of the banking business is also to serve society and facilitate the people, which is exactly the same as the railway. Bankers should also have the perseverance and crude spirit to penetrate society and make real investments before they can achieve the goal of helping production. We say that the discounting drafts is a great opportunity for cooperation between banks and railways. The railway has a business office to handle all freight transport procedures, and can directly handle discounting drafts with the bank to meet the needs of agriculture, industry, and commerce. The method is very simple, that is, whenever a customer entrusts the railway business office to transport the

goods, if discounting drafts is required, the business office will open a bill of lading to the freight station, (the bill of lading is different from the freight receipt, the former can be transferred and can be discounted, the latter cannot be transferred or discounted according to the regulations,) the name of the discounting bank is filled in the consignee column of the bill of lading, the bill of lading is transferred to the bank handling discounting drafts, the discounted money is obtained, and transferred to the consignor. The method is simple and the effect is great. It is truly a new business that banks and railways should handle.

The railway has made efforts to penetrate into social services and not seek its own interests as an effort to reform. We hope that the banking industry will also adopt this spirit and quickly cooperate with the railway to seek common prosperity. The way of cooperation can start from the above-mentioned discounting drafts method. We ask the gentlemen in the financial industry, what do you think?

Letter

Dear Sir, On the 10th of this month, I saw a news item in your newspaper's local news column about our company's construction of a tramway track. It stated that the electricity business in the 22nd year was quite developed and that it was estimated that a surplus of more than one million yuan could be obtained. I was extremely surprised to read this. After checking, although the electricity business of our company in the 22nd year was better compared to the 21st year, the expenses also increased a lot compared to the previous year. How could there be such a large surplus? I am afraid that outsiders will not be aware of this and will easily be misled. Therefore, I am specifically sending this letter to your editor for verification and request that this letter be published in the letter column to correct the misinformation and avoid its spread. I would be very grateful. Sincerely, The Chief Editor of the Shenbao Editorial Department, Huashang Electric Company, 231.10.

Reading Q&A

What We Need

"Reading Guidance" (1)

Reading Guidance:

I am very happy that there is a "Reading Guidance" creation in the Chinese Library. This is indeed a very educational thing. Your success will definitely exceed school education. Because not everyone gathered in a school is interested in studying, but those who flock around you are for their own interests and needs, a large group of people starving for knowledge who need nourishment, and they do not need to be forced.

I am very satisfied with the "Reading Q&A" of the past two days. Although the discussion is still about general issues, it is still very needed. Now I will put forward a more practical working question under your guidance.

I don't think your guidance should be exclusively for books, and especially should not teach people to simply read books. Because I think that those who are currently receiving your guidance are probably struggling to make a living while trying to learn something to cope with the needs of actual life. If you, based on your subjective views, offer them a grand list of books, write a few large volumes of someone's self-study introduction, and talk about the evolution and system of academics, it is really irrelevant to everyone. At most, it is just like Hu Shi, Liang Qichao, and others offering a list of Chinese studies books to students. These delicacies are only intimidating and deceiving, not "non-

refugee" food.

I mean, the center of your guidance should pay attention to the current practical life of readers, and give practical instructions and assistance to solve the difficulties that occur in various daily lives. Because this is the goal, guiding reading becomes a means. Therefore, I think that your work simply should not or does not need to be done grandly and impressively, but should be done calmly, practically, silently, and inconspicuously. What you should always pay attention to is life guidance, not cramming knowledge, or classical sermons in church. Therefore, the books you recommend do not need to be systematic or talk about evolution, as long as they can be used for reference to solve a certain problem. The simplicity and lack of system of the book list can be ignored. Do not regard books as sacred, and do not regard reading as a great undertaking. You yourself do not need to become scholars in the study. This is what I hope. If you can do this, your work will not be in vain, everyone will need you, and naturally this is a great project.

Precisely because of this, the difficulties in the future are probably much more difficult than running a university. However, reading your plan carefully, it has a tendency to coincide with my humble opinion. Therefore, I cherish it very much and cannot help but say it. I hope you will pay more attention and show everyone your work direction more concretely, so that everyone can thoroughly understand it, so that they can supervise each other and make this unprecedented undertaking more practical.

Do not block everyone's opinions, but sincerely absorb the true shadow of each social level of life. Have the determination and care of a scientist to dissect it, the faith of a religious person to seek to change this bad sin and animality, and at the same time, the courtesy, patience, and needs of an elementary school teacher to interact with the people who need you.

Your success and failure lie in your understanding of the depth of everyone; whether you get the support of sympathetic people and the cooperation of all readers. My direct suggestion is for your reference only. Finally, I hope that this issue will also be made public in the "Reading Q&A" to arouse everyone's research.

Telephone Bureau Expands Wusong Lines

Longhua Automatic Machine Conversion Can Be Completed in April

Increased Telephone Calls in Chinese Concession Will Expand Switchboard

The Shanghai Telephone Bureau of the Ministry of Communications has decided to expand the Wusong lines due to insufficient application. As for the conversion of Longhua's automatic machine, the expansion of the No. 0 switchboard, and the removal of cross-border phones, it will be completed in the summer of this year. The leased telephone company will add a No. 04 manual exchange, which is scheduled to be completed on February 10th. The details are as follows:

Wusong Increase Lines

There are 33 telephone users in Wusong. All telephones are directly under the jurisdiction of the Jiangwan Telephone Branch. Because the city situation in the district is not prosperous, the telephone bureau only laid three lines from Wusong to the Jiangwan branch. In theory, three lines are enough for the application of more than 30 households. However, because it needs to be transferred, there are often delays. All sectors of the area have repeatedly requested to re-equip and increase the lines. For the convenience of users, the telephone bureau decided to expand two lines, which can be completed in mid-February.

Longhua Exchange Machine

In Longhua, the market is becoming more prosperous day by day, and the number of telephone users is also increasing day by day. The Longhua Telephone Bureau originally had a branch office. All the phones were switchboards and were old. Therefore, the telephone bureau had discussed the conversion of automatic machines and submitted it to the Ministry of Communications for review. The Ministry has approved it and ordered the material purchase committee to order new automatic machines from the United States. It will arrive in Shanghai in March, and it will be supplied to users in the Longhua area. The disassembly and installation can be completed in mid-April.

Pudong Rent

As for the telephone in Pudong, since the establishment of a telephone branch by the Shanghai Telephone Bureau on November 30 last year in accordance with the telephone temporary contract and the telephone company's negotiation, and the transfer of management by the telephone bureau, the prices have been stipulated. The monthly rent for each residential unit is ten yuan, and the monthly rent for each business is fifteen yuan. The residents of the area found that the telephone rental fees in the Jiangwan, Nanshi, Zhabei, Zhenru, and Longhua telephone bureaus were seven yuan and ten yuan. Pudong is also in the urban area, but the price is expensive, so they requested a reduction. The telephone bureau took into account that the telephone company's charges for installing cross-border machines were almost twice as high as those in the leased area due to the submarine cable. It had requested instructions from the Ministry of Communications, and the Ministry advocated that the current price should still be collected.

Expand Number Zero

The Telephone Bureau's "Number Zero" switchboard has been increased more than doubled by users in each district who call to the leased area since the cancellation of the five-cent telephone fee in the Chinese Concession at the end of August last year. Especially between 12:00 noon and 2:00 pm, calls to the leased area are even busier, and there is almost no time to answer them. For this reason, the Telephone Bureau specifically approved the Ministry of Communications to ask the Material Purchase Committee to order the machine parts of the switchboard from the United States in order to expand the Number Zero switchboard for telephone calls in the Chinese Concession. Now the goods will arrive in Shanghai in May, and the Number Zero switchboard can be expanded in mid-June.

Dismantle Cross-Border Machines

After dismantling 30 of the 288 cross-border phones installed by the Shanghai Telephone Company in various parts of the Chinese Concession since September last year, the Telephone Bureau had to wait for the expansion before it could completely dismantle them due to insufficient machine parts. The Shanghai Telephone Company found that the No. 02 manual switchboard for calls to the Chinese Concession was very busy, so it decided to open a "No. 04" manual switchboard specifically for renting calls to Pudong (because most Pudong telephones call the leased area). Construction has now started and is expected to be completed on February 10th and can be applied on the 20th. After the establishment of this station, the Pudong cross-border machine will be transferred to the Telephone Bureau for processing. The cross-border machines in various places must be transferred to the Telephone Bureau after the "Zero" station is expanded. The time is around the end of June.

Shenbao National Goods Weekly

Contribution Speech

The Required Work of Women's National Products Year

— Yang Yao

This year has already been officially designated as Women's National Products Year. For women, it is naturally an unshirkable duty, and for men, it is necessary to work together to promote its success. It is essential not to think, "This year's promotion of national products can be left to the women to handle." Therefore, an organized Women's National Products Year Work Plan Committee was established to handle the planning. As a reporter, I was also pushed as part of the plan. Thus, I boldly present my personal thoughts here for the reference of enthusiastic individuals.

㈠ The principals and teachers of all girls' schools should lead their students in national products movements, starting from the school, then the family, and then society. Using speeches, talks, visits, and persuasive methods, they should proceed separately, ensuring that families and society across the country are consistently using domestic goods. If anyone in the school uses foreign goods or Japanese goods, classmates should report them and publicly display it throughout the school as a great disgrace.

㈡ Female university students are the leaders of the women's world nationwide. Starting this year, everyone should unite to serve national products and advocate for them throughout the country. Eradicate the previous habit of loving foreign goods and extravagance. Everyone should have the ambition to "transform the atmosphere; if not me, then who?"

㈢ Various women's groups, such as the Young Women's Christian Association, Women's Temperance Union, Family Renewal Association, Women's National Products Promotion Association, and women's associations, should unite to form a Women's National Products Year Committee. They should hold women's forums, social gatherings, and festive events at any time, and plan the work to be done during the Women's National Products Year.

㈣ All national products groups and national products companies should receive local women at any time, hold tea parties, social gatherings, etc., to exchange opinions with each other, so that the women's world has a deeper understanding of national products and a more sincere belief in them.

㈤ All national products companies, factories, and shops, on their storefront signs, covers, invoices, advertisements, leaflets, and gift certificates, can add the words "Women's National Products Year" so that customers always keep it in mind and never forget it.

㈥ All national products groups and national products companies should hold mobile national products exhibitions, rotating to various universities and girls' schools to display their products and provide explanations to attract the attention of students.

㈦ All theaters and cinemas should screen films promoting national products movements before the show begins and write prominently on the screen "Women's National Products Year, please women's circles to consistently use national products".

㈧ All national products companies, factories, and major newspapers should hold Women's National Products Year essay and speech contests to encourage women and female students to focus their energy, thought, and attention on national products issues.

㈨ All silk companies, woolen companies, national cloth companies, etc., should hold women's clothing or children's clothing conventions at any time to encourage women and children's interest in using national fabric materials.

㈩ On Children's Day this year, all national products companies should hold mothers' meetings, inviting mothers to lead their children to visit and talk, or use gift drawing methods to add interest.

㈩㈠ All national products companies and national products groups should collect domestic goods for household and women's use, classify them, and publish small booklets to facilitate housewives' choices.

㈩㈡ All broadcasting stations, regardless of the program, should insert Women's National Products Year information to make it known to every household and have a greater effect.

The above-mentioned is just my humble opinion; there is much other work that needs to be done. "Good government lies not in many words, but in earnest action." I hope that women's circles across the country will use a spirit of hard work, perseverance, and practicality to consistently implement this work to complete the significant mission of this year.

National Products Talk

Prospects for "Women's National Products Year"

— Xiao Bai

Since the curtain of "Women's National Products Year" was unveiled, the call for "Women's National Products" can be said to have permeated the country. Although we have not yet seen how they are actually implementing it and what results they are achieving, in the face of the influx of foreign goods and the soaring trade deficit, it is naturally something for the whole country to celebrate that our national products future can have such enthusiastic advocacy.

Originally, the establishment of a country is based on individuals and families, from families to society, and from society to the nation. Of course, his prosperity and decline depends on the quality of the national economy. In the past, my country | was shrouded in the evil atmosphere of imperialism, the market situation naturally only presented darkness and disorder. The tide of foreign goods dumping and increasing trade deficit was rampant day by day, and the storm of rural bankruptcy and market depression swept the country. However, under this severe lesson, our national products industry has been able to rise roughly in recent years. However, the influx of foreign goods remains, and the adoption of foreign goods by Chinese people also remains. The great National Products Year finally failed to wash away the disgrace of a new record of 900 million yuan in trade deficit but urgently needs and waits for the continued efforts of the "Women's National Products Year" to achieve his ambitions, which is really pitiful and ridiculous.

The fact is very clear: in the past, Chinese women, especially the so-called modern girls in cities, ignored national products and were happy to promote foreign goods, which are undeniable facts. Last year, the import of cosmetics to Shanghai alone was reportedly 600,000 yuan. A large amount of money is flowing out. Since women are housewives and in charge of household affairs, they have such outrageous behavior. It is no wonder that the national products industry’s promotion and advocacy, running around and working hard, are all counterproductive and rarely achieve results. It is urgently necessary for our "womenfolk to do it" in the hope of better results.

The year has been renewed, and the climax of my "Women's National Products" is also beginning to surge at the same time. From now on, the women's circles of the entire country will also follow this new year, realize the mistakes of the past, work hard for the future, and unite and stand on the same line. Starting this year, set an example, use national products, no matter a thread or a thread, only buy domestic goods, revealing a ray of light from the dull air, and strive to eliminate foreign goods, permanently block loopholes, and revive the countryside.

Society can be stable, creating unprecedented feats in the women's world and completing the most important mission of this year.

Welcoming "Women's National Products Year"

— Xuan Wan

Amidst the surrounding groans and cries, our solemn and great National Products Year has passed away leisurely and ordinarily, just like in previous years. However, the brand-new and beautiful Women's National Products Year, which has been named by all circles and approved by the government, has already arrived slowly. As people bid farewell to the old and welcome the new, looking back on the past and looking forward to the future, they naturally have a new ambition, new hope, and something to pray for regarding this new year.

The National Products Year of the 22nd year | in the past year, our entire country can be said to be in a state of darkness. Outside, strong neighbors are pressing the border, and the loss of land is increasing day by day. Inside, the countryside is bankrupt, and the social economy is collapsing. The most painful thing is that the new record of 900 million yuan in trade deficit is still reflected in my great National Products Year. Looking at various places in the country, foreign goods are rampant, especially the activities of enemy goods, even resorting to despicable behaviors and dirty methods, colluding with unscrupulous merchants, and dumping goods wantonly, inducing my people with weak purchasing power to get hooked and be exploited again. This situation is the greatest obstacle to the future of my national products and urgently needs to be eradicated fundamentally and prevent it from spreading and expanding day by day.

Although, the past is not worth regretting, we only need to hope for the future. The National Products Year cannot completely block the loopholes in foreign goods imports, but, in this year, the people in my national products industry have been running around and working hard, promoting and advocating, and have indeed created many glorious achievements. The most notable ones are the establishment of the China National Products Company, the establishment of the National Products Introduction Office and its branches in various places, and the establishment of various national products gatherings, which have made the national products production and sales mechanism universal throughout the country. Indeed, all of these are the dawn of the future of my national products and the beginning of industrial revitalization, which is enough to make us excited, enthusiastic, and self-motivated, and strive to continue and complete the tasks of the end of last year this year.

The naming of this year has been determined | The meaning and origin of "Women's National Products Year" must have been known to my people. As Mr. Yang Yao said: "Who controls the vitality of national products? The power lies entirely in the hands of women." Starting this year, my housewives who are in charge of household affairs can truly promote national products, be happy to use them, and no longer be salespeople for foreign goods. Then, this year will surely have better results and achieve the final victory.

At this time, in the midst of the noisy and lively sound of gongs and drums, the women's circles of the entire country do not want to be blurred by colorful New Year cards, but have a clear understanding of this year, and it will be seen that foreign goods will disappear, loopholes will be permanently blocked, and a different color will be released for the future of national products. This is the only hope for my people today.

Contribution Words Before Famous Actors Take the Stage

— Lu Boyu

From the National Products Year last year to the Women's National Products Year this year, the national products movement is gradually becoming more acute. This cannot but be said to be a good phenomenon for the future of my country's industry. Taking theater as an example, last year's National Products Year was a well-done "Tiao Jia Guan" or "Havoc in the Theatre." This year is the main play. The Women's National Products Year, of course, takes women as the main characters. The roles of male, female, painted face, clown, and supporting actor are almost entirely played by women. The responsibility of men is to play supporting roles, waving flags and shouting to boost the momentum. It is certainly not good if the supporting actors' steps are wrong, but if the singing and acting skills of the main characters are inappropriate or uneasy, or even out of tune, the audience under the stage may boo!

We are all people in the play, and at the same time, we are all audience members. Last year, we performed a national products play for a year. Although the results were not very satisfactory, they were generally still satisfactory. Unfortunately, at the end of the year, a message suddenly came that the import of cosmetics amounted to 1.4 million yuan in ten months. This is like the actors in the theater are performing happily, and suddenly a large number of female viewers leave their seats. It is really a big disappointment. The opening play in the past is no longer discussed. This year, we start all over again. The famous actors invited this year have always been appealing. We hope that after this large group of famous actors take the stage, they will work tirelessly to make the audience under the stage applaud repeatedly, and make the "sold out" sign hang early at the entrance of the theater, and make the theater next door deserted and sparsely populated. This will not only satisfy the audience and make the boss happy, but also make the stagehands and tea servers in the theater very grateful to these famous actors, so that they can get more tips. As for the actors, if they always work hard, they can certainly get many cheers on the spot, and then they will become famous, so that the general public will recognize the abilities of these famous actors, increase the status of these famous actors in the art world, and at the same time, they will not disappoint the hard work of the theater owners who have spent a lot of advertising fees on promotion.

National Products Discussion

Promoting National Products and Improving Customs

— Li Anfu

The strength or weakness of a country is not limited to one aspect, but in this era when the economy can control everything, only the economy is omnipotent; even politics must be based on economic strength to determine its direction. Therefore, it is really a blessing for a country to not allow its money to flow out as much as possible within its capabilities, and to make the country feel an economic panic. (Naturally, it is different from the capital export of imperialism.) But looking back at China, the construction of all heavy industries must rely on foreign countries. Even the manufactured products of light industries, as well as cosmetics, etc., mostly use foreign goods and consider it an honor. Therefore, in the National Products Year of the 22nd year, not only did the sales rate of anti-national products not increase as much as possible, but the foreign goods of other countries took this opportunity to impersonate national products and dumped them heavily. The future of the national products industry has fallen further and further. Tracing back to its origin, of course, it is because national products are unable to sell well.

Therefore, the first step we should study is how to make national products sell well? Naturally, advertisements in newspapers, shouting slogans, and posters on walls only create an atmosphere of promoting national products. In reality, its effect is still very small. Therefore, we have to make further inspections and discussions. Observing from the perspective of various countries, only by reforming these bad customs and human hearts can there be a remedy; because promoting national products as a formality really does not have much effect. If the power of the country is used to force people to adopt national products, it is indeed difficult to implement in reality. Therefore, we have to use these customs and habits to improve them. In the past history, there are many such examples. Even judging from what we see now, Japan is a good example. Although Japanese women wear colorful clothes and dress up gorgeously, what they use and wear are all their own national products. Japanese students also take pride in wearing national uniforms. Other daily necessities, etc., are not bought unless they are domestic products. I remember once, a friend told me that the Japanese living in Shanghai even brought their soy sauce from Japan. From this very small place, we can see how strong the patriotism of the Japanese is! The people of Germany also love to use domestic goods no less than Japan. This is also a major reason why their country can be strong.

This year is the "Women's National Products Year". The promoters really spent a lot of psychological speculation before deciding on this name, but it is difficult to say whether it will be effective; because women's psychology is mostly fond of vanity and luxury. As long as the things she chooses are beautiful and attractive, she often takes out money to buy them, regardless of whether they are domestic or foreign goods; and women with relatively lower intelligence? They often lack the ability to choose for themselves, and only know how to imitate others. They buy whatever they see others buy; moreover, the household utensils and items used by the husband are mostly handled by women, except for special items. Therefore, once this trend starts, there will be no day to promote national products. If we can change this bad habit and make up our minds not to buy anything other than national products, then it is naturally not difficult to reform this trend. Moreover, the so-called fashionable and modern are also aimless and follow the trend. If it is considered fashionable to use national products at home, then who would use foreign goods? Moreover, promoting national products only requires changing the purpose of shopping, and it is not a difficult thing. If the facts can really match the ideals, then national products will be promoted without promotion, and foreign goods will be excluded without exclusion. At that time, part of the money will not flow out.

In conclusion, to promote national products, we must start with female compatriots, and women should especially reform this luxurious custom first; then create a good custom, so that good results can be produced. I hope that female compatriots do not think that this is an ordinary thing | and falsely live up to the good name of this "Women's National Products Year."

Women's National Products Year

— Xin Xin

This year is "Women's National Products Year," and now is the beginning of "Women's National Products Year." Recently, among the products imported from Japan, the most prominent are miscellaneous goods, and among miscellaneous goods, mirrors are the most numerous. Every time a ship arrives, there are always 30 to 40 boxes, or even more than 50 boxes. The cargo ships that arrived this month totaled more than 300 boxes. Women's Contribution

Opinions on the Women's National Products Year

— Nie Huiji Fen

For more than ten years, we've been chanting slogans of resistance and promoting domestic goods every year, but imports of foreign goods have been increasing year by year, which is quite comical. In the past two years, the Japanese bandits have been pressing harder, and resistance has naturally been more vigorous, but the import of Japanese goods has increased sharply, and the trade deficit has reached a staggering 900 million, which is a huge and alarming figure. At the same time, domestic industrial and commercial enterprises are on the verge of collapse, which is even more sad.

If we do not deeply think about this contradictory situation and understand its causes, then why should we join this comical play and provide outsiders with a chance to laugh at us?

I believe that promoting domestic goods is not only about promoting domestic goods, but also about correcting people's improper concepts. Concepts are the root of desires. We must take seeking the interests of the people as our due obligation, so that we can sacrifice our personal desires for beauty and luxury. Only then can domestic goods develop without promotion. If today's society admires European and American customs, pursues material enjoyment, advocates fashion and beauty, and only cares about convenience and comfort, then it will definitely not be able to take into account the interests of the country and the people. The root of the contradictory phenomenon today lies here, and there is no other reason.

Promoting domestic goods should not be based on resisting enemy goods, but for the sake of national and personal survival. It must be like this. People with shallow knowledge do not understand this meaning, thinking that my purchase of a small amount of foreign goods will not affect the country, especially my personal survival? They do not know that when the people are poor and the wealth is exhausted, war and chaos are inevitable. At that time, there is no need to kill or set fires. Simply due to lack of food and inability to live, the old, the young, the weak, and the sick will naturally be poor, frozen, and starved to death.

Today, there are hundreds of thousands of unemployed people in various parts of our country, and millions or even tens of millions of unemployed people in European and American countries. This is all due to the decline of industry and commerce, which is caused by the declining purchasing power of the world. In short, the world's finances have dried up to the extreme today. Those with shallow knowledge see the superficial prosperity of the commercial market and think that they still have surplus wealth or have the knowledge and skills to support themselves, thinking that this problem will not affect them for the time being. Little do they know that in the past two years, more than 2,000 banks have closed down in the United States, and countless people have gone from rich to poor. People who used to be engineers and earn huge salaries suddenly have to line up at soup kitchens for food. Unemployed people and children often scavenge for food next to garbage bins (Americans are used to wasting food, so they discard things that are still edible). How can this be expected by ordinary people?

The strength of Japan is due to the people's ability to love their country. This is well known. Loving the country is not in slogans and written posters, but in the fact that a few people in higher positions have clear and correct concepts and the practice of hard work, serving as the leaders of the masses. The Japanese can cherish and promote their historically inherited culture and customs, and do not follow the changes of Westerners. For example, sitting on the floor and setting up temporary stalls every night are extremely inconvenient. Wooden clogs, backpacks, and high buns are all inconvenient things, but they can all be preserved. Even wealthy families do not change them. It must be known that Eastern culture mostly takes diligence and frugality as morality, and the merits and demerits of local customs are also judged from this point. What Japan preserves is the good culture of the East. Preserving it encourages diligence and frugality. If it is discarded and imitated by the West, it will tend towards luxury and laziness. Western things are convenient, but those who are used to them will gradually lose their personal abilities. Today, European and American industrial and commercial enterprises have all failed in competition with Japan. There is no other reason than the fact that the efficiency of individuals differs greatly. The development of this high efficiency is due to the ability to preserve the practice of sitting on the floor. Moreover, if Japan admires Western customs, iron beds and wooden furniture would have long exhausted Japan's economic power. Even if they were mostly self-made, they would greatly reduce their export power. How could they obtain foreign money for this amazing construction? Today, their country has achieved this success because of the clear vision and hard work of a few great men who were responsible for social guidance 50 years ago.

The Cosmetic Disturbance

— Qiaoming

The sunlight is weak and powerless, the branches and leaves of the trees turn yellow, the wind is a bit chilly, and autumn is deep!

On this day, a small disturbance suddenly occurred in Mr. Chen's house. The reason was that Mr. Chen bought a bottle of skin care product and handed it to his wife with great satisfaction.

"Did you buy it? How much does a bottle cost?" the wise Mrs. Chen asked.

"One dollar and twenty cents a bottle," Mr. Chen replied.

"A small bottle of something costs one dollar and twenty cents? Too expensive! Too expensive!"

"It's an old foreign brand with excellent quality."

"Are you a worshiper of foreign goods?" Mrs. Chen immediately frowned. She said sternly, "In this era, everyone knows to promote domestic goods, but you want to be a salesman for foreign goods. You know foreign goods are good, but do you know that domestic goods have made rapid progress in recent years? Moreover, applying foreign goods to your face, even if it's beautiful, should be considered ugly. You can abandon the root and pursue the branch, but I can't make a fool of myself!..."

Mr. Chen was speechless by Mrs. Chen.

A few days later, Mr. Chen went to the Wuzhou Pharmacy and bought a large jar of beauty cream in one-pound packaging.

"Look! This is domestic, and it only cost seventy-five cents, which can be used by our whole family for the entire winter," Mrs. Chen said proudly.

Mr. Chen did not speak. He had clearly lost this disturbance!

The Grandeur of Domestic Wire Mesh

The picture on the right shows the magnificent appearance of the mesh fence surrounding the airfield. This kind of mesh fence used to be foreign goods, but in the past two years, the Shanghai Gongqin Iron Factory has produced them, and Chinese people no longer need to seek them from abroad. The picture on the left shows the mesh fence surrounding the airport station. The fence gate has steel pipes as its skeleton and is secured with a specially made lock, making it extremely strong. There is also an electrical current device. In case of emergency, turning on the switch will electrify the entire mesh, and the enemy cannot cross the battery step.

— Xu Luqian

Chinese women all use lead-based powder to apply to their faces when applying makeup, but they don't know that lead is poisonous. Over time, freckles appear on the powder application areas. There are particularly many women affected, which is a major flaw in beauty.

Although domestic products are available, they are not very effective, so Chinese people do not trust them. I have tried it and the effect is extremely good, and I am happy to introduce it.

Family Visit Record

Madam Nie

— Tianran

Madam Nie, named Jifen, is the youngest daughter of Zeng Wenzheng Gong of Xiangxiang. Since she was a child, she loved the teachings of Wenzheng Gong and was influenced by a good education. Therefore, she can write and is literate, possessing the style of Wenji Daoyun, and she is simple and frugal, with ancient morals shining on people, which is beyond the reach of modern women. Her son, Mr. Nie Yuntai, wears coarse cloth and eats vegetables, advocating the "Great Ji" doctrine, instructing young people to earn their own living. Everyone imitates Gandhi, spinning and weaving their own cloth to save the country with cloth. This is the education of the Madam. Her fourth son, Mr. Sheng, manages the Hengfeng Yarn Factory, striving to manufacture domestic yarn and cloth to compete with Japanese yarn. This is also the education of the Madam. We believe in the Madam's morality and knowledge, and especially admire the Madam's family. The Madam's management of her family can be described with the eight words "simple and straightforward, refined and courteous." All the clothes, food, and utensils in the family are all domestic products. Even a cup, a needle, and a box of matches are all domestic products. Entering her door, everything is neat and orderly, without luxury. Her sons, daughters, daughters-in-law, grandsons, and granddaughters all serve the Madam with great respect. The Madam also treats them with courtesy. Even the servants and maids are treated with politeness, without harsh words or angry expressions. At the high age of eighty-two, she looks like she is in her sixties. Her cultivation is evident here. The Madam advocates promoting domestic goods, saying that it is not in slogans and posters, but in the fact that people in leadership positions have clear and correct concepts and the practice of hard work. She greatly admires the Japanese for not easily being swayed by Western customs. Japanese women still keep their high buns, wooden clogs, backpacks, and sitting on the floor, seemingly stubborn, but the money does not flow out, and foreign goods cannot be imported, which is the foundation of Japan's wealth and strength. Chinese people are the opposite. With the productivity of the 19th century, they want to enjoy the material civilization of the 20th century, which is why they have trade deficits year after year and are so poor. The Madam said at this point, unable to hold back her tears, sighing again and again. In the end, she said that today's promotion of domestic goods is not only about promoting domestic goods, but also about correcting people's improper concepts. If everyone can sacrifice their personal desires for beauty, domestic goods will develop without promotion. If everyone worships European and American customs, tends towards modernity, and only talks about comfort and convenience, the country and the people will suffer together, and the harm will be immeasurable. Her kind and gentle words and refined and elegant demeanor command respect. It is said that there are never disputes or idle talk in the Nie family, and everything is harmonious and joyful. Madam Nie often gathers her children, grandchildren, and relatives to talk about the virtues of the ancestors and all kinds of good words and instructions, as well as the instruction to use domestic goods. Mr. Yuntai and others all take notes or publish them in the Nie family precepts. Mr. Yuntai and his wife and children all dress and behave in a very simple and generous manner, not advocating luxury, and strongly resisting extravagance. They treat people with humility and courtesy, so people can recognize them at a glance when they go out. This is all due to the Madam's profound teaching. The Madam is especially able to be consistent in her work and never tires. On New Year's Day, at the Women's Friendship Conference, the Madam served as the chairman, leading her family to the meeting, and left after the end of the meeting without showing any fatigue. It is even more rare for an elderly person to have this kind of sitting ability.
