Educational News

Special Item

Report on Vocational Education by the Ministry of Education's Commissioners to Europe for Educational Inspection (6)

㈡ Mechanic School This school is divided into several departments, such as sand casting, machine repair, and auto parts manufacturing. Students admitted must be graduates of the seventh grade of elementary school, graduate in three years, study and work part-time. There are five full-time teachers and sixteen factory craftsmen. The products of the factory vary in type, with auto parts being the most important work. The government provides an annual subsidy of 51,000 Polish currency. The factory's output has an annual profit of about 100,000. The annual expenditure is about 120,000 to 130,000 currency. Students' practice emphasizes the accuracy of work, so material consumption is extremely low.

Basic practical courses include woodworking models, forging, sand casting, electric pole quenching, and steel tool manufacturing. Sand casting is particularly emphasized, with practical classes in this course for three years.

Hu Weixi (Wowicz)

Agricultural Vocational School This school is located in the countryside and can have close relationships with students' families. Its purpose is to recruit children of farmers to enroll. After graduation, they still return to the countryside to serve. Students are admitted from the age of seventeen. There are currently thirty students. In addition to agricultural courses, the school also teaches chicken farming, cattle farming, sheep farming, and pig raising. Every week, students must calculate feed and weigh to examine the relationship between feed and weight. Teachers visit students' families from time to time to inspect the achievements of graduates. Students' parents also form a committee to cooperate with each other.

Second, Vocational Education in Germany

Among the countries in the world that enjoy a high reputation for industrial manufacturing, Germany should be the first. The world generally believes that this is due to the great contribution of vocational education in Germany. Now, its current situation is briefly described separately as follows:

(1) Classification of Vocational Schools

Supplementary Schools In Germany, it is customary that anyone who wants to learn a profession or acquire a skill must be apprenticed to a master. This has been the case for centuries. This system is called the apprenticeship system. Between the master and the apprentice, an unwritten contract is formed for a period of several years. During this period, the apprentice's treatment is the same as that of family members. With the development of modern industrial manufacturing, the apprenticeship system, although somewhat limited in handicrafts, has more strictly regulated the ranks and training. All handicraft apprentices must take a craftsman examination (Gesellenprufung) upon completion of the prescribed apprenticeship period. Those who pass the exam are called craftsmen. After several years of craftsman service and reaching the age of 25 or older, they can apply for the master craftsman examination (Meisrprufung). Anyone who has passed the master craftsman examination is allowed to recruit apprentices in the factory. This apprenticeship method also exists in commerce, but it is more free and not stipulated by law. Large manufacturing plants also often follow this custom, ordering skilled craftsmen to train apprentices.

The German Constitution stipulates that all young men and women who have received eight years of national school education, whether they are apprentices in factories or have taken appropriate jobs, must receive supplementary education if they are 14 years of age or older but have not yet reached 18 years of age. The schools stipulated in this constitution are called supplementary schools (Fortbildungsscbule). Although the whole country has not been able to fully implement it, all cities and towns have established these schools. However, there are not a small number of supplementary schools established in rural areas. The organization of supplementary schools nationwide is not uniform. The curriculum is generally three years, but the number of hours taught is small, so the subjects are kept simple. In addition to vocational subjects, there are civics, mathematics, bookkeeping, German, physical education, hygiene, and vocational application of drafting. Great attention is also paid to commonly used letters and documents. For girls' classes, there are sewing, cooking, and housework courses. However, the subjects and teaching materials sometimes vary according to local needs. For example, in large cities where industry and commerce are developed, there are many people taking supplementary lessons, and a class can be set up for each subject and taught separately, such as metal workers, locksmiths, carpenters, and tailors, each with a class. In remote areas, there are not many supplementary students, so classes are divided according to the major categories of each industry, such as all metal industries combined into one class, and all woodworking industries combined into one class. In extremely small areas, where the number of people is too small, the supplementary personnel of each industry are combined and taught together.

In rural areas, there are also similar school facilities for young people engaged in agriculture, such as farmers' children and laborers. The nature of these schools is slightly different from other supplementary schools. The teaching period is entirely in the winter, and they are called agricultural supplementary schools (LandlicheFcrtbildnngsscbule). The purpose of agricultural supplementary schools is to maintain the knowledge of culture and work and life that young people from farming families have gained in elementary school, and to cultivate their fundamental knowledge and skills in agricultural arts. The obligation for students to enter supplementary schools is also stipulated in the laws and regulations of local governments, and there are also those stipulated by local cities and villages. All young employees should have four to eight hours of school time per week. Employers have an obligation to allow employees to attend school during working hours.

Vocational schools and supplementary schools are only for supplementing the knowledge of employed employees and are not designed to train specialized skills. Therefore, for the purpose of training skilled craftsmen and engineering personnel, industrial and commercial industries have established vocational schools (Facbschule). Enrollment in vocational schools is free and not compulsory. They are full-day schools and not part-time schools. Only a few schools have half-day courses, and students can take other practical work in their spare time.

Vocational schools must cultivate talents to meet the needs of students with different levels of education. Therefore, the level of schools must be divided into shallow and deep to meet this requirement. The first type of school is where students practice art before entering employment. These schools are called preparatory vocational schools (Vorbere

tendeFachschulen). The second type of school requires students to have practical work experience before entering. These schools are called continuing vocational schools (WeiterfurendcFacbschulen). The entrance qualification for preparatory schools is eight years of elementary school graduation, while the entrance qualification for continuing schools is completion of the first two years of senior high school (Obersieknunda).

There are many types and numbers of vocational schools in Germany. Some are established for local needs, and some are close to the nature of local industries. However, most schools are directly related to the national industrial, commercial, and agricultural industries.

㈠ Preparatory Vocational Schools (i.e., Junior Schools) Junior schools can be divided into the following four categories:

(A) Commercial Schools and Secondary Commercial Schools The entrance qualification for commercial schools is limited to elementary school graduation, while the entrance qualification for secondary commercial schools is limited to junior high school graduation. The purpose is to cultivate young people's ability to engage in commerce in the future. The main courses are commercial law, commercial correspondence, accounting, bookkeeping, etc. Secondary commercial schools add foreign languages. The curriculum organization varies slightly from school to school. Some are one-year, some are one and a half years, and some are two years. When students graduate and serve, they can be exempted from part of their apprenticeship period.

(B) Industrial Schools of Mechanics and Metallurgy Industrial schools are extremely specialized in mechanical training. Therefore, school training can replace all apprenticeship training. The subjects are mechanical drawing and common sense of technology, and most of the time is spent on factory work.

(C) Women's Vocational Schools This type of school focuses on household work and garment sewing. Students are free to choose whether it is for future household life or for future self-employment. Every big city (town) must have this type of women's school, either municipal or state-owned, or schools established by public groups and societies, such as Lett|Haus and Peslulozzi|Frobel|Haus in Berlin.

(b) Agricultural Schools These are set up for the children of small farmers and middle-class farmers, providing them with the knowledge and skills needed in agricultural affairs to assist in rural development.

㈡ Continuing Vocational Schools (i.e., Intermediate Schools) This type of school is broadly divided into the following types. The levels are not uniform.

(a) Architectural Schools Now also known as National Secondary Industrial Architectural Schools, their purpose is to train those in earthwork, carpentry, and stonework to have the ability to pass the craftsman examination and practice independently, and to train assistants for private construction companies and engineering offices, as well as intermediate engineers for local engineering bureaus. The subjects are generally divided into two parts: 1. House construction department, 2. Roads, railways, bridges, and water conservancy projects. There are also land surveying courses. The curriculum is divided into five grades, with a study period of six months for each grade. The minimum age for entering students is 16 years old, having graduated from elementary school and having 12 months of continuous practical experience. However, the regulations of each state vary slightly. The main subjects are house construction, architectural drawing, as well as mathematics, physics, natural sciences, building materials science, commerce, civics, and physical education.

(b) Mechanical Engineering Schools Also known as National Machine Schools, their purpose is to train engineering personnel in mechanical manufacturing and design and management. Their scope of work emphasizes knowledge of higher industry. The entrance qualification for one part is having completed the first two years of high school, or having passed the entrance examination separately, and having two years of practical experience. The curriculum is five semesters long, with a graduation examination. The other part is having graduated from eight years of elementary school, having attended a vocational supplementary school, and having four years of practical experience. The curriculum includes four semesters, with a similar graduation examination. Within mechanical engineering schools, there are also attached precision machinery, electrical engineering, instrument manufacturing, electrical technology, machine installation, and metalworking.

(c) Textile Industrial Schools The organization of this school is similar to that of mechanical engineering schools. It is divided into two groups. The subjects of secondary textile schools train business managers, factory managers, textile engineers, mechanical engineering personnel, personnel who design textile machines, and personnel who apply chemistry to textiles in the textile manufacturing industry. The preparatory textile schools train office workers and technicians for companies or factories, as well as pattern workers. This type of school has the most complete equipment and is extremely sufficient in practical training. There is no limit to the qualifications for admission, as long as one has received a good general education and considerable practical experience.

(d) Craft Schools This type of school includes fine arts and crafts. It trains auxiliary personnel in art (personnel in painting, design, and art venues), independent art professionals, and theoretical and practical tutoring for craftsmen, journeymen, and apprentices. The subjects in the school are classified extremely complexly. Some specialize in one subject, while others combine several subjects. Some also have very complex subjects, all based on local needs. The school must have factory equipment. The duration of the curriculum is not uniform. In addition to day school, there are also evening classes and Sunday classes. There are no strict regulations for entering the school, but students must have sufficient talent and good practical experience.

Other Places

Peking University Owes More Than One Million in Educational Expenses

Intends to Issue School Bonds to Repay Gradually

(Nanjing, 10th) Chiang Menglin, President of Peking University, arrived in Nanjing on the morning of the 9th. He met with Wang Shijie and said that since the national crisis, due to the shortage of the national treasury, the regular expenses of Peking University have not been fully allocated, and the salaries of teachers and staff and other expenses have been in arrears for more than one million yuan, which has not yet been repaid. It is now planned to issue a kind of school bond to repay gradually. Since July last year, the central government has had no arrears in educational expenses, allocating 75,000 yuan per month. The educational expenses for Peiping and Tianjin are 360,000 yuan per month. After the central government unified taxation, the Ministry of Finance issued them on time without any arrears. The purpose of my trip to Nanjing this time is to report to Minister Wang, and then to visit President Wang before returning to Shanghai and then returning to the north.

Meeting of the Ministry of Education's Committee on Public Education Today

Emphasizing the Promotion of Public Schools

(Nanjing, 10th) The Ministry of Education has scheduled to hold the first meeting of the Committee on Public Education at 9:00 a.m. on the 11th. There are 19 members. The nine proposals submitted by the Ministry will be discussed first. According to Zhang Jiong, Director of the Department of Social Education, this meeting will focus on the promotion of public schools. In addition, cases such as eliminating illiteracy and enriching libraries cannot be achieved in concrete results in a short-term meeting. We should start with investigation, make precise plans, and gradually promote them.

The main purpose of the Ministry of Education's Committee on Public Education is to assist the Ministry of Education in planning and promoting national public education affairs. According to the regulations, a plenary committee meeting is held every six months. The Ministry of Education convened committee members last year in the first half of the year to hold an establishment meeting. The plenary committee meeting will be held in the conference room of the Ministry of Education starting at 9:00 a.m. today (11th). According to the regulations, the members of this meeting are the Vice Ministers of the Ministry of Education (Duan Xipeng Qian Changzhao), the Director of the Department of Social Education of the Ministry of Education (Zhang Jiong), the Section Chief (Peng Baichuan Zhong Xiu), one counselor designated by the Ministry of Education (Chen Panzao), one supervisor (Zhong Daozan), and nine to thirteen appointed members, who are hired by the Ministry of Education from three people from the Central Party Department (Wang Qi, Chen Lifu, Yu Jingtang), and one person each from the Ministry of Interior (Wang Xianqiang) and the Ministry of Industry (Xu Tinghu), personnel related to public education, and four to eight public education experts and enthusiasts for public education (Niu Yongjian, Liang Shuming, Chen Jiantong, Gao Yang, Meng Xiancheng, Yan Yangchu, Xiang Jutang). In addition to the above-mentioned dozen or so committee members, there are also Ministry of Education Commissioner Li Jiaxiang (because he has inspected social education in Europe), Director of the Anhui Education Department Yang Kang, and Director of the Preparatory Office of the Central Library Jiang Fuzong, etc. The nine proposals were finalized before the discussion. Committee members can also propose proposals at any time. The Ministry of Education previously issued a public education plan to solicit opinions. Currently, only one opinion letter from Dong Huai, Director of the Shandong Provincial Public Education Museum, and Liu Jihong, a teacher at the Wuxi Jiangsu Provincial Public Education School, has been received. Others, such as committee members, have not yet sent them, perhaps they will bring them temporarily.

Principal Li of Normal University Discusses Reasons for Resignation During Fire Investigation

Ministry of Education Has Not Approved Resignation, Li Still Responsible as Usual

Professors Donate 500 Yuan in Salary to Aid Affected Students

(Special Dispatch from Peiping) After Li Zheng, the president of National Peiping Normal University, resigned, he still went to the school to take responsibility because the Ministry of Education had not yet approved it. Today (9th), at 8 a.m., representatives of the affected students visited the president, requesting relief. Professors Yang Likui and others held a meeting last night to stipulate the method for professors to donate their salaries to help the affected students. The Ministry of Education is very concerned about the fire at the Normal University. The Normal University sent a report to the Ministry of Education the day before yesterday, detailing the location, cause of the fire, the extent of the damage, and the measures taken for aftermath, along with a list of donations and a diagram of the school building. Today (9th), the school received an express mail telegram from the Ministry of Education, inquiring about the detailed circumstances of the fire. Details of each situation are recorded as follows:

Ministry of Education Telegram to Li Zheng, Principal of Peiping Normal University: Your winter telegram has been received. The destruction of school buildings and student's books and belongings is deeply felt. Please investigate and report the cause of the fire and how the aftermath is being handled. Seal of the Ministry of Education. (Reporter's Note) The Ministry of Education's express mail telegram from the 6th arrived in Peiping at 8 a.m. on the 9th. The Normal University had already prepared a report on the cause of the fire and the aftermath measures, which was sent to Beijing by express mail on the 8th. It is expected that Principal Li Zheng's resignation report will arrive in Beijing on the 10th, so there has been no reply received in Peiping at this moment. It is expected that the Ministry of Education's reply will arrive in Peiping around the 14th.

Li Zheng Speaks to Reporter: This reporter made a special visit to Li Zheng, the principal of Normal University. According to his talk, I am resigning for two reasons: 1. In this fire, the students' notes and translations cannot be compensated, and the loss of books is also considerable. I feel deeply uneasy because I did not take sufficient precautions beforehand, so I resign to take responsibility. 2. I have been at Normal University for over a year and am ashamed that I have not achieved any results. At this moment, it is also the end of the semester, which is a break in administrative affairs. I can retire and rest, allowing others to take my place. Until the Ministry of Education approves my resignation, I will still come to the school to take responsibility. The students who have been affected by the disaster have a very good attitude and do not make excessive demands. Most of the students at Normal University are from poor families, and it is appropriate for them to ask for relief after the disaster. I express my deep sympathy. Relief funds have now been distributed, and the affected students have received the funds. As for those affected students who are entitled to receive ten yuan, after submitting a loss statement and being reviewed by the department head, a supplementary payment can be considered, only the timing will be slightly different. The Taikoo Insurance Company has sent specialists Leiber and Han Wenbin to the school to inspect, and after opening the list for review, the compensation can be paid according to the regulations, it is said.

Professors Donate Funds: Normal University professors held a meeting at the Jieying Restaurant at 7 p.m. on the 8th. Professors Yang Likui, Li Jianxun, Yuan Dunli, Li Jinxi, Liu Tuo, Zhao Jinyi, etc. were present. Yuan Dunli chaired the meeting. The chairman first gave a report, saying that the fire at Normal University was extremely unfortunate. Many of the affected students are from poor families and cannot afford to repurchase the lost books. The professors, out of their love for the students' studies, should donate funds to help the students. Please discuss this. Next, the professors spoke one after another and all agreed to donate their salaries to help the students. Finally, it was decided that the total amount of professors' salary donations would be 500 yuan, to be used specifically for the purchase of books for the affected students.

Zhejiang Education Department Revises Regulations for County Education Bureau Management of Education Funds Committee

Amendments Made to Articles 3 and 7

The Zhejiang Provincial Education Department believes that the regulations for the County Education Bureau's management of the County Education Funds Committee were distributed in January of the 21st year of the Republic of China. Now, because Articles 3 and 7 are not applicable, they have been specially revised. The revisions have been submitted to the 644th meeting of the Provincial Government Committee for discussion and approval. The revised articles are recorded as follows: Article 3: The County Education Bureau's Management of the County Education Funds Committee shall establish three standing committee members, one of whom shall be concurrently held by the Director of the Education Bureau, and the remaining members shall be mutually elected by the committee members to handle daily affairs. When a meeting is held, the standing committee members shall mutually elect one person as the chairman. Article 7: If any of the committee members are found to be incompetent, and the Education Department, after investigation, believes that a replacement is necessary, the county may be instructed to change the nomination or reappoint the member.

The Vigorous Progress of the Provincial Yancheng Middle School

Since Mr. Wu Dezhang took over as principal of the Jiangsu Provincial Yancheng Middle School this semester, he has been meticulously reorganizing the school, sparing no effort. The teaching is serious, and the management is strict. The school followed the National Salvation Education Implementation Guidelines promulgated by the Education Department, formulated National Salvation Education Implementation Programs, and submitted them to the Department for verification and approval. The Department recognized that the program was quite detailed and feasible and instructed them to follow it. In recent months, the teaching and guidance facilities have been implemented one by one in accordance with the National Salvation Education Program. Principal Wu is particularly enthusiastic and devoted to military training, and the instructors are strict. The training not only focuses on military training academic subjects, but also the students' etiquette and manners are militarized. The senior high school second and third grades held live ammunition shooting at the end of December. The entire class performed well, especially the high school second grade student Ren Fatang, who hit the target with two of the three shots, scoring 9 and 8 points, for a total of 26 points. Moreover, the three bullet holes were connected in a line, which is truly commendable. According to the squad leader of the county police brigade who was present to take care of the shooting that day, it is rarely seen even in the army. At that time, in order to encourage students' interest in shooting, Principal Wu also shot three bullets, hitting the target with all three shots, for a total of 12 points. Hu Dun, the chairman of the Jiangsu Provincial National Military Training Committee, inspected the military training at the school and was very satisfied with the students' full spirit and strict discipline. He especially praised the dormitory for adopting the company system, with neat and clean bedding. On New Year's Eve, the school celebrated the New Year with teachers and students, holding a carnival with performances mostly of new national salvation dramas. A results exhibition was held on January 1st and 2nd. As for the school's facilities, a new laboratory has been completed, and plans are currently underway to build a self-study room.

All Forms Sent to Beijing Yesterday

The second three-item general registration of Boy Scouts in this city has been going on for many days. Among these 55 troops, 34 troops are required to complete the second registration according to law. All forms, registration fees, and attachments have been submitted to the City Boy Scout Council, which has compiled and reviewed them separately. A total of 28 troops have completed the second registration procedures, with a total of more than 2,300 new and old Boy Scouts. In addition, there are 80 service members who have completed the second registration. The forms, registration fees, and attachments of the above-mentioned registered troop Boy Scout service members have been prepared by the City Council and sent to the Headquarters of the Boy Scouts of China by Xie Yanbo. Mr. Xie left for Beijing by train last night. The forms and fees for the 12 newly registered troops and more than 100 service members in this city were also brought along and submitted to the headquarters. Therefore, it is expected that the total number of Boy Scout troops in the city will exceed 70 this spring, and the number of Boy Scouts will reach more than 5,000.

Executive Yuan Replies to City Education Association Regarding Geng (Boxer Indemnity) Funds Management Method

Revenue and Expenditure Reports to Be Sent to Audit Department for Review

Use and Distribution to Be Decided by the Geng Funds Joint Committee

Funds Not Used for Establishing International Library

The Shanghai Education Association had previously requested the central government and the Executive Yuan to stipulate a unified management method for the Geng (Boxer Indemnity) funds and to announce the actual revenue and expenditure situation, and also requested a thorough investigation into whether the Geng funds were used for the establishment of the Chinese International Library in Geneva. Yesterday, the association received a reply from the Executive Yuan Secretariat. The original letter is copied below: "By order of the President, the Shanghai Education Association's Standing Director Zhou Feicheng, etc., submitted a request for the Council to stipulate a unified management method for the Geng funds and to announce the actual revenue and expenditure situation, and also requested a thorough investigation into whether the Geng funds were used for the establishment of the Chinese International Library in Geneva. It has been determined that the Executive Yuan convened a meeting of various Geng funds agencies last month and resolved that, after the end of each fiscal year, the various Geng funds agencies should submit their final accounts and monthly revenue and expenditure reports to this Yuan for forwarding to the Audit Department for review, and this Yuan will convene a joint meeting on Geng funds every year to discuss the next year's budget and the amount and plans for educational and cultural undertakings. As for whether the Geng funds were used for the establishment of the Chinese International Library in Geneva, the relevant agencies were previously asked to investigate, and the Board of Directors for the Management of Sino-Russian Geng Funds Water Conservancy Expenses, the Sino-French Geng Funds Committee, the Board of Directors for the Management of Sino-British Geng Funds, and the Board of Directors of the China Education and Culture Foundation have successively replied that they have not used their respective Geng funds. Except for the Board of Directors for the Management of Russian Funds, which has been closed, and the Sino-Italian Geng Funds Committee, which has not yet distributed or used the Italian Geng funds, it is not necessary to send a letter urging them to reply. The Secretariat should send a letter urging the Sino-French Education Foundation Committee to reply as soon as possible, and inform the original submitters of the above details." Chuminyi, Secretary General of the Executive Yuan.

Shanghai Bank's Ximen Branch Waives Tuition Remittance Fees

Limited to Schools Entrusting the Bank to Collect Fees

The Shanghai Commercial & Savings Bank has numerous branches in the Beijing and Shanghai areas, making remittances as convenient as those of the Bank of China and the Bank of Communications. Moreover, the fees are low, so the bank's remittance business is quite developed. Now, Mr. Ying, the manager of the bank's Ximen branch, has noted that the number of schools entrusting the branch to collect tuition fees has increased year by year. In order to facilitate students' payment, he has specially formulated preferential measures. All students from schools entrusting the bank to collect tuition fees who remit fees from other cities for amounts under 200 yuan will be exempt from remittance fees to show excellence. The bank has never charged handling fees for collecting tuition fees on behalf of schools, which is purely voluntary. This time, the bank has also waived remittance fees, and the bank's enthusiasm for education is truly admirable.

Shanghai, Hong Kong, and Tianjin Interport Football Lineups

Tianjin and Hong Kong's Selections Largely Determined

Shanghai's to Be Revealed After Two Trial Matches

In previous years, the interport football matches were only between Shanghai and Hong Kong or Shanghai and Tianjin. Only once before have Shanghai, Hong Kong, and Tianjin competed together in one place, due to Shanghai being the central point between the North and South, so it was held in Shanghai. As a result, Tianjin won the championship. This season will be the second triangular contest, with the location still in Shanghai, scheduled for the Lunar New Year. Shanghai, Hong Kong, and Tianjin are all actively preparing, selecting elites, and preparing to win the championship. The details are recorded as follows:

Tianjin: Tianjin has held two preliminary trial matches. One was during the New Year, divided into the Guolian and Junlian teams. Only Sun Sijing was selected among the Chinese players. As a result, Guoji won 6-2. The second was held last Sunday, divided into the Red and White teams. As a result, the White team won 7-4. Roxburg was unable to play that day due to illness. Deller, Jiang Lu, and others performed very well. Initially, in the first half, the White team won 6-1. In the second half, the two sides made slight changes to their lineups. Jie Hansen, Jones, and Aiqu'er defected to the Deng team, and Deng's team won 3-1. In total, the White team won 7-4. The Tianjin representative lineup has been largely determined as follows:

He Ou Jiang Lu

Da Silva Jie Hansen

Motuo Sun Sijing Budufu

Deller Jones

Roxburg Aiqu'er

Reserves: Huaifen, Mi Xia Rui Ke Ren

Hong Kong: Hong Kong held a trial match on the 3rd of this month, divided into the Blue and White teams, with the White team being the ideal lineup. The performance was not beautiful. The Chinese players participating were Huang Jiliang, Liang Rongzhao, Zheng Jiliang, Yang Shuiyi, Tan Jiangbai, and He Jiaqiang, etc. As a result, the White team won 2-1. After the match, the Football Association carefully considered and selected 14 players as official representatives. The Chinese players selected were Huang Jiliang, Liang Rongzhao, Tan Jiangbai, and Zheng Jiliang (all from the South China team), and it was decided that the captain would be Kirk. Although the Dagaoshanu brothers did not attend the trial match, they were still selected as official team members based on their past performance. They are scheduled to depart for Shanghai around February 9th. The lineup is roughly as follows:

Kirk

Huang Jiliang Bilu Quilao Hou Hual

Shanghai: Shanghai has many talents, and the hope of victory is stronger. After returning victorious from Hong Kong last year, they were invited by the Tianjin Xilian Association to go north to compete. In terms of the selection of personnel, they filled the ranks with inferior players, resulting in a disastrous defeat of 7-1, which was an unprecedented disgrace in the history of the Shanghai Interport team and was greatly slandered by people in the North. This season, the triangular competition is being held in Shanghai. Hong Kong and Tianjin are carefully selecting personnel to come to Shanghai to challenge, so the Shanghai team should be extra careful in selecting personnel. The performance of the trial match on New Year's Day was still good, but many players did not appear on the field, which is not enough to see the real situation. The second trial match should give a slight indication.

Assaulting Referee Case Transferred to Special District Court for Prosecution

The case of Jiaotong University students assaulting referee Shen Huichun has been going on for many days and has not yet been resolved. Mr. Shen hired lawyer E Sen and filed a lawsuit with the local court according to law. Yesterday (10th) at 1:00 PM, the prosecutor's office opened an investigation hearing. However, because the location of the defendant's crime was within the scope of the road built across the border, which is not under the jurisdiction of the local court, the court instructed that the lawsuit should be filed with the First Court of the Special District, and the case was dismissed. It has been learned that Mr. Shen has rehired his original lawyer and will file a lawsuit with the jurisdictional court.

Japanese Volleyball Team Selected for Far Eastern Games

Currently Training at Hiroshima Camp

Preparing to Win 10th Championship

| Japanese Government Subsidizes 60,000 for Far Eastern Expenses |

(Tokyo Correspondent) The expenses for Japan's participation in the 10th Far Eastern Games to be held in the Philippines in May this year have been submitted by the Japan Sports Association to the Japanese government for subsidies. The Japanese government has now approved a subsidy of 60,000 yuan. However, this amount is still considered meager, and the remainder will be raised by the Japan Sports Association itself, it is said. Spring and Autumn

Thoughts on Children's Year

— Chen Tuigan

I remember that in October of last year, the China Child Welfare Association submitted a request to the government to designate this year as Children's Year. Subsequently, the Shanghai Municipal Children's Welfare Committee formulated all the measures for Children's Year and submitted them to the government for record. Every year on April 4th, our country has followed the example of European and American countries and designated it as Children's Day. Now there is Children's Year again, which is quite novel and interesting. However, I cannot help but have some thoughts.

Our country's society has always been inattentive to children. The general mentality is that children understand nothing, so they cannot be treated the same as adults. Families with children often have difficulty renting a house (my family has lived in Shanghai for four years and moved three times. Each time I looked at a house, the landlord would always ask how many children I had in my family, believing that families with three or five children would definitely be noisy and annoying). The sound of women in the alley scolding children is even deafening. The wives of laborers, after giving birth to children, even abandon them in trash cans. Pure children, where is your happiness? How can it not be heartbreaking?

On the other hand, how much do European and American countries care for children? Almost all public facilities in society have a place for children; children's parks and early childhood education centers in cities are even more visible everywhere. And scholars generally advocate that the twentieth century is the century of children. European and American children are so happy, while Chinese children are not valued like them, which is especially heartbreaking in comparison.

Children are the future masters of the country and the new elements of national progress. If we want to revitalize the country and nation, we must take special care of children. This year, the Shanghai Municipal Children's Welfare Association is actively preparing to set up various nurseries, and those in charge are mostly domestic education experts, who raise children on behalf of families and cultivate elements on behalf of the country. This is indeed a great charitable social education undertaking. I hope that people from all walks of life will do their best to help them. We must know that this kind of facility is not only a matter of children's personal happiness, but also a matter of the rise and fall of the entire nation. Everyone should take some responsibility.

Finally, I especially hope that the Children's Welfare Committee can extend this facility to all provinces and counties, so that charitable organizations across the country will rise up in response, and more Montessori will be produced. The future of the nation is deeply dependent on this.

Lord Cha and Lord Sha

— Yan Qiao

There is a saying in Suzhou: "Lord Cha flies gold leaf paper." It is a satire on the extravagance of playboy sons, who will eventually become impoverished. It is said that there is a story behind it. On the Double Ninth Festival, he climbed the Beisi Pagoda of Baoen Temple and saw people flying colored paper, which was very fun. So he bought a lot of gold leaf paper and flew it down from the pagoda. People below the pagoda suspected that it was a golden rain and scrambled to grab it, causing a sensation far and wide. Mingzhai Xiaozhi says that this was the affair of Huang Xueqian of Qingpu, and at that time there was also a taunt of "importantly poor." However, no one mentions Huang anymore, but Cha has evolved into a drama called "Cha Pan's Rivalry of Wealth." In the end, is it Huang or Cha? It is unknown.

Who knew that there was also a Lord Sha in Wucheng Land Changchun Xiangyinlou Bintan. That Lord Sha was so extravagant that he could not hire a boat on the Dragon Boat Festival to watch the boat race in Tiger Hill. The following year, a month in advance, he ordered his servants to hire all the boat owners inside and outside the city, and did not allow them to hire to others. On the Dragon Boat Festival, people could not hire a boat, so they all discussed with Lord Sha to transfer the hire. Lord Sha generously agreed, designated a location, and dispatched them separately. The boats were lined with ready-made wine and dishes, and there were also beautiful courtesans to serve wine, without the need for tourists to spend a penny. From then on, Lord Sha's name was known to women and children. Later, he became so poor that he made a living selling snacks, and he liked to sing folk songs and ditties. Children would buy three big coins worth of oil cakes and also ask him to sing a piece like "Cutting Flowers Sha Night Tour." But people still called him Lord Sha. Although he did not have the matter of flying gold leaf paper, his behavior was similar to that of Lord Cha. Perhaps Lord Cha and Lord Sha are one and the same, because Cha and Sha rhyme and are easily confused. Otherwise, they are both Lords, "what a coincidence!" Moreover, there is nothing else seen about Lord Sha's words. The Bintan record did not note the era, and it was probably derived from hearsay, and there may be a possibility of mistaken Cha for Sha.

The current Suzhou definitely does not have such extravagant acts as Lord Cha. Even if there are a few playboy sons, they only seek their own enjoyment, and who is willing to benefit others. In this cold winter, they are at home surrounded by the stove, listening to wireless broadcasts, smoking cigars, and drinking brandy. Even the beggars at the door asking for a copper plate are waved away by the doorman. Then Lord Cha can be considered a unique creation, rare and valuable, even if he is defeated (a prodigal son), he is still glorious.

Cold Wind

— Qian Xiaoshan

Cold wind saddens the evening,

Gusts disturb carriage dust.

A guest's time is cheap,

Returning home brings genuine laughter.

Wars are not yet over,

Disasters must have a cause.

Who can foresee the coming days?

It's hard to be a peasant.

Winter Solstice

— Qian Xiaoshan

The mirage of the city rises with festive joy,

But alone before the lamp, my shadow grieves.

The cold begins, I dislike the wine's thinness,

The night cannot offset my lengthening sorrow.

Desolate, what kind of world is this now?

Endless, the sky is covered in frost.

No need to play the six pipes,

I myself lament the setting sun.

Experiment Report on "Kissing Endurance"

— Ya Men

This journal previously published a strange story of the "New York Kissing Endurance Competition," which caused a sensation among our colleagues and was spread around. Some of my colleagues are over forty years old, and their wives are yellow-faced women who do not understand what kissing is; some are just over twenty and have not yet encountered Miss, naturally not. They would not believe the endurance results of Ms. Du Liusi and her lover. However, there are also some people who are half-believing. Therefore, those who do not believe at all and those who are half-believing argued - playfully argued.

I have been newly married for not long, and my wife is still studying at the county women's normal school, which is considered more modern in the eyes of my colleagues. The outcome of their argument was that I had to go back and experiment. When they were arguing heatedly, I had the intention of going back to experiment. As soon as they appointed me, I accepted the order without hesitation.

My new wife was busy preparing for the fourth monthly exam. When I returned home at 9:00 PM, she was still working diligently. I asked her to kiss, and she reluctantly complied and then focused her eyes on the book again. I continued to ask, but she refused. I discussed with her about the things during the day. She replied to me; "I don't have that much free time." I was disappointed and gave up.

I graded papers, and she read books until 11:00 PM, when we both went to sleep. I don't know why, after a hard day, although tired, I couldn't sleep. The events of the day were just jumping curiously in my mind. I couldn't bear it, and without asking for consent, I hugged her tightly and kissed her. Oh, no, it separated in less than a minute. This was not because the unconsenting her pushed me away, I really couldn't bear it. I was really amazed at Ms. Du's achievement of more than three hours, so amazed that I didn't quite believe it.

When her and my mouths are closed together, we can't help but breathe at the same time. The carbon dioxide coming out of the four nostrils collides together and makes a sound. In that small space of the nostrils, in that short time of sixteen breaths per minute, the carbon dioxide does not have time to dissipate, and the fresh air does not have time to rush in. The second absorption is still carbon dioxide, which is very uncomfortable. If the two breathe one after the other, it would be even worse. What I absorb is exactly her carbon dioxide, and what she absorbs is exactly my carbon dioxide, which is even more uncomfortable. I am unwilling and unable to do more of the absorption of carbon dioxide, and besides, I don't want to win any championship, so I was defeated in less than a minute.

Miscellaneous Thoughts

Record of Bullfighting at Jinhua Temple (Part 1)

— Shen Yan

From the perspective of humanitarianism, bullfighting seems to be a very brutal thing, but on the other hand, it is a beautiful act of promoting civic spirit and advocating martial spirit. Probably everything in the world has its advantages and disadvantages, and we don't need to discuss it in detail; just in terms of the superficial phenomena, bullfighting is always a more exciting scene in animal games.

I believe that most Chinese people's understanding of bullfighting (referring to the majority) comes from books and movies, and everyone knows only Spanish bullfighting. Of course, I myself am the same. I have only seen magnificent bullfighting arenas, bulls with sharp knives tied to their horns, horses forced to be sacrificed, and agile warriors wielding spears in the notes of predecessors and in movies. In other words, most of us only think that bullfighting is a patent of European countries and is a very complex cornering skill, and there is never an opportunity to see it in the Americas or East Asia. However, unexpectedly, on the program list of the whole line opening ceremony of the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway, I actually found the line "Bullfighting at Jinhua Temple". What a moving program this is!

Attracted by this amazing program, a few of us took advantage of the convenience of our duties and actually stepped from Shanghai, which only sees smoke and coal in the sky, to the picturesque Jinhua at 2:00 PM on December 28th, the 22nd year of the Republic of China. Of course, Jinhua is a familiar place to us because of ham (actually, let me tell you in passing, the place of ham production is Dongyang, and Jinhua is just a transit station). After we got off the train, we reluctantly lingered at the venue of the whole line opening ceremony of the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway for four or five minutes, deliberately crossed the railway tracks, and ran to the opposite side of the station to admire our main objective - bullfighting.

The bullfighting arena happened to be set up on a plain surrounded by mountains on three sides. Several thousand people were squeezing, shouting, and floating on various mountain tops. Looking from a distance of several tens of feet, it was a vivid scene of a "human wall." So a few of us walked up a high and low dirt hill, and halfway up the hill, we saw two bamboo poles carrying a white flag with black characters, with the three characters "Bullfighting Arena" written on it. Next to the flag, a gentleman wearing a coarse cloth gown gave me a program list, which was printed with copper letters. I didn't expect them to be so sophisticated!

The program list was printed very clearly. The first pair was two bulls, so-and-so, fighting each other, and the second pair was two bulls, so-and-so, fighting each other. There were more than a dozen pairs in total, and the names of these bulls were so special that they were somewhat incredible. The most common one is to call it something "Gua," like "Double Tooth Gua," "Hero Gua," "Black Dragon Gua," etc. I really can't figure out what this "Gua" word should be interpreted as. In addition, there are those who borrow the names of ancient people, such as "Luo Cheng" and "Wu Song." The strangest ones are "Little Casual," "Little Dirty," "New Flower Dan," "Little Flower Dan," etc. It can be said that they are picked up at will and have no consciousness at all, just a simple way to be funny and amusing.

Walking up the hilltop, and with much difficulty, grabbing some foothold under the shoulders of many Jinhua friends, everyone stretched their necks and looked towards the center. The center was originally a flat area, but now it has become a shallow pond that is tens of feet long and wide; around the pond, there are countless tenants dressed up, barefoot, surrounding it in groups. In the middle, there are also several people with rolled up sleeves, their bodies covered with mud, even their heads and faces, almost like a mud man; it is said that they were specially elected to be bullfighting experts as notaries or assistants, and when the two bulls were fighting together, they would go over and separate them, so that each bull would not have any excessive behavior, and so that each bull would have equal opportunities to fight.

So how do these bulls actually fight?

From the moment I departed from the Shanghai North Railway Station until I walked to the bullfighting arena, my heart was always beating non-stop, thinking that I would definitely see a tragedy of piercing chests and abdomens, and flesh and blood flying everywhere. I think most of the people who went from Shanghai or Hangzhou this time thought this way!

Northeast Fourth Company Commander

— Zhang Henshui

Chapter Twenty-One

Whispering Under the Lamp, Painstakingly Teaching the Weak Offspring

Leaning on a Cane, Wandering Below the Mountain, Calmly Watching the Heroes

Old Zhao suddenly understood the reason why he was lingering outside the door. He put his jujube wood cane into his arms, clasped his fists, and bowed several times to Ji Zhi, laughing loudly in a high voice, "I wouldn't dare to say that." Ji Zhi said, "Old Master Zhao, you're in good spirits. The weather is good today, so you're out for a walk?" Old Zhao said, "I heard the red leaves on West Mountain are beautiful, so I wanted to take a look." Ji Zhi said, "Are you walking there?" Old Zhao smiled, holding the jujube wood cane in one hand, while smoothing his beard with the other. Ji Zhi laughed, "The red leaves are at the Badachu Park, not at the Biyun Temple. From here, it's about forty or fifty li round trip, right?" Old Zhao said, "My friend, don't look at my age. Walking twenty or thirty li is nothing. I plan to walk there and hire an animal to ride back. I was just worried about being lonely walking alone. Second Master, are you interested?" Ji Zhi recalled the time last year when he and Gui Zhi went to see the red leaves, and realized that it was that time of year again. Thinking about the past and present, he felt an endless sense of melancholy. Now that Gui Zhi was in a wealthy family and seemingly lost forever, it wouldn't be bad to take this opportunity to walk ten or twenty li with this old man to find out about Gui Zhi's news. Besides, he was feeling very troubled himself and could use some distraction. So he laughed, "If Old Master has such an interest, I'll accompany you." Zhao Weng was overjoyed to hear that he was willing to accompany him. He clasped his hands and bowed a few times, laughing, "While the weather is still early, let's go. It doesn't matter if we get tired. We'll stop wherever we reach." The rural people ate their meals early, and both of them had already eaten, so they didn't delay and started walking along the main road. Who knew that Zhao Weng was strong and energetic, and walked no less than Ji Zhi. He usually dragged the jujube wood cane he held in his hand. The two of them chatted idly as they walked, so they didn't feel tired. By a little after two o'clock, they arrived at the foot of West Mountain. (288)

Free Talk

The Glory of the Future

— Zhang Chenglu

Almost every year, foreign writers come to China, and every time they come, they cause a little trouble. First there was Bernard Shaw, then there was Tagore; only Valéry, everyone doesn't want to mention, or can't mention. Tagore didn't talk about politics, thinking he could stay out of the controversy, but he earned the title of "foreign literary riffraff" for complimenting food and sex, and our commentators debated about it here. He's probably going to write novels now.

It's impossible for our noses to be as high and straight as Europeans', but if we have a few coins in our pockets, we can watch movies the same way. Detective movies are boring, love movies are stale, war movies are tiresome, and comedy movies are pointless, so we have "Tarzan the Ape Man," "Beast of the Jungle," and "African Adventure," etc., bringing wild beasts and barbarians onto the stage. But even in barbarous lands, there must be a little bit of the curvy bodies of barbarian women. If we still like to watch it, then it shows that no matter how much we ridicule it, we are still a little reluctant to let go. "Sex" is very important to the petty bourgeoisie.

In Western Europe, literary magazines and movies are not that different; some so-called literary figures also have to find some bizarre (Grotesque) and erotic (Erotic) things to satisfy their patrons, so there are

adventurous trips, the purpose of which is not to bow to the local landlords or ask for wine. However, if asked a foolish question, they dismiss it with a joke. They don't really understand these things, and they don't need to know. Tagore is just one of these people.

But Chinese people, in the works of these kinds of writers, will appear on the stage with various so-called "natives." Just look at the itinerary of Mr. Tagore published in the newspaper ｜ China, Southeast Asia, South America. England, Germany, etc. are too ordinary. We must be aware that we are being depicted, and we must also be aware that the glory of being depicted will increase, and we must also be aware that in the future, people will find it interesting that such things happened.

In Memory of Lunacharsky

— Xiu Xia

Yesterday, I read a news item in a Tianjin newspaper titled "The Honors of a Russian Literary Giant," which said:

Moscow, 1st dispatch: The remains of the great writer Lunacharsky, who died in Menton, France, on December 26, have been transported to Moscow today. Government officials and many of Lunacharsky's relatives and friends were at the station to welcome Lunacharsky's coffin. The entire city of Moscow flew flags at half-mast in mourning. Lunacharsky's coffin was carried off the train by Litvinov and others. Another 2nd dispatch: Lunacharsky's remains were buried in Red Square today. More than 100,000 people participated in the burial ceremony, including Kalinin, Molotov, Kaganovich, etc. The People's Commissar of Education, Bubnov, delivered a speech on behalf of the government. Lunacharsky's ashes were buried in the Kremlin wall.

So, the great modern writer Lunacharsky has been dead for almost two weeks, and our country has only just received this little bit of news｜I will briefly describe Lunacharsky's life and his contributions to scholarship, to express my condolences.

Lunacharsky was born in 1876

near Poltava. His family were large landowners, but some say he was born in Kiev in 1878. His mother was Russian, and his father was Polish. Little is known about his childhood. In his own writings, he said that at the age of seven, he threw a religious icon on the ground, expressing atheistic thoughts. But his mother was a religious believer and hoped that her son would become a pastor, which resulted in her great disappointment. After graduating from middle school, he was limited by his circumstances and went abroad to university, where he learned that many exiled scholars were gathered in Switzerland. Later, he joined the "Labor Liberation Society," which was related to Plekhanov and others. He then went to Paris to study Marxism and art theory. Finally, he returned to Russia, but was exiled to Vologda. After three exiles, he returned to his homeland during the March Revolution. After the revolution, Lunacharsky held important positions until his death, at the age of only fifty-odd years.

His scholarship was very profound. From natural sciences to all fields of art, he was deeply knowledgeable. He made rich contributions to philosophy, literary criticism, and drama, and especially to aesthetics, he had outstanding insights. In his short biography of Lunacharsky, Ozaki Kei says that he possessed all kinds of excellent elements: a clear mind, a strong spirit, poetic emotions, and extremely quick comprehension—all were manifestations of outstanding talent. This is very appropriate.

Lunacharsky has now passed away before reaching old age. He left a vast amount of works for future generations to study. Although his theories have been criticized and considered not very correct, he has been working hard to correct them in recent years. This humility in accepting criticism from others is especially admirable.

In any case, Lunacharsky was always a pioneer of the times. We who study literature should regard his death as a great loss to the academic world and deeply regret it.

In a Girls' School

— Li Huiying

Quite a while had passed, and no one was entering or leaving the school. In the large courtyard, only the principal and the seven of us who had no homes to go to were holding on. The courtyard, which was usually lively, was now filled with endless silence, extremely deserted. Therefore, the sound of the autumn wind sweeping the fallen leaves on the ground clearly penetrated our eardrums.

Our hearing, at least at this time, dominated our entire bodies. It can be said that we were constantly listening intently. As long as some kind of noisy sound came through, we would all lose color and our hearts would beat uncontrollably. We were afraid of the impending encounter｜｜Japanese soldiers were about to come from Changchun to take over the provincial capital.

Changchun had already been forcibly occupied by Japanese soldiers two days ago. From any point of view, there was a need and possibility for them to continue to invade Jilin. However, the military authorities of the provincial capital did not make any defensive preparations under such tense circumstances, let alone prepare for war. Since there were no troops to resist the Japanese soldiers, the provincial capital could only be forcibly occupied by the Japanese!

The students, teachers, and staff of the city, as well as those who lived closer to home, all returned home yesterday. The school fell into a state of anarchy, and the whole city was in great chaos. The streets were full of people, carts, horses, and belongings, moving from Dongguan to Xiguan, from Jiangbei to Jiangnan, and from the city to the countryside. After a period of chaotic moving, no one knew which area was safe.

The principal looked even more pitiful than us, as if the Japanese soldiers' eyes were specially used to find the principal of the girls' school. As soon as they arrived, they would grab him first. He was terrified, his face pale, pacing helplessly in the principal's office. He also had a home and could return to it, but he had a duty and could not leave an empty school and run away.

Our dormitory was deathly still, but our hearts were, on the contrary, unusually active and unable to calm down. I thought to myself: After the Japanese soldiers occupy the provincial capital, they will definitely occupy the outer counties as well, and there will definitely be no troops to resist in the outer counties. That's for sure, in a few days we will become slaves of a conquered nation like the Koreans. But I couldn't help but think of the troops in the city. Why didn't they take any action? The state raises soldiers to defend against foreign aggression, and the people pay taxes to demand national security. Now that the Japanese soldiers are really about to occupy the city, there is no action at all. What is going on?：：：

"Wei, listen!"

I was lost in thought when I heard someone call my name. Without bothering to identify who was calling me, I just listened quietly. Indeed, there was a faint sound, but I couldn't determine where it was coming from.

After a while, the sound became louder, "Woo：：："

On the street, there was a sudden burst of more chaotic noise, shouting, running, and even crying. The "Woo：：：" sound was suppressed.

"What's going on?"

"Have they come in?"

Some of us said this in panic, and everyone's minds became tense, thinking that disaster was imminent. We couldn't escape, so we waited.

The "Woo：：：" sound grew louder at this time, and the sound of people shouting subsided, as if the sound was spreading from the sky. We ran to the center of the courtyard and looked up at the sky. Sure enough, it was an airplane. Although we had never seen this thing before, we had recognized it in pictures long ago. Seeing the sun flag on the body of the plane, we knew it was a Japanese plane. This was probably the reason why the people on the street shouted even louder.

"God!" someone shouted, shouting really miserably. At this moment, the door of a classroom opened with a "Ya" sound. We turned our eyes to look. The one who opened the door was our principal. While pressing his hat tightly on his head with both hands, he quickly hid under the lectern. He was probably afraid that the Japanese in the plane would see him, right? No, he was preventing the bombs dropped from the plane. He must have thought that the hat and the desk could protect his body.

Thinking of bombs, we also felt our own danger. The plane flew away, but our fear deepened. We thought that after the plane came, the Japanese soldiers who took the train from Changchun might be arriving at the train station soon.

What should we do? We had been worried and afraid every day for three days. Today, fear had finally begun. What should we do in the future?

Why is our Chinese territory being forcibly occupied by Japanese soldiers? Why should our compatriots be trampled on by Japanese soldiers? Where can we seek protection for our lives?

Thinking is useless. Thinking about it and thinking about it, we still can't get an answer and can't save ourselves from the dangerous situation. So we just stop thinking about it. Trying to escape is not a good way either, unless (

escaping from the world, otherwise we can't escape this disaster.

This time, I relaxed my mind and wasn't afraid of anything. I even had the leisure to run to the classroom and pull the principal out from under the lectern, laughing and saying:

"Principal Wang, the plane left a long time ago. You really have ideas. Why didn't you teach us first?"

I was still joking with him at this time. In fact, we were all equally pitiful people!

Amusing Metaphors

— Shu

(I)

As soon as you mention "the end of the Ming Dynasty," many people will feel a headache, because the materials from that time, when read now, are quite heartbreaking. In fact, that's not entirely the case. Although there are many "heartbreaking" things, there are also quite a few "appetizing" articles. At the beginning of the New Year, auspiciousness is paramount, so I'm setting aside the "heartbreaking" and talking about "amusing metaphors." "Amusing metaphors" means that many things are not said directly, and many things are not handled directly, but are explained with humorous and interesting metaphors. The intellectuals at the end of the Ming Dynasty were most adept at this, and it can truly be said that they were "unprecedented and unsurpassed." This is one of the characteristics of literature at the end of the Ming Dynasty, and it was also created by the objective environment at that time. This is the preface.

(II)

Feng Qi's letter to Yang Mengshan, a senior official, says: "Now that the court is discussing restoration, the elders are in the midst of the wind and waves, while you are letting your hair down and lying on Peach Blossom Ridge. This is like shaking your clothes in the clouds, looking down on the mundane world and the dust of the wild horses, which is laughable." This metaphor is truly beautiful. "Letting your hair down" is such a celestial attitude; "lying on Peach Blossom Ridge" is such a poetic realm, except that they can't see the "dust." This way of scolding is much more "aesthetically pleasing" than the straightforward scolding of people like us. This kind of article can be considered "the art of scolding people." What do you think, Mr. Liang Shiqiu and the gentlemen of "Yifeng"?

(III)

Yang Xunji said to others: "When I look at poetry, I don't judge it by its style or genre, but only seek to express one's feelings directly and describe the scenery realistically. If women and children can all understand what is meant, then it is considered a good poem. As for those who embellish and piece together, stubbornly picking up the spittle of the ancients, they are just puppets with false strings, and I don't take them." "Picking up the spittle of the ancients" is a very mediocre way of scolding, but when you add "embellishing and piecing together" and "puppets with false strings," it becomes an aesthetically pleasing article of scolding. This is truly an amusing metaphor. I humbly offer this to the current "puppets with false strings" of today's poets, novelists, and even magazine editors.

(IV)

Li Kai told his son: "Writing in bed and reading books in bed are familiar situations; composing poems at a banquet and riding horses on the mountain are dangerous things; I tell you the places where I have gained and lost in my life." An entire philosophy of life is said clearly and cleanly in the amusing metaphor of "writing in bed" and "riding horses on the mountain," which are picked up casually.

Two Brothers (82)

— By Maupassant, Translated by Li Weike

One morning, when he had finished washing up, the maid Josephine handed him the letter of appointment.

His first feeling was the same as that of a death row inmate who heard the notice of commutation; he immediately felt that his pain was alleviated by the thought of this long journey and this quiet life, constantly rocked by the flowing sea, constantly drifting, constantly escaping.

He now lived at home like a silent, cautious outsider. From the night he revealed the filthy secret he had discovered to his younger brother, he felt that he had severed his last relationship with his family. He often regretted that he should not have told Jian about this. He thought of himself as an ugly, vile, and sinister person, but he felt a little more comfortable because he had said it.

He had never met his mother or brother's eyes since then. Their eyes adopted an astonishing mobility and a trickery like enemies afraid of encountering each other, avoiding each other. He always thought: "What did she say to Jian? Did she admit it or deny it? What does my brother think? What does he think of her, what does he think of me?" He was annoyed because he couldn't guess. He hardly talked to them now, except in front of Roland, to avoid his questions.

When he received the letter of appointment, he showed it to his family that day. His father, who was easily made happy by everything, clapped his hands and congratulated him. Jian replied in a serious tone, but with a soul full of joy:

"I sincerely congratulate you, because I know that there are many competitors for this. You must have succeeded because of the letters of recommendation from your professors."

And his mother muttered with her head down:

"I'm glad you succeeded."

After lunch, he went to the shipping company's office to inquire about the various procedures; he found out the name of the doctor on the "Picardy" mail ship, which was sailing tomorrow, so that he could consult him about all the details of his new life and the special circumstances he would encounter in the future.

Dr. Pirait was on the ship at that time. He went on board and was received in a small room on the mail ship by a young man with golden yellow whiskers who resembled his brother. They talked for a long time.

In the resounding depths of the large ship, we heard a vague, continuous, and constant din, the sound of cargo falling into the cabin, and footsteps, voices, the movement of loading machines, the whistle of the foreman, the sound of iron chains being dragged or reeled on the wheels by the power of steam ｜ this power made the entire ship tremble slightly ｜ all mixed together.

But when Biel said goodbye to his colleague and walked back to the street, a new sorrow struck him and surrounded him like the mist that came from the end of the world and raced across the sea! This elusive, dense mist carried a mysterious impurity, like the infectious breath of a barbaric and miasmic land.

Even in his most painful moments, he had never felt like this, sinking into the gutter of suffering. This was because the final rift had been made; he was left alone. When he dug away all the sources of tenderness from his heart, he did not feel the poverty of a homeless dog that suddenly occupied him.
