Review of Last Year's Yarn and Cotton Market

Creating the Lowest Record in Ten Years

Last year (22nd year of the Republic) the Shanghai yarn and cotton market carried on the depressed atmosphere of the 21st year and remained sluggish. Since the September 18th Incident, the vast market of the three northeastern provinces was lost. The January 28th Shanghai Incident also weakened the southeastern market. Last year, in the early spring, the Japanese army first invaded Yuguan, then seized Rehe. The cotton yarn market was greatly impacted. Spring sales should have seen some improvement, but rural bankruptcy, silkworm cocoon failures, and the hardship of the villagers greatly reduced purchasing power, resulting in approximately 150,000 bales of yarn stored in Shanghai, causing the yarn market to appear precarious. All of this was caused by the Japanese.

Faced with the severity of the situation and the imminent threat to their foundation, manufacturers convened a national yarn factory meeting to discuss relief measures. As a result, it was resolved that from April 21st to May 20th, all would uniformly reduce work by 23%. At the time, the market was stimulated and rose slightly, but actual sales to customers remained weak and sluggish, still suffering from oversupply. Trademarked yarn fell directly from 205 or 206 yuan to 190 yuan.

In mid-June and July, US President Roosevelt implemented an inflationary monetary policy, and American cotton once saw an upswing, rising from 0.06 to 0.10 and then to 0.12. However, the gold market crashed and exchange rates soared. Calculating silver prices, they were actually cheaper. However, the cotton market and yarn market were inversely proportional. As inventories became increasingly thin, and sources were scarce, speculators seized the opportunity to manipulate the market, squeezing out short sellers. In the Chenhua era, in July and August, the highest price reached 48 or 49 yuan. Unexpectedly, a big tree attracts the wind. When news came that Chinese Finance Minister Song Ziwen had signed a loan agreement to purchase cotton and wheat on credit, it was like a thunderbolt from a clear sky, causing a sharp drop of more than one yuan. However, the buyers' desire to squeeze out short sellers did not die, so the cotton market was still higher than the yarn market.

Gradually, in September and October, the yarn market followed the same trajectory. As grain prices were low, new cotton increased by one-third, rainfall was adequate, and harvests were abundant, sellers gradually increased. At the same time, the US government estimated an increase on August 8th, and market prices trended downward. The world cotton industry was uniformly shaken. The trademarked yarn market became increasingly bad. Stored yarn was still difficult to reduce, and there were 20,000 to 30,000 bales of yarn put into warehouses. As the cotton market loosened, the yarn market's decline became more rapid. Therefore, in September, it broke through the 180 yuan mark. The trademarked cotton price reached a low point of 39.40 yuan.

At this time, there was talk of a cotton industry control committee under the National Economic Council. According to rumors in the market, it had great power to maintain cotton yarn prices. As a result, some well-informed people and a certain yarn factory contacted and purchased large quantities to await good sales. The almost lifeless yarn price benefited from this large purchase and rose from 179 yuan to 184 or 185 yuan. The Cotton Industry Control Committee was established on October 16th. There were many rumors in the market. Another Hexing Company was organized to take in all of the more than 20,000 bales of yarn stored at the exchange. With this assistance, the market naturally stabilized for many days.

On November 6th, the Yarn and Fabric Exchange, by order of the Ministry of Industry, refused to accept new cotton yarn deliveries from customers to stabilize yarn prices. At the time, it caused a great storm, as it was believed that sellers had all prepared actual goods and were not speculative, but were not allowed to deliver goods. They could only cover their positions in the market, and the market would soar. Brokers also refused to accept the situation due to contractual relationships. As a result, the atmosphere was extremely tense. The market was suspended for three days, and the directors went to Beijing to petition. Later, a compromise was reached, and the market reopened, increasing the special margin for buyers by 22 yuan. However, speculators, seeing the unfavorable trend, did not dare to act rashly. In early November, many empty positions were sold off every day.

On November 20th, the sudden change in the situation in Fujian and Zhejiang dealt a heavy blow to the future of the yarn market. As the largest customer of Chinese yarn, southern China held a unique position. Once military action occurred, the sales market would be hopeless. General spot goods merchants were even more panicked. As a result, those holding goods had no choice but to sell in the futures market. There was no other way out. Cracks appeared, and the falling trend was hidden. A certain large factory was also constrained by economic factors and had no intention of taking delivery. According to market rumors, the Cotton Control Committee also abandoned its decision not to take delivery. With such a large number of chips being released, it was like a dike collapsing, rushing for thousands of miles. In one day, it fell by 4 or 5 yuan. By December 7th, it had broken through the 70 yuan mark, creating a new low in the past ten years. (According to trademarked yarn since its opening, the lowest price was 121 taels and 9 qians in October 11th year of the Republic for this month's price. At this time, trademarked yarn was a 16-count Human Trademark brand, lower by 12.5 yuan. However, the previous price included the pass fee of 2.84 taels.)

In the midst of this sharp drop in trademarked yarn, the exchange, in order to maintain stability, increased the special margin many times, which was unprecedented since the exchange's inception. The exchange's total trademarked yarn turnover for the year was 9,700,3650 bales, an increase of 4,266,950 bales compared to last year. Trademarked cotton turnover was 24,339,300 dan, an increase of 9,738,000 dan compared to last year.

Grain Factories Bought Near-Term Flour

Yesterday, the flour market, after opening in the morning, showed an initial stable and then flat trend in each month's market. As foreign wheat quotations, Chicago improved by about 0.20 to 0.30 yuan, and Canada improved by nearly 0.10 yuan, the atmosphere in each month's market was slightly firmer at the opening, better than the previous day's closing price by 0.005 yuan. Then, as trading in each month became very light, with little movement from customer groups and no speculative activity from outside the industry, the market situation became flat again. The lowest price in June fell back to 2.0925 yuan. By the time the afternoon session opened, trading in each month was even quieter, with only 60,000 to 70,000 bags in and out. However, the factories bought near-term positions, and each month rose, improving by more than 0.01 yuan compared to the morning. As a result, this month improved by 0.0075 yuan, February improved by 0.0075 yuan, March improved by 0.005 yuan, April improved by 0.0075 yuan, and May and June each improved by 0.01 yuan.

Most Open Positions in Wheat Futures

Yesterday, the wheat futures market showed a slightly stable trend, as foreign wheat quotations improved by 0.10 to 0.30 yuan, and market sentiment was slightly better. However, trading in each month was really light, with most positions being opened empty and no activity. This situation was entirely due to settlement relationships, causing many to stop trading. As a result, this month improved by 0.02 yuan compared to the previous day, March was slightly down by 0.01 yuan, and the rest had no comparison. Current wheat sales were still smooth, and the standards for traders to buy were gradually opening up. It is estimated that Yao wheat opened at 4 yuan, and Bengbu wheat opened at 3.99 yuan, totaling 3,000 bags, which were handled by Fuxin and Shendah.

Late Rice Sales Dull, Continuing to Fall by 0.06 to 0.07 Yuan

(South Shanghai) Yesterday, there were still about 50 sources from various groups, totaling more than 7,000 shi, of which late rice was the most. Only about 1,500 to 1,600 bags were purchased by the northern and southern groups, so sentiment was unusually weak, and market prices fell by 0.06 to 0.07 yuan. The stores in this street had few customers due to the continuous cold rain, and market prices also fell by several points to near ruler price. Thick geng rice was the same. Duyang top-quality goods were still lacking and unchanged.

(North Shanghai) Yesterday, 25 or 26 arrivals from various sources below the river. Various sales in the market were slightly up due to the morning rain. There were few buyers on the market, and there was no way to sell. The goods delivered yesterday were all fixed on the previous day. Few transactions opened on the market. Market prices were similar to the previous day.

Indica Rice Accumulation Very Thick

Yesterday, the situation in the guest indica market was still active, but there were more than 100,000 bags of goods in the market, and there were also large quantities of foreign rice. Various cargo owners had the intention of finishing up early to end the year. Sales have not increased. Although the locals are interested in buying, they all tighten the pace, not releasing prices and freely buying. Stockists have mostly switched to handling various rice below the river and are purchasing unpolished rice and rice grains from the mainland and producing areas to prepare for long-term storage. The market is still seeing demand exceeding supply, and the market price remains flat and soft. However, although the cargo owners want to sell, the market price is not willing to be very low. The prices sold in the market yesterday were similar to the previous market. It is estimated that the Jiangxi machine late rice from this street sold 112 bags at a price of 7.10 yuan, and Hunan machine oil sold 300 bags at a price of 7.25 yuan to 7.19 yuan. The Fuzhou group sold 100 bags of Hunan machine Jing at a price of 6.50 yuan, and Jing 425 bags at a price of 5.90 yuan to 5.75 yuan, and 150 bags of red unpolished rice at a price of 5.55 yuan to 5.525 yuan. There were no other sales. However, the Fujian group has a strong appetite, and if the situation stabilizes slightly in the future, there will definitely be a batch of sales.

Sugar Market: New Sliced Green Down Another 0.3 Yuan

Turnover Over 1,700 Pieces

Yesterday, the trend in the sugar market was weak, and there was still no sign of a turnaround. The association set the price of second-grade coarse sugar at 19.05 yuan, down 0.05 yuan from the previous day, but there was a shortage of outbound goods. If there are no unexpected changes, the trend should be stable. Transshipment goods were priced higher at 6.40 yuan. No. 8 Dutch red sugar was priced at 15.20 yuan. Tate & Lyle sugar was priced at the original price, and there was still a possibility of a continued decline. The Zhenji No. 1 native fine white sugar was still priced at 18.10 yuan, and the remaining Nos. 2, 3, and 4 were reduced accordingly. The arrival of Zhangdiao green sugar was scarce. The Jinan wheel only had over 130 bags, which would all result in losses at market prices. Buyers were hoping for a good price, but the supply of Chaozhou green sugar was continuous and large. There were no sales yesterday, so it was not easy to be optimistic. The Guangdong-Chaozhou group opened another 1,700 boxes of sliced green sugar, priced at 8.50 yuan, down 0.30 yuan from the previous price.

Northern Goods

Xinghua Longan Arrivals Suddenly Increase

Since the Fujian Incident, in addition to Xiamen, where foreign ships continued to arrive as usual, the Chinese ships from Xinghua and Quanzhou were suspended to avoid danger. Last month, Lisheng chartered the foreign ship Shenyou to Xingquan. It returned to Shanghai yesterday. A total of over 5,000 pieces of longan arrived in Xingquan. To prevent being involved, they were rushing to ship to Shanghai, of which Xinghua goods accounted for one-fifth.

Oil Market: Soybean Oil Telegram Suddenly Rises 0.4 Yuan

The Local Market Also Follows Up 0.3 Yuan

The bean oil market has always been affected by the telegram fluctuations, rising or falling. If the telegram reported a terrible drop, the local oil situation would also collapse. Yesterday, the telegram reported that the current oil suddenly rose by 0.4 yuan, and "futures oil also rose, please refer to the market price column," causing general sentiment to fluctuate, and inventories had dried up in the falling price, so the market increased quickly. Compared to the previous disk, the market has risen by 0.3 yuan, with an estimated turnover of 100 pieces of Lunlian soybean oil, priced at 10.07 yuan, and 500 pieces of road goods at 10.03 yuan. 50 pieces of Lunlian Qiyou was priced at 10.05 yuan, and 250 pieces of road goods was priced at 10.035 yuan.

Metal: New Iron Products Continuously Arriving

New iron products, such as angle iron, foreign yuan bars, ribbed steel, foreign plates, and foreign squares, etc., have arrived in large quantities at various foreign wharves in Pudong and Puxi in the past two days (estimated to be about 2,000 tons). The standards of each market have little hope of rising during this closing period.

Zinc Sheet Iron Small Business Still Booming

The recent small business in zinc sheet iron is very booming. This street's thermos bottle factories, enamel factories, iron factories, etc., all have some embellishments. The market for 3'x6' is priced at 10.05 yuan per dan, and 2'x6' is priced at 11.05 yuan per dan. (The above are genuine goods.) Sub-genuine goods are priced at 10.025 yuan per dan for 3'x6' and 11 yuan for 2'x6'.

Shortage of 90-Pound American Tinplate Spot Goods

The recent shortage of 90-pound American tinplate spot goods is very serious. Although customer manufacturers have transactions, they have no goods to buy. The market is estimated at 15.4 yuan per box (without iron shell) and 15.8 yuan (with iron shell), up 0.2 yuan from the previous price.

Market for Blue Lead Still Depressed

The market for blue lead has been idle recently. Although arrivals are not vigorous, there are few transactions, so the market has not progressed much. It is still priced at 16.12 yuan per dan, while native lead only sells for 15.78 yuan. This street's printing houses, tin foil factories, etc., have small embellishments, while yellow dan factories, paint companies, etc., are very deserted.

Silk and Tea

Raw Silk Sales to America Continue to Decline

New York silk factories' silk sales have decreased significantly; the world economy is unstable; silk sales are sluggish; New York silk factories suffered considerable losses in business last year; inventories are piling up; although the labor strike last winter was resolved, only 50-60% of the machines are operating; raw silk consumption has greatly decreased. Yesterday, the local Jardine Matheson received a report from the New York Silk Association stating that the total raw silk consumption of all silk factories in New York City last month (i.e., December of last year) was 26,959 bales, compared to 35,944 bales in the previous month (November), a decrease of 8,985 bales.

35 Bundles of Cocoon Floss Transported to Inland Lake Region. Recently, cotton merchants in the inland lake region have continued to demand white cocoon floss. Yesterday, Jardine Matheson's silk thread company had 35 bundles of Wuxi white cocoon floss, which were loaded and shipped to Pinghu in the Huzhou region.

Artificial Silk Market Continues to Show Weakness. Yesterday, the local artificial silk market continued to show weakness. Hangzhou silk factories imported 35 cases of first and second grade "Liu Hai," "Golden Eagle," and "Pagoda" brands for January and February futures, priced at 208.50 to 192.25 yuan net.

Chinese and Foreign Silk Merchants Still Adopt a Cautious Stance. The European and American raw silk markets show no sign of recovery; silk sales remain stagnant. New York silk weaving factories have sufficient silk in stock to meet demand; Lyon silk factories purchase only what they need. Japanese silk is abundant and prices remain low. Sales of Chinese silk factories remain sluggish. European firms in Shanghai generally maintain a policy of small purchases at set prices. Chinese silk merchants have suffered huge losses, and the market atmosphere continues to be cautious. Yesterday, only British firms continued to make small spot transactions, with Jardine Matheson, etc., importing 14 bales of yellow and white high-grade silk, with prices remaining weak.

Ruiping

Economic Morality

— Bin Fu

After the New Year, the temperature on the thermometer has continued to drop, and the northwest wind on the streets has become increasingly fierce. Didn't we see snowflakes in this city the night before last? What lies ahead of us is another long stretch of severely cold days! Of course, the rich will not think of the hardships of the severe cold. When they go out, they have "airtight" cars, and at home, they have warm electric heaters. However, the hardworking masses are still treading on ice and frost, enduring the cold and working continuously.

Naturally, hardworking people cannot help but envy the comfortable lives of the rich, and lament their own misfortune. Perhaps they will even complain like this: "Now is truly a world of money worship. Those with money are the most respected people in society, and those without money are the lowest."

Yes, this statement may be correct, because the reality is indeed so.

As the saying goes, "A son of a thousand gold should not sit under a leaning eaves." Ordinary wealthy people, relying on the legacy of their ancestors, own a lot of land and stocks, and rely on collecting interest and dividends to obtain various sources of income, passing their leisurely years. How can society not respect them? However, they have not spent even a hair's breadth of effort to work for the country and society.

Although the reality is like this, if we observe from the perspective of modern economic morality, these people, no matter how rich and fulfilling their lives are, are morally the lowest class of people!

Conversely, ordinary hardworking men and women, work hard every day and get meager wages, barely enough to maintain their minimum living standards, or even inevitably suffer from hunger and cold. They are truly poor and miserable, but from the perspective of economic morality, they are the most noble and most respectable.

The Japanese economist Tokuzo Fukuda said: "... Everything in heaven and earth has power, but it is useless if the power is not exerted. Therefore, the existence of everything in heaven and earth requires exerting power to maintain it." He also said: "... Many people who hold land or securities, have herds of cattle and horses at home, and their income ranges from thousands to tens of thousands of yuan, are mostly people who do not work at all. And a poor family who work together; the money they use, even a thread or half a thread, is the result of their blood and sweat. From the perspective of the whole society, although it is only a slight contribution, their contribution is considerable when accumulated. Compared with those who sit on thick assets and do nothing, their personality is ultimately more noble."

The chaos in society today can be said to be mostly due to this lack of economic morality. Not to mention the capitalists who own millions of capital, even people below the middle class are psychologically filled with ideas of seeking luck and speculation, and are unwilling to earnestly support themselves and be content with poverty. If we simply count the number of people in this city who specialize in speculation and profit-making and live on debt, I am afraid we will get an astonishing number.

The world today is completely centered on economics, so our actions and thoughts should naturally not go against the principles of modern economics, but the principles of economics do not call us to "worship money." It calls us to abide by economic morality. Therefore, our most noble hardworking people, let us not covet the life of these parasites, let us not harbor the mentality of seeking luck and speculation. Let us serve society with our own blood and sweat, support ourselves, endure hunger, endure cold, and work hard to study, and strengthen our own strength!

A Frail Snowman Meets Intense Sunlight

— Yi Zhang

Spring Dream

— Yi

| Diary Excerpts |

Last night, before going to bed, I mistakenly took too much quinine. The medicine was potent, my head felt swollen and very uncomfortable, and it was not easy to fall asleep. I regretted eating medicine randomly.

However, I dreamed after falling asleep, and woke up from the dream. After waking up, I fell asleep and dreamed again. By the time it dawned, I had dreamed three or four times. And each dream had a constructed story, which was really strange. After dawn, I knew that the dreams were due to eating too much quinine. I thought of telling the world: If you want to dream, it is best to eat a lot of quinine.

First dream: || When I woke up, the aftertaste was still very clear, but I can't remember it anymore, which is a pity!

Second dream: It seemed to be in my hometown || or it didn't seem to be my hometown, but somewhere else || by the water || at the pier, a huge animal was lying in the mud. By its side on the beach, dogs and crows were fighting for food. People on the shore were scrambling to watch, and I was also watching on the shore. I was just watching the excitement in my heart, and had no other thoughts. Suddenly, a beast of some kind || I couldn't remember what it was called for a moment, but I always knew in my heart what kind of beast it was || like a horse and a tiger, its front legs looked like two human hands. It lifted the hind legs of the lying animal from the mud, wanting to tear its body into two pieces. The animal suddenly rose up and cried out. Someone said, "Man-bear, man-bear ||" People ran, and I ran too. But the man-bear chased onto the shore, and now it was only chasing me. How could this be? I ran as fast as I could, not knowing how I ran to a place where there was a small peninsula shape ahead, surrounded by water on three sides, a completely desperate situation. I decided in my heart that this was not right, and stopped. But people shouted at me with laughter. I ran up the hillside. Looking back, the man-bear was brandishing its claws in the peninsula-shaped place. I quickly ran into a place that looked like a city. A big man gesticulated and said, "That man-bear is really fierce || So-and-so went up and pounced, the strength is almost the same." Immediately, a scene of So-and-so (a boxer I knew) wrestling with the man-bear appeared on my brain like a silver screen. But I was still running with an unsettled soul. I ran to a place where I heard someone say, "It's fake, it's a person dressed up ||" Suddenly, surrounded by many people, I saw an earthen cave. Inside, the "man-bear" was wearing a big bamboo hat, its hands tied behind its back and struggling. I thought it really looked like a man-bear. Its face looked scorched black as if it had been burned. At the same time, I felt like it had been burned by fire. I woke up with a start.

What is this symbolizing? I woke up and began to ponder. Although I couldn't figure it out for a while, I always thought in my heart that it was some kind of symbol.

Third dream: In the backstage of a variety show || I can't remember what kind of variety show it was at this time, || people were in a mess. I came out to the front of the stage, and saw a clearing in front of the stage, surrounded by a crowd of people, all standing and crowding. In the crowd on the right, a burly man in black suddenly pointed at a young man in a suit and loudly asked the staff backstage: "Is he one of your staff here? My uncle || I don't know why he was there too || shouted, "Chen XX? Forget it." I looked over there, and the burly man in black was holding him, revealing a pistol. The pistol was extended from behind him to his chest to hold him down and threaten him. I don't know why, but I was afraid of being implicated and ran to the left in a hurry, entering a factory hall. My uncle, wearing a long robe and mandarin jacket that he only wore on the first day of the New Year, stood on the corridor and said loudly, "If you can't get a bottle of snuff, you come to make trouble!" I saw the young man in the suit sitting dejectedly on the chair next to him, his face covered in blood stains. It was obvious that he had been beaten by the burly man in black. I understood in my heart that it was because of a bottle of snuff. I couldn't help but get angry and scolded, "Why do you have to do this for a bottle of snuff?" I said sympathetically, "Stealing snuff is not a crime, just like we scholars stealing books from bookstores, what crime is it?" But as I said that, I immediately felt like I had insulted myself and walked away.

When I got outside || on the road || someone suddenly hugged me around the waist and shouted "Got you!" I was shocked in my heart. Without asking why, I tried hard to avoid him and ran away as fast as I could. That person was chasing me. In my heart, I felt as panicked as if I had met an enemy. Running to the fence of the countryside, several good friends came head-on at the turning point, looking like they were going to help me. I shouted loudly, and with a backhand punch, I knocked the person to the ground. "Kill him, destroy the evidence!" everyone shouted. I used a sharp metal weapon of some kind to strike the person's head. Everyone looked and saw that the person was originally our neighbor! I pointed at him and counted his crimes, saying how his father and brothers, like my eldest brother and fifth brother, were so good to me, and now you have changed your mind and want to harm me? He seemed to repent and said some pitiful words, and even corrected me, saying that his fifth brother was his second brother. I couldn't help but feel sympathetic. I didn't care about killing him and told him to leave quickly. I also woke up. I was still thinking in my head, what if he brought more people to retaliate, wouldn't that be terrible?

It's really a strange dream || I want to kill someone? However, when that person wanted to harm me, if I didn't kill him, I would be harmed by him || I didn't expect that I couldn't implement the new morality of "long-term resistance" even in my dreams.

Moon

— Lüdi

I am not a poet, but I am so fond of the bright moon. I often lean on the windowsill of my bedroom alone, gazing at her obsessively, to the point where it has become a habit and I suffer from insomnia.

That was in my hometown, already five years ago.

My younger brother and I's bedroom was at the very back of the house. Opening the east-facing window on a moonlit night, the patch of woods after the ridge vaguely swayed in the wind, dancing so sparsely. There were no clouds in the sky, and the bright moon shone on the entire quiet countryside. You could forget everything, forget the pain of life.

Blue sky, intoxicating breeze blowing. In summer, fireflies twinkled like stars in the fields. In autumn, although it is a relatively desolate season, the sky is high and the air is clear, and the moon is bright as a picture. You will not feel the sorrow of aging. In winter, white light reflects white woods, white houses, white fields, white firewood piles, and you yourself may be dissolved by the current scenery and turned into a white plaster statue.

It has been five years already. I can't help but cry out, how quickly time passes!

Throwing myself into the embrace of the city, I have not seen the moon once in five years.

The sky in Shanghai is so small. Whether looking out from the window of a small building, or standing on the third-floor sundeck, it is such a small corner that you cannot see the stars or the moon.

The world in Shanghai has no night. I am afraid that the night is brighter than the daytime || on the surface; the electric lights are so dazzling, and the electric red lights are so charming. Although I always return home at midnight every day, I cannot see the stars or the moon. For five years.

On New Year's Eve, three friends and I returned from North Sichuan Road in the cold wind. Everyone walked with their heads buried, stepping on their own shadows that were sometimes long and sometimes short, so cautiously, as if mourning the fleeting 1933.

Walking past the quiet roads, the indifferent patrolmen stood listlessly by the large glass cabinets, with their heads hanging down, not caring about us passersby. Walking past the bustling streets, there were traces of Santa Claus, and the songs of jazz, as if we passersby had been abandoned. We kept our heads down, and no one paid attention to their companions, or perhaps the dinner party gave everyone unspeakable hidden pain.

My companions reached their homes, nodded and said goodbye to me. I seemed to have forgotten that it was time to sleep. The rickshaw pullers greeted me eagerly, but I didn't look at them and walked with my head buried.

It was already midnight. There were no pedestrians on the road, and the wind blew piercingly. I occasionally raised my head and took a long breath. I couldn't believe it || hanging above my head was the moon that I hadn't seen for five years.

She was as well as ever, so bright, so radiant. She sent me home from North Sichuan Road with such affection || she had even followed me closely for five years without interruption.

Moon, you have not changed your attitude in five years.

Regarding "Talking About Careers"

— Zhi

After I read "Wen Bing"'s article "Talking About Careers" in "Talks," I felt that the consciousness in that article was a bit vague, and the main argument was too far removed from the realities of social life. Therefore, I wrote an article "The Doctrine of Service First," pointing out that the doctrine of service first || dedication to work, enjoyment of work, perseverance in work || is a kind of self-deception that is close to joking in today's world, where the whole world is trapped in the panic of unemployment and joblessness.

My motivation for criticizing this kind of self-deception is very simple: In today's situation, where efforts to transform and reform China have almost ceased, we young people have the responsibility to sweep away all ambiguous concepts that are enough to deceive social consciousness. It is by no means a kind of "domineering" and casual scolding, as "Wen Bing" claims.

However, "Wen Bing" wrote a long article to answer me, and insisted on his "correct theory," saying: "Purely using deformed facts to overthrow my article's theory, but without pointing out the errors in my theory" ("Wen" Bing's original text). Here, the first question is: According to Wen Bing's logical method, are deformed facts still deformed facts, and is Wen Bing's theory still Wen Bing's theory? Are facts and theory not to be linked?

According to "Wen Bing"'s explanation: "... My article is to explore the light, to cross this deformed current stage, and to address the society we desire and the reasonable profession" ("Wen Bing"'s original text). Then the second question is: Can the "deformed current stage" be crossed? Without realistic social content, the theory that abandons the actual life in front of us and speaks with closed eyes to the "society we desire (?) and the reasonable profession (?)," what is the truthfulness of that theory, what is the practicality of that theory?

"Wen Bing" is indeed a young man who is "unwilling to stay in this deformed and dead current stage." "Wen Bing" wrote in the conclusion of the article "Talking About Careers": "What I hope is that friends who already have a profession and those who are seeking a profession and have confidence can thoroughly recognize the essence and importance of a profession, and not be careless." "Wen Bing" said a lot of great truths about dedication to work, enjoyment of work, and perseverance in work in the front of the article, and in the conclusion, he reminded friends with jobs and those looking for jobs like a preacher, not to be careless. Here, the third question is: In this "deformed and dead current stage," which profession can be respected, enjoyed, and persevered in? If not, then why did "Wen Bing" so sincerely remind and teach people not to be careless? Is this kind of reminder from Wen Bing also a statement after crossing this deformed current stage? I would like to ask "Wen Bing" to make another statement.

"Wen Bing" said that deformed facts cannot overthrow his "correct theory." Then, please "Wen Bing" give a normal fact of this day, this time, and this place as the basis for his "correct theory." However, I believe that in the entire deformed society, there are only facts of the type that 1) cannot take into account their own "interests," 2) their talents are not "commensurate," 3) and they are not "contributing" to society but are "harmful" (exactly the opposite of the three basic conditions in "Wen Bing"'s theory). Moreover, there are countless facts where some people cannot even find a job regardless of their interests, talents, or whether it is beneficial or harmful to society. Open your eyes and see, isn't this society a bloody picture of everyone grabbing for a bowl of rice? In this struggle for everyone, whoever has long breasts is the mother! If "Wen Bing"'s theory is correct, he should have seen this fact, and not said that charming "talents are suitable for professions, and professions are suitable for talents" dream while targeting the phantom of the three characters "respect, joy, and perseverance."

The fact is that there is no profession to talk about in this society now. Therefore, "Wen Bing" immediately declared that he was talking about the professions in the "future" society after exaggerating the current stage. I don't need to criticize this anymore, because the organization of the future society is still an existing form, or another form. I cannot predict that if it is another form of society, then there will be no so-called individual profession. The group participates in the work of a certain production sector under the needs of society. The needs of society determine the individual's work. "Wen Bing"'s great theory || respect, joy, perseverance || fundamentally violates the spirit of that era. If the form of the current society is still the form of the future society, then naturally "Wen Bing"'s theory will be appreciated. The fact is that none of the bosses of the current companies or stores do not hope that their partners are faithful to their professions, and who does not want their partners to hold the grand aspirations of "respect, joy, and perseverance" to the end. "Wen Bing" said: "But some are not so rigid, but advocate new facts." I interpret these so-called new facts (referring to "Wen Bing"'s theory) in this way.

I am only explaining that "Wen Bing"'s "Talking About Careers" is untenable, and there is no personal temper mixed in. If there is an opportunity to climb up, I will "look at you with new eyes."

XXX

— Wei Ba

In these years, it is really not easy to be an intellectual. It is difficult not only to write, but also to read. Opening a newspaper or magazine, you will always encounter the above symbols or blanks, making you feel like you are reading a "heavenly book."

Recently, I saw Shen Congwen's "Record of Ms. Ding Ling" in the Tianjin Guowen Weekly. The article is full of "X"s. The most places have even twenty or thirty X's in a row. However, the places where X is used are often extremely important, just like the blank spaces in newspapers. It is not that the reporter fell asleep and forgot to write. On the contrary, there is something eager to come out, ready to emerge. Therefore, readers have to use the method of reading the Book of Changes and hexagrams XX to deduce the news they want to know from the extremely simple symbols. Although the deduced news is not completely correct, it is not far from it. At least, at least the reader's level is improved as a result.

Some people say that this is the highest expression in literature. In the old literary criticism, is there not a saying that "not a word is written, but all the charm is obtained"? Verified by Buddhist philosophy, this statement is even more credible. At the Vulture Peak Assembly, the Buddha smiled while holding a flower, and only Kashyapa understood in his heart. Therefore, he passed on the robe and bowl and founded Zen Buddhism. Probably the greatest thing in the world is silence. Because all names and forms, once put into words, lose their true meaning. Therefore, babies are called the greatest poets. Ms. Bing Xin's poem says:

Babies are the greatest poets,

In their incomplete language,

They spit out the most complete verses. (The general idea is like this, the original text has been forgotten.)

This is being able to understand the meaning beyond words, but this kind of cleverness has also "existed since ancient times," and it is not considered a special creation, but it is now applied more universally. Let me copy a note from a predecessor as the end of this article.

Qing Liang Shaozhu's Two Kinds of Rank Yu'an's Random Notes Volume 2 Circle Letter Clause says: "A prostitute sent a letter to her lover. When opened, there was not a single word. First, she drew a circle, then a set of circles, then several circles in a row, then another circle, then two circles, then a full circle, then a half circle, and finally countless small circles. A nosy person wrote a poem on it, saying: 'I want to record my lovesickness, how can I record it? Draw a circle instead. The words are outside the circle, and the heart is inside the circle. I add circles closely, and you must know my intentions closely. The single circle is me, the double circle is you; the full circle is reunion, and the broken circle is separation. There is still endless lovesickness, draw circles all the way to the end.' Creating something out of nothing makes people can't help but smile."

(According to the last two sentences, if they are borrowed for modern use, they should be changed to "Turning something into nothing makes people want to cry without tears.")

My Own Job Introduction

A certain gentleman, a native of Nanjing, is now twenty-three years old. He has previously worked in the telephone engineering department and foreign machine shops. He has some experience in electrical matters. If there are any electrical circles or foreign machine shops in this city or other cities that need this kind of talent, please send a letter to Mr. Li, No. 1 Debei Lane, Fumin Road, in Shanghai City, for transfer to a certain gentleman. Hebei native, has been in Beiping for many years, is twenty-five years old, has a strong physique, is capable and efficient, and is fluent in writing. He has been trained in the army for more than a year, but has only recently arrived in Shanghai and does not know Shanghai dialect. He is now willing to guarantee the work of bodyguards, gatekeepers, and servants such as housekeepers and messengers. Correspondence address: Zhao Baoshan, No. 138 Yonghe Lane, Rehe Road, Xinjiang Road.

Ms. C, is twenty-three years old, a graduate of Xinhua Music and Physical Education School, and has worked as a teacher in primary and secondary schools for many years. She is good at literature and art. If there is a need for this kind of talent, she is willing to go to this city or other cities. Correspondence address: Shao Guoyao, Broker Association, No. 80 Avenue Edward. Mr. Liu Zhengji, a sophomore in the Department of Physics at the university, is now willing to serve as a mathematics and physics teacher in junior high school and elementary school, a mathematics and physics tutor for families, or a physics teacher in high school. He can be part-time or full-time, and the salary is half-paid as a volunteer. Correspondence address: Guanghua University (Da Xi Road).

Ms. Chengming, a native of Jiangsu, graduated from the normal school and has worked as a class teacher in primary school and junior high school and as a family teacher for many years. She is now willing to serve in the above two positions or as a clerk or copyist. The salary is above twenty yuan. Correspondence address: Wu Hanfang, No. 156 Shanhai Pass Road, this city.

Amateur Mailbox

Father's Debt

Editor Sir:

I am twenty-eight years old. My father passed away due to illness when I was four. Suddenly, the year before last, a person surnamed Mou came forward with a promissory note signed by my father during his lifetime, along with three title deeds, totaling a debt of one hundred silver dollars. From the date on the note, it has been thirty-six years. The intermediary on the note has also passed away. This year, that person surnamed Mou sent someone to demand the principal and at least an equivalent amount of interest. If ignored, they threatened legal action. However, since my childhood, my mother has told me that the land was originally our family's property but was sold due to economic difficulties during my father's lifetime. After my father passed away, the person surnamed Mou never came to our house to inquire or demand repayment. Later, after I grew up and got married, the person surnamed Mou never mentioned it. Now, my family is poor and life is difficult, making it hard to repay even if there were such a debt dispute. Moreover, this is an unclear matter that has been separated by so many years, making it difficult to think about. I was young and ignorant and do not understand worldly affairs. After thinking it over and over, I really have no solution.

Sir, you are a savior of society. I hope you will not hesitate to provide instructions on how to deal with this. Moreover, given that the dispute has been separated by so many decades, is it legally valid? I would be most grateful. Sincerely,

Respectfully wishing you well, Lu Zhenjin

Editor's Note: Regarding this issue, Mr. Lu should examine the promissory note to see if it is indeed in your father's handwriting. As a son, you should have the ability to distinguish whether your father’s writing is genuine or fake. Otherwise, you can compare it with other documents that are known to be genuine. Everyone's handwriting is different. Once compared, the authenticity can be immediately determined. If it is fake, then there is naturally no problem. If it is genuine, then thirty-six years is still not considered a loss of validity. As for not pursuing the debt after your father's death, that is also common. People take pity on orphans and widows and do not press for payment. Later, even though you grew up, you were still not well-established and did not make things too difficult. This is mostly due to their kindness, so how can you deny the debt based on that? As for your current poor family situation and difficult life, being unable to repay your father's debt is another issue. Current laws have restrictions on inheritance, but unfortunately, they were promulgated many years after your father's death, so they cannot be invoked. However, the other party also has shortcomings in their procedures. The debt was originally secured by land. Then the other party should have paid close attention to the land claimed as collateral. When your father sold the land during his lifetime, the other party should have immediately come forward to negotiate. Even if the friendship was deep and they didn't want to investigate deeply, they should have requested your father to issue a statement clarifying the situation and designating other collateral. Now, all these procedures are missing, making people doubt whether the debt was actually settled at the time. The reason why the promissory note was not returned may be that there was a declaration of loss and a procedure for issuing a receipt. Therefore, we believe that reconciliation is the best course of action. Consider repaying some amount, retrieving the promissory note, and eliminating future troubles. It is not cost-effective to go to court for a debt of one or two hundred dollars, especially since this dispute cannot be resolved in one or two court hearings!

Novel

Prison Diary (6)

— Wheels

14th

After waiting for several days for the exercise ground to dry, based on our experience, we know that it has been dry for one or two days. There is hope of being taken out for exercise. After the meal, I changed into my leather shoes and waited anxiously for the drum to be beaten to take us out. I tapped on the wall and asked Mr. Pi next door if there was any possibility of being taken out for exercise.

"Don't worry, Old Zhang. The sun is so good today. Yesterday, the day before yesterday, and the day before that were also good. The ground is dry. I guarantee you will be taken out for exercise!"

Indeed, I am afraid of being trapped by the rain, afraid of being trapped by the walls. The blue sky can only be seen as big as the window. Although philosophers see infinite things contained within the window frame, prisoners do not want this kind of infinity. They want to look left, right, up, and down, to touch everything soft and green with their eyes, to embrace endless green. The eyes have only this simple request. The spine, legs, and arms seem to be pressed down and cramped by the roof ridge. They just want a few minutes of freedom away from this small room to be supervised for a few days—exercise.

They want to breathe in a breath of fresh air, just like the lungs, to move them, to tremble them—just this small request, like a dog stretching its body after waking up from sleep.

Probably not only I am praying for the exercise leader to come like waiting for a god, but this god is not a god who saves all living beings.

An hour after the meal, Mr. Pi knocked on the wall. I was pacing back and forth at the time. I immediately concentrated my hearing and stood still, because the sound only comes through the wall hole at the top of the wall where the light is installed.

"Not guaranteed, Old Zhang—not reliable!"

If Mr. Pi says it's not reliable, I am also disappointed, because he only comes in the few minutes right after the meal, often before some people with bigger appetites have even finished their rice bowls, he comes to open the cell door and take people out for exercise. There is no hope after an hour. In fact, this is when it is possible to exercise. Running right after eating often makes people's stomachs ache. He doesn't care.

16th

It's raining again today. We haven't had any hope of exercise when the weather is good. How much longer do we have to live like this?

22nd

That day it only drizzled a little, not even enough to wet the ground. However, several days have passed until today before we got to exercise. But it was over in less than five minutes. He said it was because our order was not good. But how can we have good order?

Film Special

A Serious Warning Issued by an American Film Magazine

— Cairo

Disappointment Caused by Various Film Contests

The Majority are Ignorant and Uninformed Young Women

American film producers are constantly seeking new talent. They are searching all over the world, looking among people of all classes. They have exhausted their efforts and money, launching countless competitions as a way to find true talent. Is this good news for American women? Some say yes, but the American "Motion Picture" magazine has issued a serious warning in its January issue. The reporter read the contents and was also somewhat shocked. Now, I will briefly describe the reasons why the magazine issued the warning and the actual situation of various competitions.

In short, the magic of Hollywood is too great, tempting women across the country, causing them to leave their families, abandon their husbands and children, and leading to various tragedies. Everyone hopes to become a movie star. When this proves impossible, they fall into despair and decline, and even commit suicide. These national competitions are especially the beginning of creating disappointment and tragedy. If you win temporarily, you may still fail in the end; if you fail, then you fail forever and lose all hope, money, and family. Therefore, those who know something about the film industry cannot help but issue a warning to friends all over the world: "It is best not to step into this arena of controversy and embark on a path of destruction; otherwise, you should look ahead and behind, and never forget where the exit is, so that you can make a quick retreat at any time."

According to recent statistics from Hollywood, in the past twelve months, film companies have launched a total of one hundred and ninety-two competitions. Two thousand one hundred winners were hired to Hollywood; and several times as many near-winners paid their own way to Hollywood. More than eleven million American women participated in these many competitions, and the total number worldwide is estimated at twenty-eight million. One competition attracted four million six hundred and forty thousand women. Among them, the most applicants came from medium-sized cities. For example, in Nashville alone, twenty-three thousand four hundred people applied. So it seems that after these many film competitions, America must have millions of disappointed contestants!

The names of the various competitions are truly diverse. There are at least twenty or thirty kinds that can be mentioned. But in the end, they often fail to find a person with the talent they need. They can only invite a few outstandingly beautiful women to Hollywood for a trip, and then send them back home with some money. In this regard, I am afraid that Shanghai people have not forgotten that foreigners also launched a competition in China last year. What the result was, I am afraid there is still no explanation now. However, not many Chinese women participated at the time, so the disappointment was naturally not very significant, because Chinese women are not so star-struck and rarely willing to squander their family wealth and abandon their families to seek opportunities. But American women's thinking is somewhat beyond the norm.

The most unfortunate thing about these competitions is that the people who are attracted are usually young women from small cities and schools who are relatively ignorant and uninformed. They have never had contact with society, so they have never tasted disappointment. They are not prepared for hardship. When they find that their ambitions outweigh their experience, they often cannot withstand the blow and embark on a path of irreversible decline. Just open the newspaper and you can see many "missing person" small advertisements. If you read them carefully, you can discover that wives have disappeared; they hid it from their husbands to join beauty contests, and after being disappointed, they never returned. There are also many suicides after the end of the competition. The police receive countless requests from parents to find their children. After investigating the reasons, some blame it on the various competitions of film companies.

Film Review

Review of "The Bat"

— Moore

Die Fledermaus

The promotional effect of movies is recognized by the world. However, there are some people who deliberately do not recognize the promotional nature of movies, or even all art. On the one hand, they try their best to produce promotional films. So-called promotional films are naturally not limited to positive films promoting certain political views. Even those films that hypnotize those they need to hypnotize and anesthetize those they need to anesthetize, they also work hard to produce. Naturally, the effect is no worse than their positive propaganda. On the one hand, they can avoid the name of propaganda films and the political nature of art. "The Bat" is obviously this type of film.

Many people estimate that this kind of powdery and greasy film in the boudoir is just entertainment for idle people, but in reality, this estimate is not sufficient.

Generally speaking, European filmmakers find it easier to achieve results in making boudoir films than American filmmakers. Because America is too young, and the stories and settings of boudoir films are all from the past. So American filmmakers are not very familiar with them. On the one hand, because the modern economic organization of the United States, and the expression techniques of movies, are also more suitable for expressing modern male and female disputes, and not very suitable for boudoir stories. Take "The Bat" as an example, its sets and shots are generally more ancient and slow than American films, and this ancient and slow doubtlessly more realistic and more suitable for this kind of film.

As for the director, he pays great attention to the evenness of the proportions, especially the supporting characters of the central story. This gives the audience a very rich and comfortable feeling. Of course, this richness and comfort does not mean superfluity and laxity.

Under the decision of the story, the performance of the actors will naturally not be as frivolous and floating as in American films. In short, if we want to see some old art of European films, we can see it in this "The Bat".

Review of "Qiongdong Scenery"

— Ling He

(1)

Here, I can only write a few thoughts.

Winter gives people a terrible feeling. Grayish-white clouds are pressing high above our heads, and the cold air tightly binds our hearts, making us almost lose our ability to breathe. I struggled in the cold wind with a painful feeling. I thought: It snowed a few days ago. Of course, in these few days, perhaps there will be an even more terrible white appearing before our eyes. However, the thought that winter will pass and spring will arrive immediately gives us a very joyful and fresh hope. Thinking of this, it increases my great courage. Okay, let's struggle. Lovely spring will always come to the world.

(2)

"Qiongdong Scenery" is being released in this cold winter, making the air in the theater especially solemn and terrible.

I endured my depressing feelings and watched the official newsreel, and then watched this extremely vulgar and incoherent "Qiongdong Scenery". I deeply regret that the art of film is being destroyed for no reason. If film, this thing, is ruined in China like this, then, friends, think about it! We will inevitably deny the true value of film.

(3)

Film always has its true value in art, especially in this stormy year, when everyone feels artistic hunger, we should uphold the dignity of film in art.

But the true value in art of films like "Qiongdong Scenery" has been completely destroyed, and it has become a propaganda tool. This is extremely contemptible. To be honest, the Chinese audience absolutely does not need this kind of unreasonable propaganda. In this time when the country is dying, we have heard enough of the saying "Settle internal affairs before resisting foreign aggression".

(4)

Furthermore, the fact that film has become a propaganda tool is now obvious. However, propaganda must be based on facts, and at the same time, this kind of propaganda must be accepted by the people. For example, "White House Scenery" is a propaganda tool, and "Royal Palace Spring" is also a propaganda tool. Both give people a feeling of disgust, but their propaganda skills are very high.

Then what about "Qiongdong Scenery"? It's really ridiculous. No matter how you look at it, it is extremely clumsy. It can simply be said that it is not a film at all!

Besides, I don't want to say anything more.

Hollywood at the End of the Year

— Luo Fen

Hollywood feels more lively at the end of the year than anywhere else. The people of Hollywood are very happy to spend a few happy days. These days are filled with joy, and all worries and unhappiness have been forgotten.

Charlie Chaplin usually does not go out. He is rarely seen on the streets of Hollywood. But at the end of the year, he can often be seen in several small dance halls and small cafes. But he is not often seen at large banquets and dance parties.

John Barrymore and Lionel Barrymore, the two brothers, are not fond of slapstick, but they also know how to have fun at the end of the year. The two of them established a huge charity dance party last year. All the ticket money collected that day was donated to the poor relief fund.

Myrna Loy is a very popular figure in Hollywood recently. This year, she prepared a lot of clothes for the children of poor families, and she personally signed her name on each piece of clothing. She is determined to do her best to help these poor children every year.

Mary Pickford is also one who likes to send food to poor children. Every year at the end of the year, she personally makes a lot of cakes and food. On the morning of New Year's Day, she distributes them at her door to the children of poor families on the street. This is her old rule. There is always a lively scene in front of her house on New Year's morning.

The Taste of Kissing

— Dong Lin

Neil Hamilton, a famous young actor in the American film industry, has kissed seventy-six different women in his screen career. Therefore, this also means that he has experienced seventy-six kinds of kissing. According to him: "When filming love scenes, if you don't consider the personality of the actress, the performance is bound to fail. Kissing is also the same. The method of kissing varies with the woman."

Now let me introduce the five major actresses' kissing styles as classified by Hamilton: "Helen Hayes's is the most ideal; Joan Crawford's is like a storm; Norma Shearer's is realistic; Ann Harding's is rational; and Mary Brian's is the purest."

Film Novel

The Song Altar: The Cat and the Fiddle (2)

— Mo Chen

Produced by MGM | Starring Ramon Novarro and Jeannette MacDonald

She glared at him and said, "No!" The driver turned around and asked where to go. Shirley told him to go to the Lafayette Apartments. Victor laughed, "Then we are neighbors! We will have a chance to meet: : : meet often." She ignored him. The car arrived at the entrance of the apartment. Victor hurriedly jumped out of the car to carry her suitcase. Shirley grabbed it from him. The suitcase opened, and silk lingerie spilled all over the ground. She quickly squatted down to pick them up, her eyes shining, almost crying. Victor knelt beside her, helping her pick them up: : : those things made of thin silk, lace, and ribbons, were as beautiful and moving as Shirley herself: : : and there was also a faint scent of lilac, which was the intoxicating scent of Shirley herself.

She hurriedly walked into the apartment. The apartment door slammed shut behind her, but Victor was holding a silk bustier in his hand. He felt as if he had Shirley herself: : : he could no longer be angry and ignore her: : : she seemed to be clinging to his heart. He returned to his room, wanting to compose the conflicts and impulses in his heart into music, Shirley's music, filled with roses and gold. He felt the melody涌 surging in his chest, but suddenly, a burst of clanging jazz music came from the apartment next door, suppressing the song idea in his stomach. He ran to the window in uncontrollable anger and shouted, "Stop banging the boiler! Stop it! Stop it! Did you hear me?" The window opened, and Victor's heart also sank. The person at the window was none other than Shirley. She said, "I heard it." Victor pretended to ask, "Are you playing the piano there? It sounds great. That harmony! That spirit!" Shirley said, "That's just banging the boiler: : : didn't you just say that?" Victor quickly pleaded, "Me? I didn't say anything! I was just sitting here dreaming. When I woke up, I picked up something." He said, raising the bustier in his hand and waving it, but the window slammed shut with a bang.

This made Victor very sad. He knew he shouldn't have been so frivolous. He shouted, "Shirley! Shirley! I know I was wrong." But the window was still closed, and the piano music started again, which made him even more afraid. Everything is over! Would she think of him as a frivolous man and ignore him for the rest of her life? If he could see her again and explain, he would die without regret. So he stepped out of the window and climbed on the sloping roof. He jumped over and grabbed a window frame, hanging in the air. He suddenly felt her hand pulling him, helping him up. After he climbed in through the window, she asked, "Aren't you afraid of falling to your death?" Victor laughed, "The tune you were playing just now seemed to be calling me. Please play it again, okay?" So she sat down and replayed that intoxicating tune, and raised her clear voice, singing "The night was made for love"

Victor ran out of Shirley's apartment with a belly full of songs. He ran straight to the music school, because his professors, Mr. Bertier and Mr. Dodd, had been waiting for him for a long time. When he arrived at the music school and entered the door, a person was coming out from there, and happened to collide with him. Victor, feeling that the person had awakened him from his good dream, couldn't help but scold "Bastard!" Behind him, Professor Bertier shouted madly, "Victor, that's Mr. Dodd. But you must not know him: : :" Victor's dream burst like a rubber ball, because the theater manager who had come all the way from Paris turned around and walked out. But Victor suddenly shouted, "My future is gone. But what does it matter! I'm so happy! Today I saw the most beautiful woman in the world. What does the future matter: : : she smiled at me!" (To be continued)
